	166	Umusozo 	168	Indangasoko 	168Amuga Yakoreshejwe 	170ABANDITSIOliva Bazirete ni umwarimu muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda, Koleji yՕbuzima kuva 2003. Yize Ububyaza no kwigisha ababyaza (RM, BNE/Kaminuza yյ Rwanda), yihugura byisumbuye ibyյmwuga wo kwita ku buzima bwյmubyeyi nյmwana (MS, Nursing/University of Western Cape). Ari mu masomo azamuhesha impamyabumenyi yթkirenga (PhD/Kaminuza yյ Rwanda) mu byյbuzima bwյmubyeyi nյmwana. Yanditse inyandiko zinyuranye zerekeye umwuga wյbuforomo nյbubyaza nյburyo bwo kwita ku mubyeyi uri kunda. Anne Marie Kagwesage ni umwarimu muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda, Koleji yՉndimi nՕbumenyi Nyamuntu kuva 1999. Yize Iyigandimi nՕbuvanganzo byՕrurimi rwՉcyongereza (BA/Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda), yiga ibijyanye no kwigisha indimi (MPhil/University of Western Cape), abona nթmpamyabumenyi yթkirenga mu byյburezi (PhD/Linkping University). Yanditse inyandiko zinyuranye zerekeye uburyo bwo gukoresha icyongereza mu kwigisha amasomo ya kaminuza.Evode Mukama ni umwarimu nյmushakashatsi wթnararibonye mu burezi bushingiye cyanecyane ku ikoranabuhanga. Afite impamyabumenyi yթkirenga mu burezi yavanye muri Kaminuza ya Linkping yo mu gihugu cya Suwedi mu 2009. Ubushakashatsi bwe bwashyizwe ahagaragara mu bitangazamakuru byյbumenyi bikomeye byo hirya no hino ku isi. Yayoboye inzego zյburezi bushingiye ku ikoranabuhanga nթyakure mu Kigo kՉgihugu Gishinzwe Guteza Imbere Uburezi no muri Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda. Yabaye umuyobozi wungirije wՕrwego rwՕbushakashatsi muri iyo kaminuza. Ubu ni umwarimu nյmushakashatsi muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda РKoleji yՕburezi.Charline Mulindahabi ni umwarimu muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda, Koleji yթndimi nյbumenyi nyamuntu kuva mu 1999. Yize ibyՉmicungire yթbya rubanda mu kiciro cya mbere (BA/ Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda) nթcya kabiri cya kaminuza (MPA/University of Western Cape), abona nթmpamyabumenyi yթkirenga mu byՁmahoro nՉterambere (PhD/University of Gothenburg). Ubushakashatsi akora bwibanda ku buyobozi nթmiyoborere ndetse no ku gukemura amakimbirane.Jean Baptiste Ndikubwimana yigisha muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda kuva 2008. Yahize ikiciro cya mbere mu bya Politiki (BA/Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda). Kuva 2009 yakomeje amasomo mu burenganzira bwa muntu no gukemura amakimbirane mu mahoro (Universit du Burundi). Kuva muri 2012 yize ibyթterembere (MA/Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda). Ubu ariga ibyյburenganzira bwa muntu (PhD/University of Nairobi).Tlesphore Ngarambe ni umwarimu muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda. Yize Iyigandimi nՕbuvanganzo byՕrurimi rwՉcyongereza (BA/Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda). Yakomereje ikiciro cya gatatu cya kaminuza (MA) muri University of Witwatersrand mu ihinduranyandiko. Afite impamyabumenyi yթkirenga (PhD) mu ihinduranyandiko nյbusemuzi yahawe na Kaminuza yյ Rwanda. Ubushakashatsi bwe bwibanda ku ihinduranyandiko nյbusemuzi, politiki rusange, umuco, itumanaho nթkoranabuhanga.Epimaque Niyibizi ni umwarimu muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda, Koleji yՕburezi kuva 2001. Yize iyigandimi nյbuvanganzo byյrurimi rwՉcyongereza (BA/Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda), yiga ibyթmyigishirize yթndimi (MA/University of South Africa), abona nթmpamyabumenyi yթkirenga mu myigishirize yթndimi (PhD/University of Witwatersrand). Yakoze ubushakashatsi anasohora inyandiko zinyuranye ku myigishirize yթndimi kavukire nթndimi mvamahanga, na politiki yթndimi.Jean Chrysostome Nkejabahizi ni umwarimu muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda kuva mu 1994. Yigisha kandi agakora ubushakashatsi ku ndimi, imico nյbuvanganzo nyafurika, yibanda ku Rwanda. Mu byթngenzi yatangaje harimo Ubusizi nyarwanda (Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda, 2009), Amateka yյbuvanganzo nyarwanda kuva ku kinyejana cya XVII kugeza magingo aya (Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda, 2011) afatanyije na Gamariel Mbonimana, Ubuvanganzo nyarwanda. Inkuru ndende nթkinamico (Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda, 2013), Rwandan Short Stories in English, French and Kinyarwanda (Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda, 2013), Les wellrismes du Rwanda. Approche ethnolinguistique (Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda, 2013).Laurent Nkusi ni umwarimu nյmushakashatsi wթnararibonye. Yigishije muri Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda kuva 1976 kugeza 2000, aba umuyobozi mu mashami yayo, ndetse aba umuyobozi wՕrwego rwՕbushakashatsi. Ubu arakigisha nkՕmwarimu udahoraho muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda no mu zindi, akigisha iyigandimi, isesenguranyandiko, iyigamuga nթyigarutonde, ihakana nթpfobya rya jenoside. Afite impamyabushobozi ya Doctorat dՅtat s Lettres et Sciences Humaines, yabaye Minisitiri muri Leta yյ Rwanda imyaka umunani. Ubu ni Senateri РInteko Ishinga Amategeko, aho ahagarariye Abarimu nՁbashakashatsi ba Kaminuza zigenga.Evariste Ntakirutimana yigisha muri Kaminuza yՕ Rwanda, Koleji yՉndimi nՕbumenyamuntu. Ikiciro cya mbere nթcya kabiri yabyize mu Gashami kՉndimi nՕbuvanganzo Nyafurika (1983б988) muri Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda. Mu kiciro cya gatatu (1998в001) yize Iyigandimi nyamubano muri Kaminuza ya Laval muri Kanada. Mu nyandiko ze zinyuranye, Ntakirutimana yibanze ku isano iri hagati yթndimi nթmiryango yաbazivuga. Kimwe mu bimushishikaza cyane ni ugusesengura imbwirwaruhame.Sylvestre Nzahabwanayo ni umwarimu muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda, Ishuri ryՕburezi. Afite impamyabumenyi yթkirenga mu burezi (PhD/University of the Witwatersrand). Ubushakashatsi bwe bwibanda ku burere mboneragihugu bwյrubyiruko kugira ngo rushobore kuba abaturage banogeye igihugu cyanecyane mu bihugu byaranzwemo jenoside nաndi makimbirane.Pierre Claver Rutayisire ni umwarimu muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda, Ishami ryՉbarurishamibare kuva muri 2000. Yize ibarurishamibare ryibanda ku mihindukire yթmibare yաbaturage nթngaruka zayo (MSc Demography/Universit Catholique de Louvain), abona nթmpamyabumenyi yթkirenga (PhD/Utrecht University) mu Buholandi. Yanditse inyandiko zinyuranye zerekeye uburyo bukoreshwa mu kwegeranya no gusesengura imibare yաbavuka, abapfuye, abinjira nաbasohoka mu gihugu.Joseph Appolinary Rusanganwa ni umwarimu mu ishami ryթndimi zաmahanga muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda. Mu kiciro cya mbere cya kaminuza (BEd Hons/University of Dar es Salaam) yize indimi zաmahanga (Igifaransa, Icyongereza, Igiswahili) nթyigandimi (MA Linguistics/University of London). Ikiciro cya kabiri yize iyigandimi mu buryo burambuye. Icya gatatu (PhD/Linkping University) yize kwigisha indimi akoresheje ikoranabuhanga. Ubushakashatsi bwe bushingiye mu kwigisha hakoreshejwe iyakure.Pierre Canisius Ruterana ni Umwarimu muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda, Koleji yՉndimi nՕbumenyi Nyamuntu kuva 1998. Yize iyigandimi nյbuvanganzo byյrurimi rwՉcyongereza (BA/Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda), yiga gusemura (MA/University of Warwick), abona nթmpamyabumenyi yթkirenga mu byյburezi (PhD/Linkping University). Yanditse inyandiko zinyuranye zerekeye uburyo bwo kubungabunga no kumenya indimi neza, guteza imbere no kugira umuco wo gusoma.Marie Chantal Uwimana ni umwarimu muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda, Koleji yՕbuzima nՕbuvuzi kuva 2006. Yize Ubuforomo nյbubyaza mu Ishuri Rikuru ryՕbuzima mu Rwanda, abona ikiciro cya gatatu buyobozi nթmicungire yաbaforomo (MS Nursing Management/ University of KwaZulu Natal). Yanditse inyandiko zijyanye no kunoza umwuga wյbuforomo nյbubyaza. Akora ubushakashatsi ku bijyanye no kugabanya imfu zաbana nաbabyeyi mu rwego rwաmasomo ajyanye nթmpamyabumenyi yթkirenga (PhD/University of the Witwatersrand).Dieudonne Uwizeye ni umwarimu muri Kaminuza yյ Rwanda kuva muri 2007. Yize ikiciro cya mbere cya kaminuza, ishami ryՕburezi (BEd/Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda). Yakomereje mu masomo yթterambere (MA, Development Studies/Kabaale University), yiga kwigisha ururimi rwՉcyongereza (MA, English TESOL/California Baptist University), arangiza yiga isesengura ryթmibereho nթmibanire yաbantu (PhD, Demography and Population Studies/ University of Dar es Salaam). Yanditse inyandiko zisesengura ukubaka iterambere rishingiye ku muturage.UMUTWE 1IRIBURIRO:  IMIZI YՕBUSHAKASHATSI Evode Mukama na Laurent Nkusi Kwibaza no kwisubizaKuva kera na kare, abantu ntibahwemye kwitegereza, kwibaza no gusesengura ibidukikije kugira ngo barusheho kubisobanukirwa, kubigenzura no kubigenga iyo bishoboka. Abanyarwanda baravugaga bati ҕtazi akaraye i Fumbwe araza ifuӮ Ibi byerekana ko bari bazi kwitegereza ibimenyetso byթbihe, bakamenya ko i Fumbwe aho Рbitewe nաho babaga baherereye Рhari icyoko kթmvura. Ibyo rero byabahaga guteganyiriza ibihe bibi byթmvura, bagakora hakiri kare ibyo badashobora gukora mu gihe iri kugwa. Uko amajyambere yagiye aza, ubumenyi nkյbu bwa kimenyabose bwagiye bwunganirwa nյbumenyi bwimbitse kandi bwizwe gihanga. Byongeye, ikoranabuhanga ryihutishije kumva no kugenzura ibidukikije. Nkյbu iteganyagihe rikoresheje ikoranabuhanga rishobora kutubwira ku buryo bwizewe kandi bwihuse igihe imvura izagwira haba uyu munsi, mu cyumweru gitaha, mu mezi ndetse no mu myaka iri imbere. Kwibaza no kwisubiza si umwihariko wաbanyarwanda. Ubushakashatsi iyo buva kubakagera ni cyo buba bugamije. Ariko rero abantu ntabwo bibaza kimwe, nta nյbwo basubiza kimwe ibibazo bibaza cyangwa babajijwe. Ibyo ari byo byose, uwibaza nյbaza hari ukuri baba bagamije kumenya. Kugira ngo ibyo byose bigerweho byasabye abantu kwitegereza, kugerageza, gutekereza no gukora ubushakashatsi nyirizina. Iri riburiro rigiye kubiva imuzi maze risozwe ritubwira umwihariko wթki gitabo nթbigikubiyemo. Kwitegereza no kugerageza: niba umunyarwanda yaritegereje inshuro nyinshi, agasanga koko igicu kijimye kandi kibuditse giturutse i Fumbwe ari cyo gitanga imvura, agereranyije nթbindi bicu byabudikiye mu bindi byerekezo, ni bwo yashoboye gufata umwanzuro ko i Fumbwe ari icyoko kթmvura. Mbere yo gufata umwanzuro, ashobora kuba yaribazaga ati ҅se koko iyo ikubiye i Fumbwe iragwa?ӠIki ni ikibazo cyյbushakashatsi. Kwitegereza no kugerageza inshuro nyinshi biri mu byatumye ashobora gufata umwanzuro ko igitekerezo ke ari ukuri: ҉yo yakubiye i Fumbwe iragwaӮ Iki gitekerezo ni inkeneragihamya (hypothesis). Kuri iyi nkeneragihamya rero umunyarwanda yasanze ari ukuri: yitegereje inshuro nyinshi asanga koko igicu kijimye kandi kibuditse giturutse i Fumbwe ari cyo gitanga imvura. Umunyarwanda yakoze ibi akoresheje ubumenyi kimenyabose abandi babwita ubumenyi kimeza. Ntabwo yabikoze kuri gahunda izwi, cyangwa se ngo abe yafashe umugambi wo gusubiza cya kibazo cyյbushakashatsi, emwe ndetse ntiyari agamije kwemeza cyangwa guhakana ku buryo bweruye inkeneragihamya. Icyo twashima kwitegereza no kugerageza ni uko byubakiye ku kibazo cyյbushakashatsi cyangwa ku nkeneragihamya, ubikora yaba abigambiriye cyangwa atabigambiriye (Mouly, 1978).Imitekerereze: uburyo bwa kabiri abantu bagerageza kumva no gusobanukirwa ibidukikije ni ugutekereza. Ubu buryo bwթmitekerereze buri ugutatu (Mouly, 1978):  Imitekerereze nganamuzi (deductive reasoning): iyi mitekerereze yahimbwe nյmugereki Aristote igaragazwa nյruhererekane rwթngingo eshatu zitangirira ku ikomatanya rusange ukagana ku kintu-muzi (ikintu kimwe kihariye), noneho ugafata umwanzuro. Dore urugero rukunze kwifashishwa mu gusobanura imitekerereze nganamuzi:Imibumbe yose izenguruka izuba;Isi ni umubumbe;Ni ukuvuga ko isi izenguruka izuba. Iyi mitekerereze iragaragaza ko umwanzuro Ҏi ukuvuga ko isi izenguruka izubaӠukomoka ku isesengura ryթngingo ebyiri za mbere kandi ikazuzuza. Aristote rero ari ku isonga mu babimburiye abandi mu gushaka kumva no gusesengura ibidukikije ku buryo bukurikije gahunda. Ariko rero byaje kugaragara ko gahunda yթnyabutatu yթmitekerereze nganamuzi idatanga umwanzuro wյkuri buri gihe.  Imitekerereze mvamuzi (inductive reasoning): mu myaka ya 1600 ni bwo umuhanga muri filozofiya wյmwongereza, Francis Bacon, ahereye ku ntege nke zթmitekerereze nganamuzi, yaje kwerekana ubundi buryo bushya bwթmitekerereze ishingiye ku kwiga ibintu-muzi byinshi (ibintu byinshi byihariye), noneho akaba ari byo bikugeza ku nkeneragihamya, ndetse byanashoboka bikakugeza ku ikomatanya rusange. Umwihariko wa Francis Bacon ni uko yatumye noneho abahanga barushaho kumva ibidukikije bahereye ku gukusanya no gusesengura amakuru afatika yթbiriho. Aho kugira ngo uruhererekane rwթngingo remezo zifatwe nkթhame ryթmyanzuro, ahubwo izo ngingo zihinduka inkereragihamya ishobora kwemezwa cyangwa guhakanywa bitewe nyine nաmakuru yakusanyijwe kandi yasesenguwe ku bintu-muzi byinshi. Uburyo mvamuzi-nganamuzi (Inductive-deductive approach): birumvikana ko ubu buryo bushingiye ku rujya nյruza rwթmitekerereze ya Bacon nթya Aristote mu bushashakashatsi. Muri iki gihe, abashakashatsi bashobora kwitegereza ibidukikije, bagakora inkeneragihamya cyangwa se ibibazo byյbushakashatsi (Uburyo mvamuzi). Iyi nkeneragihamya nթbi bibazo bashobora kubifataho imyanzuro kugira ngo barebe isano bifitanye nյbumenyi rusange busanzwe buzwi (uburyo nganamuzi). Iyo bibaye ngombwa, bashobora kongera gukusanya andi makuru, bakayasesungura kugeza igihe babonye igisubizo kimbitse ku nkeneragihamya bihaye cyangwa ku bibazo byյbushakashatsi bibazaga. Uru rujya nյruza hagati yo gukusanya amakuru, kuyasesengura, imyanzuro, inkeneragihamya nթbibazo byյbushakashatsi ni byo biranga uburyo mvamuzi-nganamuzi mu bushakashatsi. Ubu buryo burakoreshwa cyane mu bushakashatsi bwյbumenyi nyamuntu nթmibanire yաbantu.Ubushakashatsi: umuntu yavuga ko ubushakashatsi ari uruhurirane rwo kwitegereza, kugerageza no gutekereza bikozwe ku buryo buri kuri gahunda, bugenzuwe kandi bwubakiye ku makuru afatika ku bibazo nթnkeneragihamya ku bidukikije. Ni ukuvuga ko mu gusesengura no gusobanukira ibidukikije, ubushakashatsi bushingiye ku buryo mvamuzi-nganamuzi. Ubushakashatsi rero burategurwa, bugakorwa kuri gahunda kandi bukagira intego. Ubushakashatsi bushingiye ku gutara no gusesengura amakuru ku bintu byigwa. Aha, umuntu yavuga ko ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi bishobora kugeragezwa kugira ngo bigire ubwizerwe (reliability), ububonere (validity) nյbwemerwe. Byongeye, ubumenyi bwagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi bushobora gukosorwa cyangwa kongerwa. Ntabwo ubumenyi butura nkյmusozi, iyo ubushakashatsi busanze harabaye ikosa mu myumvire yթbyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi, bushobora gukosorwa cyangwa guhindurwa rwose (Mouly, 1978). Icyo kiri mu gituma ubushakashatsi buryohera ababukora kandi umushakashatsi agahorana amatsiko yթgishya agiye kuzana ku bumenyi busanzwe buzwi. Ubushakashatsi no gushakisha ukuriEse ukuri ni iki mu bushakashatsi? Kuba hehe se? Bagushaka bate? Kwibaza bene ibyo bibazo no gushaka kumenya inkomoko yյbumenyi birajyana. Kubisubiza rero byatumye havuka inkingi zo kumva no gusobanura ukuri mu bushakashatsi. Abanyakuri mpame (positivists): mu ntangiro zթkinyejana cya 19, ni bwo umuhanga muri filosofiya wյmufaransa Auguste Comte yagaragaje ku buryo butaziguye ko ubumenyi iyo buva bukagera bushingiye ku bidukikije, ku birango byabyo nաmasano ari hagi yabyo. Ku banyakuri mpame rero, umuntu amenya ko ibiriho biriho yifashishije kwitegereza nթgerageza-bushakashatsi (experiment) akoresheje ibyumviro byյmubiri. Ni ukuvuga ko ibidukikije nաmasano ari hagati yabyo ari ukuri kuriho, gufatika kandi gufite amategeko akugenga. Kugira ngo umuntu yige uko kuri, agomba kwitarura ibidukikije maze agakoresha uburyo bwa gihanga mu gusesengura amasano nաmategeko ari hagati yabyo. Kuri Auguste Comte, kwiga ukuri kuri ubu buryo biberanye nթngeri zյbumenyi mu byթnyenyeri, ubugenge, ubutabire nյbumenyi bwթbinyabuzima. Cyakora avuga ko ubumenyi mu mibanire yաbantu butaragera kuri urwo rwego. Kugira ngo rero umuntu akore ubushakashatsi mu bumenyi bwթmibanire yաbantu atavanze ibitekerezo bye mu kuri yigaho, abanyakuri mpame bavuga ko ari ngombwa gukoresha uburyo nyamubaro kimwe nթsesenguramakuru rishingiye ku ibarurishamibare (Benton & Craib, 2001). Ababandasobanura (interpretativists): iyi mitekerereze igaragaza ko ukuri gushobora guhinduka yaje ishimangira ko ubushakashatsi mu bumenyi bwթmibanire yաbantu budakwiye gushingira gusa ku gukoresha uburyo nyamubaro nkյko abanyakuri mpame babikora. Ababandasobanura bemeza ko ukuri gushobora kubakwa nաbantu bashyize hamwe mu biganiro, mu gutekereza, mu kungurana inama, kandi bakoresheje ibintu bibakikije (Myers, 2008). Ntibemera rero ko ukuri ari ntayegayezwa cyangwa ko kuri ahantu runaka, ko ntaho guhuriye nթmitekerereze ya muntu. Ababandasobanura bumva ko umushakashatsi afitanye isano nաbantu cyangwa ibintu yigaho kandi ko adashobora kubyitarura burundu. Ukuri rero gushobora guhinduka bitewe nյkuntu abantu babayeho, ibidukikije babana na byo nյburyo babanye na byo. Mu yandi magambo, abantu batekereza uko batekereza kandi bitwara uko bitwara bitewe nաho bari nյburyo babayeho mu gihe runaka. Abantu bari mu buzima runaka baba bafite igisobanuro baha imiberereho yabo ku buryo butandukanye nյko undi muntu utari muri ubwo buzima abyumva. Ukuri kurenga ibyo umuntu ashobora kubonesha amaso. Ababandasobanura bavuga ko kugira ngo ukuri ku mibereho nթmibanire yաbantu kumenyekane, umushakashatsi agomba guha urubuga abagufite bakakugaragaza. Imbonerahamwe 1 	Igereranya ryյbunyakuri mpame nթbandasobanuraIngingoUbunyakuri mpameIbandasobanuraImiterere yյkuriKurazwi, kurafatika, ni kumweKubakwa nաbantu, ni kwinshiIntego yյbushakashatsiGusobanura, guteganya ibizabaGusobanukirwa, kutibanda cyane ku guteganyaIgishishikaje umushakashatsiIkomatanya rusange, impuzandengo; ubuhagararizi (ibirango bihagarariye itsinda ryose)Ikintu muzi, umwihariko nթkinyuranyoUbumenyi bwagaragajweAmategeko Ntibuhinduka (ntibujyana nթgihe, ahantu cyangwa indangagaciro)Bujyana nթbisobanuro. Burahinduka (buterwa nթgihe, ahantu nթndangagaciro)Isano iri hagati yթkigwa/uwigwa nյmushakashatsiBiratandukanye rwoseBarashyikirana, barakorana, bose babirimoAmakuru akeneweNi abantu bangahe bakora ikintu runaka cyangwa bafite ikibazo runakaBamwe muri aba bantu batekereza iki kandi barakora iki, ni ikihe kibazo bahura na cyo, ese icyo kibazo bagikemura bateIyi nkingi yթbandasobanura (interpretativism) ni yo ishamikiyeho ubushakashatsi nyamimerere. Itandukaniro ryյbunyakuri mpame (positivism) nթbandasobanura (interpretativism) rigaragara neza mu imbonerahamwe (Pizam & Mansfeld, 2009).Izi nkingi ebyiri zidufasha kumva no gusobanura ukuri mu bushakashatsi. Byongeye ziratwumvisha ko ibidukikije tubyiga kubera ko dukeneye kunguka ubumenyi. Ariko rero ubwo bumenyi na bwo bwigwa nյmuntu uteye uko ateye kandi akurikije iyoboramikorere/inozaninzira (methodology) isobanutse. Tugiye kwifashisha Burrell na Morgan (1979) kugira ngo dusobanure ingingo zթngenzi zikomoka ku nkingi ebyiri zյbushakashatsi twavuze hejuru.Iyigabaho (ontology = science of being): mu bumenyi bwթmibanire yաbantu, usanga abashakashatsi basizanira kumva kamere yթmibanire yաbantu. Ese hirya yթbigaragara, ni iki gituma ukuri kwթbintu bibera mu bantu kuba uko kuri? Umuhanga muri filozofiya wյmunyarwanda, Alegisi Kagame, avuga ko kamere yթkigize umuntu Рikintu Рahantu Рukuntu ari igicumbi ҮtuӠku Banyarwanda ndetse no ku bandi bantu bՁbanyafurika (Kagame, 1976). Hari abanenze iyi mitekerereze bavuga ko Kagame yagerageje gusanisha zimwe mu ngingo zթmitekerereze ya Aristote mu iyigabaho ryՁbanyafurika (Thomas, 1977). Nyamara, Maniragaba Baributsa (1988) na Martinon (2013) bagaragaza ko ibyo atari byo habe na mba kuko ҫubaӠno ҫubahoӠbivugwa muri filozofiya yՁbagereki bidahuje igicumbi na ҮtuӮ Kuri ibyo byiciro bine bya kamere rero, Maniragaba Baributsa (1988) yongeraho ubuntu, naho Martinon (2013) akagerekaho ubumuntu. Icyo aba bahanga bose bahurizaho ni ugushaka ukuri gutuma umuntu Рikintu Рahantu Рukuntu Рubuntu Рubumuntu biba ibyo biri koko. Iyi mitekerereze igaragaza ko ukuri kurenga ibigaragara, bityo gushobora kuba mu bimenyetso biguhagarariye cyangwa se bihagarariye aho kuri. Abashakisha ukuri ku bintu bibera mu bantu baribaza bati: ҅se uko kuri kuba hanze yաbantu noneho kukabagiraho ingaruka mu mitekerereze yabo cyangwa se gukomoka ku mitekerereze yabo?ӠMu yandi magambo ni ukwibaza niba ukuri baguhabwa biturutse hanze cyangwa niba baguhanga mu bitekerezo. Ingingo ya kabiri ikomoka ku nkingi yյbunyakuri mpame nթbandasobanura ni iyigabumenyi (epistemology): abahanga nաbashakashatsi mu bumenyi bwթmibanire yաbantu bashishikazwa no kumva kamere yյbumenyi, ubwoko bwabwo, uko bwigwa nյko bushobora guhererekanywa. Ibi rero bituma ababushakashaka bakwibaza niba ubumenyi ari ikintu gifatika kandi kizwi rwose ndetse gishobora guhererekanywa nkթkintu nyine (ingero: igitabo, telefoni), cyangwa se niba ubumenyi ari ikintu kidafatika, gishobora guhinduka, cyumvishwa ukwemera ku buryo umuntu yakitoza agashyirwa akimenye ku giti ke (Burrell & Morgan, 1979). Mu yandi magambo, ikibazo ni ukwibaza, ku ruhande rumwe, niba ubumenyi bwigwa kandi niba bwigishwa; ku rundi ruhande, ni ukwibaza niba ubumenyi ari ikintu umuntu ahura na cyo mu buzima akakimenyereza we ubwe. Abashakashatsi bumva ko ubumenyi ari ikintu kizwi kandi gifatika, abo babwiga bakoresheje uburyo nyamubaro (quantitative methods) imeze kimwe nթyթngeri zյbumenyi mu byթnyenyeri, ubugenge, ubutabire nյbumenyi bwթbinyabuzima. Aba twabashyira mu rwego rwաbanyakuri mpame. Naho ababona ko ubumenyi ari gatozi, ko bushobora guhinduka bitewe nաhantu, nթbintu ubufite abamo, abo bakoresha uburyo nyamimerere (qualitative methods). Ni ababandasobanura.Ingingo ya gatatu ishingiye kuri za nkingi ebyiri zյbushakashatsi twavuze haruguru ni kamere muntu cyanecyane ariko ni isano riri hagati yթkiremwamuntu nթbidukikije (Burrell & Morgan, 1979). Mu bumenyi bwթmibanire yաbantu, ukora ubushakashatsi ni umuntu, uwigwa na we ni umuntu. Uyu muntu rero tuvuga ashobora kubaho mu buryo bubiri: 1) muntu ujya iyo byerekeza; mbese muntu ubana nթbidukikije nkթgikoresho cyabyo. Bene uyu muntu akoreshwa nթbidukikije. Ni wawundi uhora ugira ati: Ҏone se ko ari ko Imana yabishatse, nagira nte? Ni uko bimeze nyine nta kundi.ӠAbaho uko isi ishaka. 2) Muntu ufata iya mbere mu guha ibidukikije ikerekezo. Bene uyu muntu ahora ashakisha uburyo bushya yakoramo. Ni umuhanzi wթbidukikije; ni we ubigenga kandi akabigenzura. Afite ubushake mu gukora ibimubereye. Aba bantu bombi ni abahezanguni, abashakashatsi mu mibanire yաbantu baherereye ahagana hagati yթmyumvire yabo.Ingingo ya kane ikomoka ku nkingi yյbunyakuri mpame nթbandasobanura mu bushakashatsi ni iyoboramikorere/inozanzira (methodology). Nkյko twabigaragaje hejuru, buri ngingo muri izo eshatu twabanje gusobanura (iyigabaho, iyigabumenyi na kamere muntu) yifitemo ibice bibiri bibusanye kandi buri gice kikagira uburyo ubushakashatsi bukwiye gukorwamo. Abashakashatsi babona ko ukuri ku bintu bibera mu mibanire yաbantu ari ukuri kuri ahantu runaka, ko kuzwi kandi ko gufatika ni abanyakuri mpame. Uzasanga abanyakuri mpame bakoresha ubushakashatsi nyamubaro (quantitative research) mu kwiga ukuri ku bintu birebana nթmibanire yաbantu bagendeye ku masano ari hagati yabyo agaragazwa nթbarurishamibare. Aba bagerageza rwose kwitarura isoko yաmakuru kugira ngo batavaho bayagiraho ingaruka. Naho abashakashatsi babona ko ukuri ku bintu bibera mu mibanire yաbantu ari ukuri kubakwa kandi gushobora guhinduka bitewe nթmibereho nyakuri yաbantu, uzasanga bakoresha ubushakashatsi nyamimerere (qualitative research). Ubu bushakashatsi bushingira kandi bugasesengura ukuri kuba mu makuru agendanye nթmibereho yաbantu nաho baba no mu bitekerezo ndetse nթmyumvire yabo. Ubumenyi busanzwe buzwi nյkora ubushakashatsi nyamimerere bushobora kumufasha kubaza ku buryo bwimbitse andi makuru abwerekeyeho. Uyu mushakashatsi ashobora kandi gukorana no kubana nաbatangamakuru igihe kirekire kugira ngo arusheho kumenya uburyo babayeho nյko batekereza, ibyo byose bikaba ari amakuru yյbushakashatsi. Muri iki gihe, hari abashakashatsi bafata impu zombi, maze bagakoresha icyarimwe ubushakashatsi nyamubaro nյbushakashatsi nyamimerere. Gukoresha ubu buryo bwombi mu bushakashatsi bumwe ni byo byitwa uburyo rukomatanyo (mixed methods). Ibi rero bifite akamaro kuko bituma haba ubwuzuzanye mu bigaragazwa nյbushakashatsi nyamubaro na nyamimerere. Ubwo bushakashatsi bushobora kandi gutuma ikigwa bagicengera ku buryo bwimbitse. Byongeye bushobora gutuma abanyakuri mpame bakorana kandi buzuzanya nաbabandasobanura. Cyakora birumvikana ko bisaba ubushobozi buhagije kugira ngo ubwo bushakashatsi bukorwe kandi busuzumwe. Rimwe na rimwe nյbwo abashakashatsi bakoresha uburyo butandukanye bashobora gukorana, hari ubwo bitaborohera cyanecyane iyo uburyo bundi bwakoreshejwe batabuzi neza.Umwihariko wթki gitaboNtibyoroshye gushyira imbago hagati yյbumenyi nyamuntu (humanities) nյbumenyi bwթmibanire yաbantu (social sciences). Impaka ziracyagibwa. Ubumenyi nyamuntu bwatangiye kwigwa kera nաbahanga bՁbagereki bo hambere. Abiga ubu bumenyi usanga bakunda kwibanda ku gusesengura ibintu bituma umuntu aba umuntu: amategeko, amateka, indimi zo hambere nթzo dukoresha mu buzima bwa buri munsi, filozofiya, iyobokamana, ubugeni nթbindi. Usanga kandi iryo sesengura bariha isura yo gucengera imitekerereze yegamiye kuri filozofiya. Naho ubumenyi bwթmibanire yաbantu bwahawe umurongo cyanecyane na Karl Marx, Emile Durkheim na Max Weber. Ubu bumenyi bwahawe umurindi nթmpinduramatwa yabaye mu gihugu cyՕbufaransa nթyo mu byթnganda yabaye mu bihugu byo mu burengerazuba bwթsi. Ubumenyi bwթmibanire yաbantu usanga bwibanda byյmwihariko ku nyigo zirebana nթmiterere ya sosiyete: ubumenyi gakondo, imiyoborerere, uburezi, ubukungu, ubumenyi mu mitekerereze ya muntu, ubuvanganzo, ubumenyi bwa politiki, amategeko, amateka nթbindi. Iri gerereranya riratwereka ko ubumenyi nyamuntu nյbumenyi bwթmibanire yաbantu bifitanye isano kandi bijya gusa.Muri iki gitabo twahisemo gufata uruhande rwa Terence, aho agira ati Ҏdi umuntu, ikireba umuntu cyose nticyanyibetaӠ(Homo sum, humani nihil a me alienum puto), ari byo byahinduwe mu cyongereza ngo ҉ am human, and I think nothing human is alien to meӠ(Forehand, 1985; Davis, 2014). Ubwo rero ibireba ubumenyi nyamuntu nյbumenyi bwթmibanire yաbantu, nta kibi umushakashatsi abishyize hamwe. Ubumenyi bufite amahame bugenderaho: kwanga amarangamutima (objectivity), kuva imuzi icyo wiga (exhaustiveness), kutivuguruza (coherance) no kutarondogora (simplicity). Ni icyo tugamije. Izo mpamvu zose ni zo zatumye dukomatanya ubushakashatsi bwյbumenyi nyamuntu nթmibanire yաbantu muri iki gitabo.Undi mwihariko wթki gitabo ushingiye ku rurimi twakoresheje mu kucyandika. Nյbwo ubushakashatsi bwatangiye gukorwa mu Rwanda ku buryo butaziguye kuva mu myaka irenga ijana ishize, biragaragara ko butigeze bwinjira mu muco wաbanyarwanda ngo buhererekanywe mu rurimi kavukire rwabo bumva neza. Ikinyarwanda kirakenewe kugira ngo umuco wյbushakashatsi uhabwe intebe mu gihugu no kugira ngo hashimangirwe ubufatanye hagati yաbashakashatsi, abarimu, abanyeshuri, abanyapolitiki nաbandi bafata ibyemezo ndetse nաbaturage barebwa nթbyavuye muri ubwo bushakashatsi. Ngiyo impamvu yatumye iki gitabo cyandikwa mu Kinyarwanda. Kwandika iki gitabo mu Kinyarwanda bizatuma ibigikubiyemo bishobora kwifashishwa mu gukora, gusesengura, kugenzura no gusuzuma umurimo wյbushakashatsi, ari ku bashakashatsi ubwabo, ku banyeshuri nաbarimu, ku bafata ibyemezo, ku baturage, ku baterankunga, ku nzego za Leta ndetse no ku bandi bakenera ubushakashatsi cyangwa ibyabuvuyemo.Iki gitabo ntabwo kigamije kwigisha ururimi rwՉkinyarwanda. Ikigamijwe kթngenzi ni uguha umusomyi wթki gitabo ibikoresho bya ngombwa kugira ngo ashobore gukora ubushakashatsi bufite ireme. Iki gitabo kiraha umusomyi ubushobozi bwo gutegura umushinga wյbushakashatsi, kuwushyira mu bikorwa, gusesengura ibice byabwo byթngenzi no kugaragaza uko bikorwa. Byongeye, kirasobanura imikoreshereze yաmahame ngengamyitwarire mu bushakashatsi, kikanatanga umurongo ngenderwaho ku gukora isesengura ryթbyanditswe mbere nաbandi bashakashatsi. Iki gitabo kirerekana uburyo bwթngenzi bwo gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru nյko bakusanya ndetse bakanasesengura amakuru yյbushakashatsi, yaba amakuru akomoka ku bushakashatsi nyamimerere cyangwa se nyamubaro. Umusomyi azasobanurirwa kandi uko bakora nյko bandika ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi, isobanura bwite nյmwanzuro. Uretse gukoresha ururimi rwՉkinyarwanda, iki gitabo gifite nյmwihariko wo gukoresha amuga mashya ajyanye nյbushakashatsi. Ururimi ruhora rwiyubaka. Ruhora rwunguka amagambo mashya, amwe nաmwe akagororwa cyangwa agasimbuzwa andi aboneye kurushaho bitewe nթbihe nթmico inyuranye abarukoresha bagezemo. Nkյbumenyi mu ikoranabuhanga bwatumye haduka amuga mashya: mudasobwa, iyakure, murandasi, ubutumwa bugufi, imbuga nkoranyambaga nաyandi. Ayo muga arushaho kugira ireme, ububonere nյbwizerwe iyo habonetse intiti nթnzobere mu ngeri zյbumenyi runaka zikayigaho, zikayashungura, zikayasobanura maze ayemejwe akungura ururimi rusanzwe rukoreshwa. Biratangaje kandi birababaje iyo ubushakashatsi bwavumburiwe mu mahanga abavuga ururimi rwՉkinyarwanda badashobora kubugeraho ngo kuko nta muga yյbuhanga abaho kugira ngo buhererekanywe muri urwo rurimi bumva neza. Aha ni ukwibeshya cyane, ni no kwipfobya gukabije. Ayo muga ntiyabaho ntawayacuze. Urugero ni iki gitabo. Hari abibwiraga ko kwandika igitabo nkթki mu Kinyarwanda bidashoboka. Niba byarashobotse rero nթbindi birashoboka. Ibitabo byinshi byanditswe mu cyongereza ntihaca kabiri bidahinduwe mu gifaransa, ikirusiya, ikesipanyoro, ikidage, igishinywa nթzindi ndimi zikoreshwa mu bihugu byakataje imbere mu majyambere. Ibyo ni imbonekarimwe mu bihugu bikiri mu nzira yաmajyambere harimo nյ Rwanda. Kudakoresha ururimi rwacu twumva neza mu guhererekanya ubumenyi bwavumbuwe hirya no hino bishobora kuba biri ku isonga mu gukumira iterambere rirambye, ryihuta kandi rigera kuri benshi. Gukoresha ururimi rwacu kavukire kandi twumva neza bituma ubumenyi butwegera, tukabugira ubwacu kandi tukabusangira, ndetse tukabusegasira. Ibihugu bikiri mu nzira yաmajyambere bikunze kohereza abanyeshuri kuvoma ubumenyi muri za kaminuza zo mu bihugu byateye imbere. Abenshi biga mu ndimi kavukire zթbyo bihugu bagiyemo: Icyongereza ku isonga, igifaransa, ikirusiya, igishinywa, igisipanyoro, ikidage nթzindi nyinshi. Iyo umunyeshuri arangije kwiga muri rumwe muri izo ndimi agasubira mu gihugu ke kavukire, akomeza kuba umuntu ku giti ke iyo ibyo yize atabyanditse mu rurimi rwe ngo abisangize nաbandi. Ibi ni byo abayapani banze, bahitamo imvugo igira iti Ҕubyakire tubigire ibyacuӮ Magingo aya, isi yose isizanira kujya mu Buyapani guhaha yo ubwenge! Ngicyo icyatumye twiyemeza gucura amuga ku bushakashatsi. Twifuzaga ko abashaka gukora ubushakashatsi bagera ku kigamijwe koko, aho kureremba mu ndimi zաmahanga batanumva neza. Twifuzaga ko abavuga Ikinyarwanda, bamenya gukora ubushakashatsi koko, bakabubyaza ubumenyi, ubwo bumenyi bakabuhererekanya, bakabukoresha kandi bakabugira ubwabo, mu yandi magambo, bukabafasha gukemura ibibazo nyabyo bahura na byo mu buzima bwa buri munsi. Ni ukuvuga ko ubumenyi bwagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi bukwiye kuba koko umusingi wաmajyambere arambye kandi ashingiye ku byo igihugu gikeneye.Undi mwihariko wթki gitabo ushingiye ku ngero zifatika zavuye mu buzima bwa buri munsi bwաbanyarwanda nթzishobora kugaragara mu karere kաbakoresha urwo rurimi. Ni yo mpamvu iki gitabo cyandikiwe gufasha abantu bakoresha ururimi rwՉkinyarwanda, atari mu Rwanda gusa, ahubwo nաbari hakurya yarwo. Iki gitabo gishobora kwifashishwa nաbiga gukora ubushakashatsi, abanyeshuri, abarimu bյbushakashatsi cyanecyane mu bumenyi nyamuntu nթmibanire yաbantu, abayobozi bյbushakashatsi nաbashakashatsi ubwabo. Iki gitabo gishobora gufasha umuntu wese ushaka gukora ubushakashatsi ku giti ke cyangwa mu matsinda, kimwe nաbashaka gutegura umushinga wյbushakashatsi kugira ngo bashake inkunga yabafasha kuwushyira mu bikorwa.Ku buryo bwյmwihariko, iki gitabo kizarushaho kugira akamaro igihe gikoreshejwe mu mahugurwa nաmasomo yo gutegura umushinga wյbushakashatsi no kuwushyira mu bikorwa. Icyo gihe, utanga amahugurwa nյwigisha bashobora guhuriza abahugurwa mu matsinda matomato kugira ngo bungurane ibitekerezo kuri buri ntambwe yo gutegura no gukora ubushakashatsi bifashishije ingero zifatika. Gukorera mu matsinda ateguwe neza bituma uhugurwa wese ashobora kubona umwanya wo gutanga igitekerezo. Ibyo kandi bimufasha kugerageza gucengera no gushyira mu bikorwa ibyigwa. Amatsinda afasha uwiga kubaza, gusobanuza no gusobanurira bagenzi be, gusesengura, kujora no gufatanya nաbandi gutanga ingero yendeye ku buzima bwa buri munsi. Mu bihugu byakataje mu majyambere, usanga ubushakashatsi ari nkթtara rimurikira ibikorwa byաmajyambere kandi bukaba nյmuyoboro wթterambere rirambye haba mu bukungu, ubumenyi nթkoranabuhanga, imibereho myiza yաbaturage, imiyoborere yթgihugu, umutekano no mu zindi nzego. Isano iri hagati yյbushakashatsi nթterambere rirambye ishingiye ahanini ku ivumburabumenyi cyangwa se mu yandi magambo ku igaragazabumenyi rikorwa nաbashakashatsi. Ubwo bumenyi bwavumbuwe bushobora kwifashishwa mu gusobanura, guhanga, guteganya cyangwa se kugenzura ibibera mu gihugu ndetse nթbihakorerwa. Ni ukuvuga ko itandukaniro hagati yյbushakashatsi nzimbuzi (foundamental research) nյbushakashatsi ngiro (applied research) rigenda rigabanuka. Mu yandi magambo, ubushakashatsi ntibuberaho kuvumbura ubumenyi gusa kutagamije gukemura ibibazo biriho kimwe nյko budashingira ku gukemura ibibazo biriho gusa ngo busige inyuma guhanga ubumenyi bushya. Ubushakashatsi nzimbuzi nյbushakashatsi ngiro rero ni magirirane. Ubu bumwe bwյbushakashatsi ni bwo iki gitabo cyubakiyeho, ari na yo mpamvu hakoreshejwe ijambo rimwe ryյbushakashatsi ribumbye icyo gisobanuro.Ibiri muri iki gitaboIki gitabo kigabanyijemo ibice bibiri byթngenzi. Igice cya mbere kiraduha ihange ari wo musingi iki gitabo cyubakiyeho. Mu mutwe wa mbere, Mukama na Nkusi baradushushanyiriza igitereko kթki gitabo. Barasesengura imizi yյbushakashatsi nաkamaro kյbushakakashatsi mu gushakisha ukuri. Abanditsi bյyu mutwe baradutekerereza impamvu iki gitabo cyanditswe mu Kinyarwanda nյmwihariko wacyo mu ruhando bwթvumburabumenyi.Mu mutwe 2, Ntakirutimana, Mukama na Niyibizi barasobanura isano iri hagati yյbushakashatsi, ururimi nյmuco. Barerekana ukuntu ururimi rufasha mu gutekereza, kubaka no gutangaza ibitekerezo. Basobanura uko ururimi rugize umuyoboro ubumenyi bwubakwamo kandi bugahererekanywamo. Mu mutwe 3, Nkejabahizi asesengura uko ubuvanganzo nյbushakashatsi ari magirirane kandi byombi bigafata ibara ryյmuco wa ba nyirabyo. Arerekana uruhare rwթsesenguranyandiko nթjoranganzo mu bumenyi nyamuntu. Nkejabahizi ashimangira ko ubushakashatsi ku buvanganzo bwաhantu nաbantu runaka butaba bugamije gusa kuvumbura ubumenyi bushya ahuko ko bunagira akamaro mu guteza imbere umuco wյrurimi bwakozwemo. Nkejabahizi aravuga ku isano ubushakashatsi bugira mu iterambere ryթgihugu ndetse akerekana uburyo ikoranabuhanga rigenda ryagura iyoboramikorere ryյbushakashatsi.Mu mutwe 4, Ruterana aragaragaza kandi akanasesengura amahame ngengamyitwarire mu bushakashatsi. Arasobanura akamaro kayo nթbyangomba bigomba kwitabwaho kugira ngo ayo mahame yubahirizwe ahereye ku burenganzira ntavogerwa bwաbatangamakuru: uruhushya rwo gutanga amakuru, kutamena ibanga, kutavamo uwaguhaye amakuru, kutavuga uwatanze amakuru, gusaba uburenganzira bwo gukora ubushakashatsi no guhura nաbatangamakuru, ukutavogerwa, gukemura ibibazo byagizwe nյmutangamakuru bitewe nյko amakuru yatanze yagiye ku karubanda, cyangwa se bitewe nթngaruka / ihungabana ashobora kugira kubera ko yahishwe ku bushake impamvu nyayo yյbushakashatsi nթbindi.Igice cya kabiri kթki gitabo kirinjiza umusomyi mu migendekere yյbushakashatsi nyirizina: uko butegurwa, uko bukorwa nյko ibyagaragajwe na bwo bitangazwa. Mu mutwe 5, Mukama na Nkusi barasobanura akamaro ko gusesengura ibyanditswe mbere mu bushakashatsi harimo gutuma abantu bashobora guhererekanya ubumenyi no kubwubakiraho ifatiro ryյbundi bumenyi bushya; gufasha umushakashatsi kwerekana igishya azanye mu bisanzwe bizwi cyangwa se kubitangaho ibisobanuro byթnyongera; kugaragaza icyuho umushakashatsi aje kuziba mu bumenyi busanzwe buzwi no gukora inyigo ku bitarigeze byigwaho na gato. Muri uyu mutwe, Mukama na Nkusi barasobanura iyoboramikorere ryo gusesengura ibyanditse mbere. Barasobanura inkomoko yթnsanganyamatsiko, inkeneragihamya nթbibazo byյbushakashatsi.Mu mutwe 6, Mukama, Kagwesage, Uwizeye na Ndikubwimana bava imuzi uburyo bwo gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru. Barasobanura akamaro kթtsinda nkeshwamakuru mu bushakashatsi, igihe baritegurira, uko bahitamo ingano yaryo nյko babikora. Baratanga ingero zifatika zo gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru: uburyo bwo gutoranya amatsinda nkeshwamakuru ashingiye kuri tombola nաshingiye ku ihitamo.Mu mutwe 7, Ngarambe, Mulindahabi na Mukama berekana uburyo bugari bwթyoboramikorere bukunze kwifashwishwa mu ikusanyamakuru nթsesenguramakuru. Nkյko twabivuze hejuru, uburyo bwo kukora ubushakashatsi bushobora gushyirwa mu mirongo migari itatu: ubushakashatsi nyamubaro, ubushakashatsi nyamimerere nյbushakashatsi rukomatanyo. Muri uyu mutwe hibanzwe cyane ku bushakashatsi nyamimerere nյbwo hagaragaramo ingingo ziranga ubushakashatsi nyamubaro nյbushakashatsi rukamatanyo.Mu mutwe 8, Mukama, Rutayisire na Nzahabwanayo baribanda ku isuzuma nթsesengura ryաmakuru nyamubaro hakoreshejwe ibarurishamibare. Uyu mutwe ni ingirakamaro kandi birashoboka ko abanyeshuri bakora ubushakashatsi burangiza amashuri makuru bazawukunda. Mukama na bagenzi be bawanditse ku buryo butinyura abanyeshuri kwifashisha ibarurishamibare mu gusesengura amakuru nyamubaro bakoresheje intoki cyangwa porogaramu yo muri mudasobwa izwi nka Excel. Abanyeshuri benshi bakunda kubaza ibibazo byյbushakashatsi bisaba gusesengurwa bakoresheje ibarurishamibare. Nyamara bo bakabisobanura ku buryo nyamimerere. Uyu mutwe wթki gitabo rero uje kubafasha gukemura icyo kibazo hifashishijwe ingero zifatika nթmvugo yoroshye kuyumva. Mukama na bagenzi be baragira bati ҵyu mutwe uzafasha ushaka gukoresha amakuru nyamubaro gukora inyigo iboneye bitewe nաmatsinda nkeshwamakuru nթmfatashusho byakoreshejwe, ndetse ashobore no gutanga igisobanuro no gufata imyanzuro ikwiye ku isesengura yakozeӮ Hari uburyo bwinshi bwo gukusanya no gusesengura amakuru nyamubaro. Uyu mutwe wթki gitabo wibanze ku bwթbanze kandi bukunze gukoreshwa. Umutwe 9 ari na wo wa nyuma uribanda ku gusesengura uko bategura nյko bashyira ahagaragara ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi. Mukama, Rusanganwa, Uwimana na Bazirete barasobanura ingingo ku yindi uko umushakashatsi yandika ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi nյko akora isobanura bwite. Abanditsi bյyu mutwe barifashisha ingero zifatika mu kwerekana uko umushakashatsi asubiza ibibazo byյbushashatsi yibazaga kuva mu ikubitoro. Ni ngomba ko umushakashatsi yerekana mu buryo butomoye akarusho kյbushakashatsi bwe, haba ari ugutanga ibisubizo kuri buri kibazo cyյbushakashatsi yibazaga, haba se umusanzu atanze mu kongera ubumenyi bwari busanzwe buzwi, haba se uruhare ubushakashatsi bwe bugiye kugira mu gukemura ibibazo biriho mu gihugu nթbindi. Byongeye, abanditsi bյyu mutwe barerekana uko umushakashatsi yandika umusozo wյbushakashatsi bwe. Uyu mutwe ni wo twagize umusozo wթki gitabo. Urutonde rwաmuga yakoreshejwe: nkյko twabivuze haruguru, kwandika iki gitabo ntibyari gushoboka iyo tudahanga amuga mashya yյbushakashatsi. Kugira ngo rero dufashe umusomyi usanzwe uzi ururimi rwՉcyongereza gusobanukirwa vuba amuga twakoresheje, twakoze urutonde rwաmuga yՉkinyarwanda maze tuyaherekesha ayo bivuga kimwe mu rurimi rwՉcyongereza. Ayo muga ari ku mugereka wթki gitabo.IndangasokoBenton, T., & Craib, I. (2001). Philosophy of social science: The philosophical foundations of social thouhgt. New York: Palgrave.Burrell, G., & Morgan, G. (1979). Sociological paradigms and organizational analysis. London: Heinemann Educational Books.Davis, J. E. (2014). Terence interrupted: Literary biography and the reception of the Terentian canon. American Journal of Philology, 135(3), 387 Р409.Forehand, W. E. (1985). Terence. Boston: Twayne.Kagame, A. (1976). La philosophie bantu compare. Paris: Prsence Africaine.Mariragaba Baributsa. (Avril-Juin 1988). Alexis Kagame et le dbat philosophique. Revue Trimestrielle, 20, 149-166.Martinon. (2013). After ҒwandaӺ In search of a new ethics. Amsterdam: Editions Rodopi B.V.Mouly, G. J. (1978). Educational research: The art and science of investigation. Boston: Allyn & Bacon.Myers, M. D. (2008). Qualitative research in business & management. London: SAGE Publications.Pizam, A., & Mansfeld, Y. (2009). Consumer behaviour in travel and tourism. London: Taylor.Thomas, V. L. (1977). La philosophie bantou compare par Alexis Kagame. Archives de sciences des religions, 43, 266 Р267.IGICE I Ireme ryՕbushakashatsiUMUTWE 2 UBUSHAKASHATSI,  URURIMI NՕBUREZIEvarisiti Ntakirutimana, Evode Mukama na Epimake NiyibiziInshamakeUrurimi rwubakiye ku muco ndetse rukaba nյmuyoboro wթmyigire nթmyigishirize. Ururimi rurigwa, rukigishwa. Umuco na wo ni uko, urahererekanywa kandi ukagenda uhinduka buhorobuhoro kubera ko nթsi dutuye ihinduka, cyanecyane muri iki gihe ikusanyabukungu nթkoranabuhanga bidusunikana imbaraga nyinshi. Umuco wթgihugu cyangwa wաhantu runaka ushobora gucengerwamo nթmico yաhandi. Ni ngomba gushungura, hagafatwa gusa ibyաhandi bifite akamaro. Ubushakashatsi ku muco rero ni ngombwa kugira ngo hagaragazwe ibikwiye. Iyo abantu babihuriyeho ari benshi, kubihererekanya mu muryango binyuze mu nzira rusange yo kurera no kwigisha biroroha, bityo bikaba umusemburo wթterambere, bigatuma nյrurimi ari rwo muyoboro wյmuco rudasigara inyuma. Umwana atozwa umuco byյmwihariko nյmuryango avukiyemo ndetse nաmashuri. Uyu mutwe rero uribanda ku isano iri hagati yյbushakashatsi, ururimi nյmuco.IriburiroMuri iki gihe, nta we ushidikanya ko ishuri ari isoko yյburezi, uburere nյbumenyi. Ni ngombwa rero ko riha umwanya ufatika ubushakashatsi kugira ngo abaryigamo nաbarirangije bafunguke, bashobore guhindura isi nաbayituye. Muri iki gikorwa, ururimi rufite uruhare runini cyane. Ni rwo rutuma abiga bumvikana nաbigisha, bigatuma bumva neza ibyo biga. Ni na rwo rutuma ibyo bize bashobora kubyifashisha mu buzima bwa buri munsi no gufasha abandi kubyungukiramo, bagatera intambwe nkթyabo cyangwa yisumbuyeho. Umwanzuro wa karindwi wՉnama yՉgihugu yՕmushyikirano ya 15 yo ku wa 18 na 19 Ukuboza 2017, ushishikariza Abanyarwanda ҇ukomeza gushimangira ubufatanye hagati yթnzego za Leta, ababyeyi, sosiyete sivile nթmiryango ishingiye ku madini nաmatorero mu kurushaho kwigisha ururimi rwՉkinyarwanda bihereye mu muryango, mu mashuri, mu biganiro bitangwa mu bitangazamakuru, kandi Abanyarwanda bթngeri zose bagahugukira kwiga, kumenya no gukoresha neza IkinyarwandaӠ(Guverinoma yյ Rwanda, 2017). Ibi birerekana ko ururimi rufasha umuntu kugera ku migambi yiyemeje, binyuze mu bukangurambaga no mu biganiro. Ibi kandi biragaragaza ko mbere yo kwifuza kumenya indimi zաhandi, umunyarwanda akwiye kubanza kumenya neza ururimi rwe kavukire, ari narwo rushobora kumufasha kwiga izindi ku buryo bushyitse kandi bwihuse. Ubushakashatsi ku rurimi: ururimi nkյmuyoboro wյbumenyi nթbitekerezoAkamaro kթbanze kյbushakashatsi ni ukuba imvumburabumenyi. Icyo abahanga benshi bahurizaho ni uko ubumenyi buhangwa ndetse bugahererekanywa binyuze mu rurimi (Piaget, 1981; 1926; Halliday, 1978; Vygotsky, 1978). Kuri iyi ngingo, Halliday (1978), umuhanga mu iyigandimi, asobanura ko ururimi rushora imizi mu muco. Yemeza kandi ko ururimi ari umusingi wo kwiga. Umuhanga mu mitekerereze yաbantu, Vygotsky (1978), agaragaza ko ururimi rugira imimaro ibiri itandukanye mu mitekerereze yյmuntu: ururimi ni igikoresho nyoborabitekerezo rukaba kandi nթgikoresho cyյmuco. Aha, Vygotsky aba ashaka kuvuga ko, ku ruhande rumwe, ururimi rufasha abantu gushyira ku murongo ibitekerezo byabo, kwiyumvisha ibintu mboneshwajisho ku buryo mboneshwabwenge. Ku rundi ruhande, ururimi nkթgikoresho cyյmuco, rufasha abantu kungurana ibitekerezo. Ibi ni byo bituma umuntu ashobora kugereranya ibitekerezo bye nթbyաbandi, ari byo bishobora kuvamo kubyemera, kubyubakiraho, kubyongera cyangwa se kubinenga no kubikosora. Ni ukuvuga ko ku byerekeye ubushakashatsi, ururimi rushobora kubera ubukungu abarwumva neza, ariko rukabera inshoberamahanga abataruzi.Kimwe nաbandi bahanga benshi, Wells (1999) avuga ko iyo umuntu yiga ururimi rwe kavukire aba yicengezamo umuco urwo rurimi ruhetse. Kumenya ururimi nyabyo, bisaba kumenya umuco urwo rurimi rubumbatiye kugira ngo ubashe gusobanukirwa nթnshoza zirukoreshwamo cyangwa se ushobore kwishushanyiriza igitekerezo gikubiye mu bivugwa. Birumvikana rero ko umuntu yubaka ibitekerezo bye ku buryo bunoze mu rurimi yumva neza, akenshi ruba ari ururimi kavukire. Nko mu mvugo zՁbanyarwanda ziranga amasaha: ku gasusuruko, inyana zisubiye iswa, mu mataha yթnka, inka zishotse, nթzindi, utari umunyarwanda ntahita yumva icyo zivuga. Twatanga urugero rwյmwana mwarimu wՉkinyarwanda yabajije icyo ҫurara ubusaӠbivuga. Umwana kubera ko atigeze aburara yihutiye gusubiza umwarimu ko ari ukurara utambaye imyambaro yo kuryamana ҰijamaӠ(pyjama). Urundi rugero ni urwյmuntu babwiye ko ҡsa na bikeӠagahita arakara kuko yumvaga bamututse. Mbere yo kumva ururimi rero umuntu agomba kubanza kumenya umuco wաbaruvuga. Kurwiga bigasaba kwiga uwo muco. Mu Rwanda hari ubushakashatsi bwakozwe ku myigire nթmyigishirize yթndimi bugamije kugaragaza akamaro kյrurimi mu burezi. Bumwe muri ubwo bushakashatsi bwakozwe na Ntakirutimana, Williams, Nayimfashe na OՓullivan (2004), bagamije gusuzuma ubushobozi bwo gusoma no gusobanura ibyasomwe mu ndimi zakoreshwaga mu mashuri icyo gihe (Icyongereza, Igifaransa nՉkinyarwanda). Bafatiye ku itsinda nkenshwamakuru ryաbanyeshuri 958 bo mu mashuri abanza nաyisumbuye, barimo abakobwa 509 nաbahungu 449. Ubwo bushakashatsi bwagaragaje ko abanyeshuri bՁbanyarwanda bafite ubushobozi buke cyane mu ndimi mvamahanga ariko bakagaragaza ubushobozi mu rurimi rwabo kavukire, Ikinyarwanda. Muri rusange, abanyeshuri bashyizwe mu byiciro bitatu: Ikiciro cyաbadashoboye (amanota ari munsi ya 50 %), ikiciro cyաbagerageza (hagati ya 50 na 65%), nթkiciro cyաbashoboye (hejuru ya 65%). Ubu bushakashatsi bwakozwe mu 2004 bwagaragaje ko 12.92% byաbanyeshuri bari barangije amashuri yisumbuye bari bafite ubushobozi buke mu gusoma no gusobanura ibyasomwe mu rurimi rwՉgifaransa, naho 28.71% barageragezaga, mu gihe 58.37% bari babishoboye. Ubwo bushakashatsi bwasanze ubushobozi buke bwաbanyeshuri barangije ayisumbuye mu gusoma no gusobanura ibyo basomye, bwagaragaraga cyane mu rurimi rwՉcyongereza (53.58%), mu gihe 20.1% bageragezaga, naho abari babishoboye bakaba 26.32%. Ntakirutimana na bagenzi be bemeza ko muri uwo mwaka wa 2004 abanyeshuri hafi ya bose (97.13%) bari bashoboye kumva Ikinyarwanda, mu gihe 2.87% bonyine ari bo bageragezaga. Aha twakwibutsa ko Itegeko Nshinga rya Pepubulika yյ Rwanda ryo muri 2003 uko ryavuguruwe kugeza ubu rivuga ko Ikinyarwanda ari rwo rurimi rwթgihugu, naho Icyongereza, Igifaransa nՉgiswayire zikaba indimi zemewe gukoreshwa mu nzego za Leta kimwe nՉkinyarwanda. Mbere ya jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu wa 1994, ururimi rwo kwigishwamo mu mashuri abanza rwari Ikinyarwanda naho mu mashuri yisumbuye na Kaminuza rukaba Igifaransa. Nyuma yaho, u Rwanda rwatangiye gukoresha indimi eshatu, bityo ururimi rwo kwigishamo mu mashuri abanza rukomeza kuba Ikinyarwanda, mu gihe Igifaransa nՉcyongereza byigishwaga nkաmasomo. Mu mashuri yisumbuye ho, umunyeshuri yashoboraga guhitamo kwigishwa mu Gifaransa gusa cyangwa se mu Cyongereza gusa, mu gihe Ikinyarwanda na rumwe muri izo ndimi zաmahanga atahisemo zigishwaga nkաmasomo. Ibyo byarangiranye nյmwaka wa 2008 kuko guhera muri 2009, ururimi rwo kwigishwamo mu mashuri yisumbuye mu Rwanda rwabaye Icyongereza gusa mu gihe izindi ndimi zigishwaga nkաmasomo (Guverinoma yյ Rwanda, 2008; Minisiteri yՕburezi, 2009, Werurwe; 2011).Ubushakashatsi bwa Ntakirutimana na bagenzi be (2004) bwerekana ko umwana wՕmunyarwanda yagombye kwigishwa mu rurimi rwe kavukire kuko ari rwo afitemo ubushobozi buhagije. Ibi ariko ntibivugwaho rumwe, kubera ko akamaro kյrurimi katareberwa gusa ku bushobozi umuntu arufitemo. Ni na ngombwa kwita ku mubare wաbaruvuga, ingeri zյbuhanga nթzյbuzima busanzwe rukoreshwamo, uko aho rukoreshwa hangana, iterambere ryաbarukoresha, nթbindi. Mbese muri rusange akamaro kյrurimi kagomba kureberwa mu ndorerwamo yթkusanyabukungu nթkoranabuhanga. Ibi ni byo bituma Ikinyarwanda gihura nթngorane mu kwemerwa nkյrurimi rwo kwigisha Abanyarwanda. Umwanya wacyo mu ikusanyabukungu nթkoranabuhanga uracyari muto cyane.Ubushakashatsi bwa Mukama (2007; 2008) bwasuzumaga uko abanyeshuri bo mu mashuri makuru basesengura amakuru yյbumenyi bakura kuri murandasi bwagaragaje ko iyo abo banyeshuri bari mu matsinda, bakoresha cyane ururimi rwabo kavukire kabone nթyo inyandiko baganiraho iba iri mu Cyongereza cyangwa mu Gifaransa. Ubu bushakashatsi bwagaragaje ko Ikinyarwanda ari cyo kibafasha kwisanzura mu bitekerezo, kujya impaka, gusobanurirana, gusesengura no gusuzuma ibyanditswe ku buryo bashobora kugera ku mwanzuro wabo bwite bishimiye kandi bumvikanyeho. Ni ukuvuga ko Abanyarwanda bashobora kwifashisha ururimi rwՉkinyarwanda mu kubaka ubumenyi bumvikanyeho kandi ibi ni ingenzi mu burezi. Ubumenyi bwubatswe kandi bukumvikanywaho nաbavuga ururimi bumva neza no mu muco wabo, usanga bwihutisha gukemura ibibazo nyamukuru bwաbo bantu. Ingero twatanga ni izյkuntu Abanyarwanda bakiriye vuba kandi bakagira izabo gahunda zթtorero, gira inka munyarwanda, ubudehe, gacaca nթzindi. Izi gahunda ziri mu rurimi bumva neza, mu muco wabo karande kandi zirasubiza ibibazo byabo bya buri munsi. Ni uko nյbumenyi mu ishuri bwagombye kubakwa no kwigishwa.Mukama (2008) asobanura ko abanyeshuri bՁbanyarwanda bari mu Rwanda babaho ubuzima butandukanye bitewe nյrurimi bakoresha. Ku ruhande rumwe, baba mu buzima bwo mu ishuri, bwubakiye ku rurimi baba basabwa kwigishwamo. Ku rundi ruhande, bagaruka mu buzima bwa buri munsi iyo basohotse mu ishuri, aho barara, aho birirwa, aho bafungurira, mu nsengero, ku isoko, mu kazi nաhandi hose bavuga ururimi rwabo kavukire. Mukama yerekana kandi ko uku gutandukana kwյbuzima bwo mu ishuri nյbwo hanze yaryo bushobora kuba inzitizi ikomeye mu kubaka uburezi bufite ireme no mu gushimangira iterambere rirambye kandi ryihuse. Ni yo mpamvu asaba ko imipaka hagati yթndimi zikoreshwa mu gihugu yari ikwiye kuvanwaho igasimburwa nյbwuzuzanye bwazo. Uyu mushakashatsi ashimangira ko, aho bishoboka, Ikinyarwanda cyari gikwiye kwigishwamo bitewe nթkigamijwe. Urugero: niba isomo ari ukwiga gutera igiti, kugitera nyirizina no kukitaho ngo kizatange umusaruro ugitegerejweho, kubyiga mu ndimi zաmahanga ntacyo byongera ku kigamijwe. Ahubwo izo ndimi zishobora kuba imbogamizi zo kugera ku ntego mu gihe uwiga cyangwa uwigisha atazizi neza. Nyamara igihe ikigamijwe ari ugusangira ubumenyi cyangwa guhererekanya umusaruro wթgiti ku isoko mpuzamahanga, aha kwiga mu ndimi zաmahanga bishobora kugira akamaro. Ubwuzuzanye bwթndimi Mukama avuga muri urwo rugero ni uko uwize mu rurimi rwՉkinyarwanda gutanga umusaruro wթgiti mwiza kandi mwinshi mu gihe gikwiye yakuzuzanya nյwize mu ndimi mvamahanga kuwucuruza mu banyamahanga cyanecyane ko ubwumvane bwabo buca mu ndimi mpuzamahanga. Mukama asobanura ko ibi bishobora kugira agaciro mu guteza imbere uburezi bwa bose, kwihuta mu iterambere, gushimangira uburezi bufite ireme kandi bushingiye ku musaruro ugamijwe kugerwaho. Ubundi bushakashatsi ni ubwakozwe hagati ya 2007 na 2009 nթtsinda rigizwe na Ntakirutimana, Lyambabaje na Iyakaremye (2016) bagamije kwerekana isano iri hagati yյrurimi, imyigire nթmyigishirize byթnyigisho zյbuhanga nթkoranabuhanga. Ubu bushakashatsi bwerekanye ko abanyeshuri bաbahanga mu ndimi ari nabo batsinda neza amasomo yյbuhanga nթkoranabuhanga. Ndetse nթyo urenze urwego rwաbanyeshuri ku giti cyabo, usanga ibigo byաmashuri bitsinda neza mu ndimi ari na byo bitsinda neza mu masomo yյbuhanga nթkoranabuhanga. Ubu bushakashatsi bwafatiye ku masuzumabumenyi ba nyirabwo batanze mu mashuri yisumbuye 38 akusanya abanyeshuri 1537. Nyuma baza no gusesengura amanota yաbanyeshuri yatangajwe nՉkigo kՉgihugu Gishinzwe Guteza Imbere Uburezi (REB), basanga nayo ashimangira ibyagaragajwe nաmanota yաmasuzuma. Ibi birerekana akamaro kյrurimi mu burezi. Muri rusange rero, ireme ryյburezi rifite imizi mu myigire nթmyigishirize yթndimi. Kugira ngo ushobore kwiga wumve ibyo wiga, ugomba kumva indimi zikoreshwa mu nyigisho mbere na mbere. Ugomba kandi kumenya nթndimi zաmahanga kugira ngo umenye aho abandi bageze nթbyo bakora. Mu Kinyarwanda umuntu udaciye akenge, dukunze kumwita umwana. Iyo usesenguye usanga ibi bifite aho bihuriye nթjambo ryՉgifaransa enfant. Iri jambo rikomoka ku rurimi rwՉkiratini infans aho risobanura ҵmuntu utazi kuvuga, umuntu utaramenya kuvugaӱ (Roquefort (de), 1829, p. 273). Nanone, umuntu yabihuza nթmvugo ya kinyarwanda igira iti ҉kinyoni kigurutse kitavuze bakita icyanaӮ Iyi mvugo ishobora kwerekana ukuntu ururimi ari umuyoboro wյbumenyi nյbuhanga. Ikigaragara rero ni uko ururimi kavukire rwՉkinyarwanda rwumvwa kandi ruvugwa na benshi, emwe ndetse bakarwisanzuramo cyane, ugereranyije nթzindi ndimi zikoreshwa mu Rwanda. Ibi birashimangirwa nթsesengura Niyibizi na Ahimana (2018) bakoze bagereranya ubushobozi bwo gusoma hagati yաbanyeshuri bo mu mashuri abanza bo mu Rwanda, muri Malawi no muri Zambiya, hagereranywa indimi kavukire zo muri ibyo bihugu nՉcyongereza. Iryo gereranya ryari rishingiye ku byavuye mu bushakashatsi bwakozwe na Williams (1996; 1998), Williams, Nayimfashe, Ntakirutimana na OՓullivan (2004), ndetse nյbwakozwe na Niyibizi (2016). Iryo gereranya ryagaragaje ko abanyeshuri bari bazi gusoma neza mu ndimi kavukire, kuko 90% babashije gusoma neza mu Kinyarwanda, 65% bashoboye gusoma neza mu rurimi rwa Chichewa rwo muri Malawi kandi rwigishwamo, naho 10% gusa nibo bashoboye gusoma neza mu rurimi rwitwa ChiNyanja rukoreshwa muri Zambiya, ariko rutigishwamo andi masomo. Ibi bikatugaragariza ko ururimi kavukire rumenywa neza iyo rukoreshwa mu kwigisha andi masomo. Muri ubu bushakashatsi kandi, 99.33% byաbanyeshuri 251 bյmwaka wa gatandatu wաmashuri abanza bari batoranyijwe mu Rwanda ntibashoboye gusoma neza mu Cyongereza (Williams na bagenzi be, 2004); 70% byաbanyeshuri 290 bo mu mwaka wa gatandatu wաmashuri abanza muri Malawi ntibashoboye gusoma neza mu Cyongereza (Williams, 1996); mu gihe 74% mu banyeshuri 227 bo mu mwaka wa gatandatu wաmashuri abanza muri Zambiya batabashije gusoma neza mu Cyongereza (Williams, 1998). Ibi birashimangira ibyagaragajwe nաbandi bashakashatsi twavuze hejuru, ko abanyeshuri batamenya neza izi ndimi zաmahanga. Uretse abanyeshuri, nաbarimu ubwabo bagaragagaza ko basanga batazi kuvuga neza izi ndimi zաmahanga, nյbwo bazigisha bwose. Mu bushakashatsi Niyibizi (2016) yakoze ku barimu nաbanyeshuri 324 bo mu mwaka wa mbere kugeza mu wa gatatu wաmashuri abanza mu Rwanda, abarimu 44.4% bo mu mashuri yo mu cyaro berekanye ko ari bo bazi kuvuga Icyongereza neza nյbwo bakigishagamo bwose, mu gihe 88,9% bagaragaje ko bazi kuvuga neza Ikinyarwanda. Ibi birakomeza kutugaragariza ko indimi kavukire zimenywa neza kurusha indimi zաmahanga.Ikindi cyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi mu myigire yթndimi, ni uko ari byiza kwiga indimi umuntu akiri muto. Icyo gihe agace kյbwonko kita ku byerekeye indimi, kaba kagifite ubushobozi bwinshi bukagenda bugabanuka uko umuntu akura. Iyo umuntu akiri muto, ibigabane bibiri bigize ubwonko bwe biba bikorana bya hafi. Uku gukorana kugenda kugabanuka, noneho buri rugingo rukagira umumaro warwo rwihariye. Ni yo mpamvu umuntu ukiri muto, utarengeje cyane imyaka 20, ashobora gutakaza ubushobozi bwo kuvuga, bukagaruka; ariko iyo akuze ntibishoboka cyangwa se bikagorana cyane, nkյko byagaragajwe nաbahanga nka Abdelilah-Bauer (2006), Nikolov na Djigunovic (2006) nաbandi. Aha bagaragaza ko ari byiza ko umuntu yiga indimi akeneye akiri muto rero. Gusa aha twavuga ko nanone abahanga mu byթyigandimi batabivugaho rumwe, kuko hari abavuga ko umuntu afite ubushobozi bwo kwiga no kumenya ururimi neza, yaba muto cyangwa ashaje. Bamwe mu bashakashatsi mu byթndimi bemeza ko kwiga indimi umwana akiri muto bituma azimenya neza barimo UNESCO (1953/1968, 2003), SkutnabbKangas (2000), Singleton (1989), Alexander (1999), Benson (2003, October), Cummins (2000) nաbandi. Aba bashimangira ko ari ngombwa guhera no kubanza kumenya neza ururimi kavukire mbere yo kwiga indimi zindi. Gusa hari nաbemeza ko ku myaka iyo ari yo yose umuntu yakwiga ururimi akarumenya neza, barimo Nikolov na Djigunovic (2006), Abdelilah-Bauer (2006), Spolsky (2004), Baker (2006) nաbandi. Imyaka fatizo yibandwaho mu kumenya neza izo ndimi kavukire ni ukugeza ku myaka 12 ndetse no kugeza ku bugimbi (Collier, 1989; MarinovaTodd, Marshall, & Snow, 2000). Ni ukuvuga ko umunyeshuri yakagombye gukomeza kwiga amasomo yose mu rurimi kavukire kugeza nibura mu mwaka wa gatandatu wաmashuri abanza. Gusa nanone ubushakashatsi bwakozwe na Nikolov na Djigunovic (2006) bwagaragaje ko abantu bize indimi nyuma yթgihe cyյbugimbi bazimenya neza nka bene zo bazize nkթndimi kavukire. Mu burezi rero, abashinzwe integanyanyigisho bari bakwiye kureba ukuntu indimi zakurikirana ku buryo ya myaka yյbugimbi twavuze yagera umunyeshuri amaze kuzimenya. Zigomba gukurikirana hakurikijwe inyurabwenge ishobora gushingira ku masano hagati yթndimi cyangwa se ku hantu umunyeshuri ahurira nazo mu buzima bwe bwa buri munsi.Gusa nanone, ntitwavuga ku myigishirize yթndimi muri iki gihe, tutavuze ku ivangandimi, ari mu Rwanda ndetse no ku isi hose. Twibanze iwacu mu Rwanda, ubushakashatsi bugaragaza ko ivangandimi rikoreshwa nաbanyeshuri nաbarimu bo mu byiciro byose byյburezi. Muri ibi byiciro byյburezi, ubushakashatsi bwakozwe na Niyibizi (2015) na Niyibizi, Makalela na Mwepu (2015) bwagaragaje ko abarimu nաbanyeshuri bo mu mashuri abanza bo mu wa mbere kugeza mu wa gatatu bakoresha ivangandimi mu ishuri; ubwa Habyarimana (2014) bugaragaza ko abo mu mwaka wa gatandatu wաmashuri abanza babukoresha; ubwa Maniraho (2015) bugaragaza ko mu mashuri yisumbuye ategura abarimu (TTC) na bo bavanga indimi; ndetse no muri Kaminuza, nkյko ubushakashatsi bwa Niyomugabo (2012), ubwa Kagwesage (2013), nյbwa Niyomugabo, Sibomana na Niyibizi (2018) bwabigaragaje. Ivangandimi ntirikoreshwa mu Rwanda cyangwa muri Afurika gusa, ahubwo rigaragara mu bice byose byթsi. Ivangandimi abantu baryishimira ku buryo butandukanye, bamwe bagaragaza ibyiza byazo mu myigishirize yթndimi, iyo rikoreshejwe neza cyangwa iyo dukoresheje ivangandimi riboneye (Makalela, 2014). Gusa hari nաbumva ko ivangandimi rihungabanya imyigishirize yթndimi, cyanecyane iyo hakoreshejwe ivangandimi ritaboneye (Canagarajah, 2013). Ikigaragara ni uko iri vangandimi na ryo rikenewe gusesengurwa mu buryo bwimbitse kuko akamaro kթvangandimi riboneye kagenda kigaragaza mu bijyanye nյbwuzuzanye bwթndimi mu myigishirize, cyanecyane mu bihugu bifite indimi nyinshi. Aha twashingira cyane ku gitekerezo cya Canagarajah (2013, p. 6) aho agira ati: ҉ndimi rwose ntabwo ziri mu makimbirane cyangwa mu ntambara cyangwa ngo zibe zihanganye hagati yazo, ahubwo ziruzuzanya mu gutuma abantu bavugana kandi bakumvanaӮ Mu mico yՁbanyafurika nթndimi zabo, Makalela (2016) agaragaza ko ivangandimi ryisanisha cyane nթmibereho yՁbanyafurika, rishingiye ku muco wՕbuntu. Ibi bigaragarira mu ntekerezo yise ҕbuntu TranslanguagingӠmu rurimi rwՉcyongereza, mu Kinyarwanda twasobanura nkՠ҉vangandimi rishingiye ku muco wՕbuntuӠ(Makalela, 2016). Aha Makalela ashingira ku mibanire myiza yթndimi maze ururimi rukabwira urundi ruti Ҏdiho kubera ko nawe urihoӻ ҕriho kubera ko natwe turihoӻ ҍugenzi wange ngwino iwange mu nzu kugira ngo nange numve ko nuzuyeӠ(Makalela, 2016, p. 6). Aba bahanga baratugaragariza ko ivangandimi ari ngombwa kandi rifite akamaro kuko indimi ziraturanye mu miryango yacu, mu mashuri nաhandi hose. Aha twakwibutsa ko ivangandimi ari ugutangira uvuga cyangwa wandika mu rurimi rumwe undi akagusubiza mu rundi rurimi, cyangwa se gukoresha indimi zitandukanye mu nteruro no mu migemo yթzo nteruro (Garcia, 2009; Gafaranga, 2015; Makalela, 2016). Nkյko bigaragarira buri wese muri iki gihe, ivangandimi rirakoreshwa mu ngeri nyinshi zթmibereho yաbantu, mu mashuri, mu biganiro no mu nyandiko zihererekanywa hagati yաbantu, ubanza tutaba dukabije tuvuze ko muri iki gihe rikoreshwa mu buzima bwa buri munsi, cyanecyane mu bihugu no mu miryango ifite indimi nyinshi. Mu Rwanda naho rirahari kuko dufite Ikinyarwanda mbonera nթndimi shami zacyo, tugakira Icyongereza, Igifaransa, Igiswayire, ndetse nթzindi ndimi zivugwa mu miryango imwe nթmwe cyangwa mu bantu bamwe na bamwe, bityo tukaba twumva ivangandimi rikoreshwa ahantu henshi.Ubushakashatsi ku muco nյmuco wյbushakashatsi mu bureziIjambo umuco abahanga bariburiye igisobanuro bahuriyeho. Ibisobanuro byթri jambo birenze 250. Ariko icya Taylor ni cyo usanga kenshi abantu bakunze kwibandaho. Taylor agira ati ҵmuco ni ikintu rukomatanya gikubakubiyemo byinshi nkյbumenyi, iyobokamana, imyuga nյbukorikori, ubupfura, amategeko, imigenzo nթbindi byose umuntu yigira mu muryango avukamo akahabana nաbandi2Ӡ(byahinduwe mu Kinyarwanda na Kamanzi, 2007, p. 12). Ibi birerekana ko umuco utavukanwa ahubwo wigishirizwa mu muryango. Umuco wաbantu aba nաba, ugaragarira mu mvugo no mu ngiro bya buri munsi. Ni ukuvuga ko ururimi ari umuyoboro umuco unyuramo kugira ngo ugere ku bandi. Ni byo Abanyarwanda bigisha iyo bavuga bati ҕtaraganiriye na se ntamenya icyo sekuru yavuzeӮ Ni byiza rero gukora ubushakashatsi tukamenya ibyiza ba sogokuru bavuze bityo tukabiherekanya tuzi icyo dukora.Ubushakashatsi ku muco nթndimi nyarwandaUmuco ni umusingi wթterambere rirambye maze ururimi na rwo rukaba ingobyi ihetse umucoNkյko byasobanuwe mbere, umuco ufite uruhare runini mu burezi no mu majyambere yթgihugu. Umuco kandi si ntayegayezwa, ntutura nkյmusozi, urahinduka buhorobuhoro, ariko iyo uhinduka cyane uracuya. Kera umuco nyarwanda wari ishingiro ryյbumwe nաmahoro, byombi bikaba umusingi wթterambere rirambye. Umuco kandi wari nkթmwe mu nkingi ya mwamba yյbukungu bwյ Rwanda, ugatozwa Abanyarwanda bթngeri zose binyuze mu miryango no mu matorero kandi buri wese akabigiramo uruhare. Umuco nyarwanda uriho, urakomeye kandi urakungahaye. Ikibura kenshi ni Abanyarwanda bawukomeyeho mu magambo no mu bikorwa. Kwigirira ikizere Abanyarwanda bafite muri iki gihe, banga ko hagira uwaza ngo abamire bunguri cyangwa se ngo abangamire ubusugire bwթgihugu, ni bimwe mu bishimangira ko umuco nyarwanda uriho. Ni yo mpamvu ari ngombwa kwiga no gusesengura ibiwuranga byose maze ibibi bigakosorwa, ibyiza bigasigasirwa. Umuco wթgihugu ni nkյmutima mu mubiri. Abanyarwanda babivuga neza iyo bagira bati ҁgahugu kabuze umuco karasiba kagasibanganaӮ Nkյko nta muntu ubaho atagira umutima, nta nթterambere ridashingiye ku muco wաbariharanira (Maniragaba Baributsa, 1987; Nahimana, 1988). Iyo rishingiye ku muco wa ba nyirawo, iterambere ririhuta kuko abantu baba babyumva kimwe. Kera umuco nyarwanda witaga ku bintu bikoze neza, ku kwanga umugayo, kugira ubupfura, ubutwari, gufatanya, gusabana, kwizerana, kubahiriza igihe, kwirinda ubuhemu, ikinyoma, kudashyira inda imbere, kutikanyiza, gukurikiza amategeko, kubaha umutungo kamere, ibidukikije nթbindi. Ibi byose iyo bikurikijwe, nta kabuza biba ishingiro ryաmajyambere arambye. Kuri iyi ngingo, uwabishaka yasoma agatabo ka Ntakirutimana (2011) gasesengura uko gusubira ku isoko nyarwanda byagize uruhare mu gukemura bimwe mu bibazo byյbukungu, imibanire, ubutabera nթbindi. Ubushakashatsi ku muco nyarwanda rero bwafasha kugera kuri byinshi bishimangira iterambere ryթgihugu. Gusa ntawashidikanya kwemeza ko ubushakashatsi ku muco bugenda biguru ntege atari ukubera amikoro make gusa, ahubwo nյmuhate wo kuwusigasira. Muri iki gihe, ibivugwa cyane nթndangagaciro na kirazira byյmuco nyarwanda. Ariko se mu ngeri zose zյbuhanga abakurambere bacu ntibari bihagazeho? Bari bazi kuvura indwara banga ko zibavutsa ubuzima cyangwa ubwisanzure. Iyo umuntu arebye neza, asanga ubushakashatsi ku muco nyarwanda bwaratangijwe nաbanyamadini bաbazungu muri za 1950. Nyuma Abanyarwanda, cyanecyane Aloyizi Bigirumwami na Alegisi Kagame, bunzemo. Ikindi kigaragara ni uko inyandiko nyinshi zanditswe mu ndimi zաmahanga, cyanecyane Igifaransa. Umuco rero ntusigana nյrurimi kuko abahanga nթnararibonye mu byյrurimi nյmuco bashimangira ko ururimi ari ingobyi ihetse umuco kandi rukaba umuyoboro wյmuco (Minisiteri yՕburezi, 2011; Baker, 2006). Mu Rwanda ho ni umwihariko wաgahebuzo, kuko dufite ҵrurimi rumwe, umuco umwe, mu gihugu kimweӠ(Minisiteri yՕburezi, 2011). Aha dutandukanye cyane nթbindi bihugu bifite ҩndimi zitandukanye nթmico itandukanye, mu gihugu kimweӠnkյko bigaragazwa na King na Van den Berg (1992) batanga urugero ku gihugu cya Afurika yՅpfo. U Rwanda kandi, kimwe nթbindi bihugu bitanu bya Afurika, bifite umwihariko wo kugira umubare munini cyane wաbaturage bavuga ururimi rumwe kavukire, mu Cyongereza bita ҥndoglossic countriesӬ nkյko bigaragazwa na Abdulaziz (1993). Ibyo bihugu ni u Rwanda, aho 99.4% bavuga Ikinyarwanda (MINECOFIN, 2014); u Burundi, aho abarenga 99% bavuga Ikirundi (Ndayipfukamiye, 1994); Somaliya, aho abarenga 95% bavuga Igisomali (Warsame, 2001); Swaziland, aho abarenga 80% bavuga Setswana. Hari kandi Lesotho, aho abaturage benshi cyane bavuga ururimi kavukire rwaho rwitwa Sesotho. Uyu ni umwihariko ugaragara muri ibi bihugu bitandatu bya Afurika, mu gihe mu bindi bihugu usanga abaturage bavuga indimi nyinshi kandi zitandukanye. U Rwanda kandi nյbwo rubarirwa mu bihugu bifite abaturage hafi ya bose bavuga ururimi kavukire rwՉkinyarwanda, rubarirwa no mu bihugu bikoresha indimi nyinshi. Izikoreshwa mu nzego zյbutegetsi ni enye, arizo Ikinyarwanda, Icyongereza, Igifaransa nՉgiswayire, dore ko zinagaragara mu ngingo ya 5 yՉtegekoNshinga rya Repubulika yյ Rwanda ryo muri 2003. Igiswayire cyo kemejwe nkյrurimi rwa kane rukoreshwa mu nzego zյbutegetsi muri 2017. Izi ndimi uko ari enye zivugwa nՁbanyarwanda ku rugero rutandukanye, ugereranyije ibice byթcyaro nթbyյmugi, cyangwa ukagereranya abagabo nաbagore. Imbonerahamwe zikurikira zirabigaragaza neza.Imbonerahamwe 1: I janisha (%) ryաbazi kuvuga buri rurimi ukurikije ibarura rusange ryաbaturage ryo mu 2002Aho byavuye: MINECOFIN (2005) Ibarura rusange ryաbaturage ryo muri 2002Imbonerahamwe 2: I janisha (%) ryաbazi kuvuga, gusoma, kwandika no kubara muri buri rurimi ukurikije ibarura rusange ryo mu 2012Aho byavuye: MINECOFIN (2014) Ibarura rusange ryաbaturage ryo muri 2012Iyi mbonerahamwe ya kabiri ifatiye ku Banyarwanda bafite imyaka 15 kuzamura, bazi gusoma, kwandika no kubara muri buri rurimi. Umuntu rero asesenguye imibare igaragazwa nթbarura rusange ryաbaturage ryo mu 2002, biragaragara ko abatuye u Rwanda bagera kuri 99.4% bazi kuvuga Ikinyarwanda mu gihe izindi ndimi twavuga ko zizwi nյmubare muto wՁbanyarwanda: Igifaransa: 3.9%, Icyongereza: 1.9% naho Igiswayire bakaba 3%. Nyamara ibarura rusange ryաbaturage ryabaye mu 2012 rigaragaza ko hari impinduka nyinshi zagiye ziba urebye umubare wՁbanyarwanda bazi gusoma, kwandika no kubara mu ndimi zikoreshwa mu Rwanda: Ikinyarwanda: 67.7%, Igifaransa: 11.4%, Icyongereza: 14.7%, izindi ndimi: 3.7%, naho abatazi gusoma, kwandika no kubara na mba muri izo ndimi zose bari 29.4%. Tugereranyije umugi nթcyaro, imbonerahamwe ziratwereka ko indimi zikoreshwa hombi, ariko imibare yաbazikoresha ikagenda itandukana. Indimi zose zikoreshwa nաbantu bթgitsina gore nաbթgitsina gabo, nabwo imibare ikagenda itandukanaho gato, mu bagore nաbakobwa, abagabo nաbahungu bo mu cyaro nաbo mu mugi. Iyi mibare rero iragaragaza ko Abanyarwanda baba bafite amahirwe menshi baramutse bakoresheshe Ikinyarwanda mu kwiga nkյrurimi bavuga cyane kandi bazi kwandika, gusoma no kubara barwifashishije kurusha izindi.Ku byerekeye ubushakashatsi ku muco nanone, umuntu ntiyakwirengagiza inyandiko zյbushakashatsi zanditswe nաbanyeshuri barangiza ikiciro cya mbere nթcya kabiri cya Kaminuza, cyanecyane mu ishami ryթndimi. Benshi bakoze ubushakashatsi ku ngeri zinyuranye zյmuco nyarwanda. Ikibabaje ni uko izo nyandiko zaheze mu nzu zթbitabo za Kaminuza, ntizigire icyo zimarira abadashobora kugerayo kuko batamenya cyangwa ngo bamenyeshwe ibikorerwa iyo. Ba nyirubushakashatsi nabo iyo bamaze kubumurika bakabona amanota, abenshi baherukira aho kuko icyabaharanyaga kiba kirangiye. Turabigarukaho mu gace gakurikira kerekeye umuco wյbushakashatsi.Umuco wյbushakashatsi mu RwandaIbyemezo bigomba gushingira ku bumenyi bwizwe gihangaMu Rwanda, ubushakashatsi bwaba bwaratangiye gukorwa ku buryo butaziguye mu gihe igihugu cyari indagizo yՁbabirigi. Ikigo kՉgihugu Gishinzwe Ubushakashatsi mu Buhinzi (Institut des Sciences Agronomiques du Rwanda), mu magambo ahinnye yՉgifaransa ISAR cyatangiye mu 1933 ari ikigo gikora inyigo ku buhinzi muri Kongo-Mbirigi no muri Ruanda-Urundi (Institut National pour lՅtude Agronomique du Congo-Belge), mu magambo yթmpine INEAC. Icyo kigo cya INEAC cyaje kubyara ISAR aho u Rwanda rumariye kubona ubwigenge muri 1962. Kuri ubu, ISAR yimuriwe mu Kigo Gishinzwe Ubuhinzi bita mu Cyongereza Rwanda Agricultural Board (RAB). Naho Ikigo cyՕbushakashatsi mu Bumenyi nՉkoranabuhanga cyo cyatangiye muri 1947/1948 ari Ikigo cyՕbushakashatsi mu Bumenyi cya Afrika yo Hagati (IRSAC). Icyo gihe imirimo yacyo yarebaga KongoMbirigi na Ruanda-Urundi. IRSAC yaje guhinduka Igiko kՉgihugu Gishinzwe Ubushakashatsi nՕbumenyi (INRS) muri 1964. INRS ni yo yahindutse Ikigo cyՕbushakashatsi mu Bumenyi nՉkoranabuhanga (IRST) muri 1989 (UNR, ISAR, & IRST, 2000). Uretse ibyo bigo byյbushakashatsi, haje kuvuka nաmashuri makuru na Kaminuza mu Rwanda: Kaminuza Nkuru yյ Rwanda (UNR) muri 1963 nՉshuri Rikuru Nderabarezi (IPN) muri 1966. Imwe mu nshingano zաya mashuri ni ubushakashatsi bwiyongera ku kwigisha no gukora ibikorwa biteza imbere abaturage. Muri 2016, mu Rwanda habarurwaga amashuri makuru 45 arimo 35 yigenga nաndi 10 ya Leta (MINEDUC, 2016).Nյbwo hashize imyaka myinshi ubushakashatsi bukorwa ku buryo butaziguye, imbogamizi zinyuranye zatumye butagira byinshi buhindura mu mibereho yաbaturage. Raporo yakozwe ku bufatanye bwa UNR, ISAR na IRST ku miterere yյbushakashatsi mu gihugu, igaragaza ko umuco wյbushakashatsi utarashinga imizi mu Rwanda. Ibi bigaragazwa byյmwihariko nթbi bibazo byanditse muri iyo raporo, magingo aya bikaba bikigaragaza (UNR, ISAR, & IRST, 2000, p. 52): Ibyemezo byinshi bifatwa ntibishingira ku bumenyi bwizwe ku buryo bwa gihanga. Nyamara biragaragara ko isi igenda iba nkյmudugudu kandi kuyibamo bigasaba ko ibikorwa bigomba kuba bifite ikerekezo kidahubukiweho. Ubushakashatsi bukorwa usanga akenshi budakemura ibibazo bifatika byաbaturage kuko kenshi ababukora nաbagomba gukemurirwa ibibazo usanga ntaho bahurira. Nta buryo busobanutse buhari bwo kugeza ibyavuye mu bushakashatsi ku bo bugenewe kandi nթsuzuma ryabyo ntirikunda gukorwa. Abakora ubushakashatsi baracyari mbarwa. Nաbahari usanga bahora mu mahugurwa atarangira nyamara umusaruro ukaba muke.Uwavuga rero ko umuco wյbushakashatsi utarashinga imizi mu Rwanda, ntiyaba aciye inka amabere. Ibikorwa byթbigo byյbushakashatsi binyuranye, kenshi ntibitugeraho uko tubyifuza nթgihe tubyifurizaho, cyangwa ngo bitugezeho ibyo twifuza byose mu buzima bwacu bwa buri munsi. Abitwa abashakashatsi nabo, bashimishwa no kwitwa iryo zina, ariko bigahera mu magambo. Abarimu benshi ba za Kaminuza ubusanzwe baba ari nաbashakashatsi, ariko usanga akazi kabo kթbanze ari ukwigisha gusa. Abagerageza nabo, usanga akenshi atari urukundo bafitiye ubushakashatsi, ahubwo baba bagamije ikizatuma bazamurwa mu ntera mu kazi, bityo nյmushahara ukiyongera. Iyaba nabyo byakorwaga.Bimwe mu bigo byյbushakashatsi na za Kaminuza usanga nta ngengo yթmari yihariye bigenera ubushakashatsi. Nթyo ihari, usanga idahagije ndetse kenshi ugasanga ikoreshwa indi mirimo idafite aho ihuriye nյbushakashatsi. Ibi nabyo bituma umuco wյbushakashatsi utimakazwa. Nkյko twabisobanuye mbere, abarangiza Kaminuza ari nabo bagombye kuzahura umuco wյbushakashatsi kugira ngo babe ba bandebereho, usanga iyo barangije bacana ukubiri na bwo. Umuntu ntiyabibarenganyiriza, kuko akenshi usanga nթsomo ryյko ubushakashatsi bukorwa nta ngufu rihabwa, ndetse rimwe na rimwe ugasanga uryigisha nta bunararibonye mu bushakashatsi afite. Ibi bituma yigisha amahange gusa, imyitozo ikaba mike cyangwa ntinakorwe na busa. Bigaragazwa kenshi nթmishinga yյbushakashatsi ikorwa nաbanyeshuri bitegura kurangiza ikiciro cya mbere ndetse nթcya kabiri. Usanga bahuzagurika cyane, bakazumva ibyo bagombaga gukora nյko bagombaga kubikora barangije inyandiko yabo. Habamo ndetse nաbarinda barangiza nta na kimwe bumvise muri ibyo byombi, kubera gucungira gusa ku nama zաbarimu babayoboye muri ubwo bushakashatsi. Ntitwirirwa tugaruka ku ngorane abanyeshuri bagira mu guhitamo ingingo bazakoraho ubushakashatsi. Kuba bahura nթyi ngorane, umuntu yakwemeza ko baba batarigishijwe neza ngo bumve ibibazo aho biri nյko biteye. Twibutse ko iyo nta kibazo gihari, nta nյbushakashatsi bukorwa. Ubushakashatsi bubereyeho gukemura ibibazo no gutuma ubuhanga nյbumenyi bitera imbere. Hari abahuza umuco wյbushakashatsi nյmuco wo kudasoma, ukunze kuvugwa muri Afurika. Bamwe bati Ҵurandika bisomwe na nde?ӠAha ni ho bamwe bahera bavuga ngo iyo ushaka guhisha umunyafurika ikintu, uracyandika. Abandi bati Ҕurandika bigurwe na nde?ӠAha hakaziramo ikibazo cyյbushobozi. Gusa nաbabufite, usanga mu byյkuri, batitabira kugura ibyandikwa. Umuco wo kudasoma rero uzambya iterambere kuko nյbushakashatsi bukozwe butamenyekana ngo bushyirwe mu bikorwa haba mu gufata ibyemezo, nkյko twabivuze, cyangwa se kugeragezwa mu bikorwa nyirizina. Kimwe mu byafasha kwimakaza umuco wյbushakashatsi mu burezi bwյ Rwanda, ni imikoranire ya hafi kandi inoze hagati ya za Kaminuza, inzego kimwe nթbigo bya Leta ndetse nթbyաbikorera. Ibi bigo usanga byita ku byatuma Umunyarwanda arushaho gutera imbere no kumererwa neza. Kaminuza nkթsoko yյbuhanga nյbumenyi bunyuranye, zagombye kwifashishwa uko bikwiye nkյko ahandi bigenda. Imyitozo yյbushakashatsi abanyeshuri bahabwa, ikaza ikemura ibibazo byթngutu byugarije Abanyarwanda. Ibi byatuma nաbarangije kwiga bagumana umuco wo kwita ku bibazo bifatika bigaragara mu gihugu. Umwanzuro Uyu mutwe wari ugamije kwerekana isano hagati yյbushakashatsi, uririmi nյburezi. Nkյko byagaragajwe, ubushakashatsi buvumbura ubumenyi, ubumenyi bukigishwa hifashishijwe ururimi. Birakwiye rero kwimakaza umuco wյbushakashatsi mu Rwanda cyanecyane mu mashuri makuru na Kaminuza kuko ari ho inyigisho zյbushakashatsi zitangirwa. Birakwiye kandi ko habaho ubufatanye hagati yաbashakashatsi nաbaturage hakitabwa no ku rurimi bahuriyeho kuko ari rwo rwumvikanisha neza ibikenewe na rubanda rwa giseseka. Iyo urebye abagerageza gukora ubushakashatsi mu Rwanda, usanga bakunze gukoresha indimi mvamahanga cyanecyane Icyongereza nՉgifaransa. Ibyo bikorwa mu gihe mu Rwanda abaturage bagera kuri 99.4% bazi Ikinyarwanda. Ibi nabyo bituma umuco wյbushakashatsi uba umwihariko wa bamwe. Reka dusoze twibutsa ko gushyira hamwe, ari byo byubaka igihugu kuko nta mugabo umwe. Bisaba ko abantu baba bahuriye ku rurimi rumwe cyangwa ku ndimi zimwe; iyo bitabaye ibyo baba batatanya imbaraga.IndangasokoAbdelilah-Bauer, B. (2006).
