Ntitwiriwe tuvuga uruhare rwabyo mu byյbukungu nյbucuruzi bubyubakiyeho nkյbukerarugendo, gucuruza ibivabugeni binyuranye birimo inyandiko zյbuvanganzo nթbindi. Kuri ubu, abanyenganda nաbacuruzi bashaka kurema cyangwa guhindura umuco wաbaguzi, binyuze ahanini mu kwamamaza. Ubwinshi bwթmodoka, kubera ibyotsi zicucumura, bihumanya ikirere, terefone ngendanwa nյbundi buryo bwթtumanaho ryihuse byahinduye uburyo bwo gushyikirana hagati yաbantu, basigara babana ku izina gusa. Kwandarika hose amashusho yթmibonano mpuzabitsina byahinduye isura yյrugo nյmubano wաbashakanye, bituma ubutinganyi nաndi mahano bihinduka ҵmucoӮ MacDonald yinjiye mu mirire yաbatuye isi, ivuyanga ibyari umuco gakondo wabo. Ibyitwa ҵbwenge butari nturukabwonkoӠ(intelligence artificielle/artificial intelligence) byatumye imashini ihigika muntu ku murimo yakoraga, maze aho kuyigenzura ikaba ari yo imugenzura. Ibyo byose byubakiyeho igisa nՒumuco mushyaӬ bikaba ari iriba rikomeye nթnganzo yյbumenyi bidakwiye gukerenswa mu rwego rwյbushakashatsi. Umuco wisanzurira mu buvanganzo nյrurimi bwanditsemo, bisigasira iterambere3 ryաbaruvuga; byombi bikaba inzira abakora ubushakashatsi banyuramo ngo bamenye amateka, imibereho, ubuhanga byaranze abantu runaka mu gihe iki nթki. Turabisuzuma mu ngingo enye: kugaragaza ko ubuvanganzo nյbushakashatsi birangwa nյmuco wa ba nyirabyo, tuvugamo ubushakashatsi ku muco nաho umuco uhurira nյbuvanganzo. Ingingo ya kabiri ni uruhare rwթsesenguranyandiko nթjoranganzo mu bumenyi nyamuntu, tuvuga zimwe mu nzira zikoreshwa; kuko gukora ubushakashatsi ku buvanganzo bwաhantu nաbantu runaka ari ukugaragaza uruhare rwabo mu gukungahaza ubumenyi rusange bwթnyoko muntu. Iya gatatu ni ukuntu muri Afurika no mu Rwanda byյmwihariko, hakwiye guhangwa cyangwa kubyutswa umuco wյbushakashatsi, ibyo bigahuzwa kandi nթkoranabuhanga4. Abategetsi, abikorera nաbanyabwenge bakabiha agaciro, kuko ari byo pfundo ryթterambere rirambye, nkյko UNESCO idahwema kubyibutsa. Ubuvanganzo nյbushakashatsi birangwa nյmuco wa ba nyirabyoUmuntu yandika, ahanga ahereye ku byo azi, agahimbiraho ibindi. Mu rwego rwյbuvanganzo bigaragarira mu kuvuga aho inkuru ibera. Muri Afurika yթburengerazuba hakunda kuvugwamo ibitekerezo bya ba griots, bameze nkաbatekereza nաbabitswabanga bo mu Rwanda rwo hambere; hakabamo ibisa nթmigani ishingiye ku byo bemera: umuntu ashobora kuroga undi kugira ngo amurye, akihindura cyangwa agahindura undi inyamaswa nթbindi5 Ibihugu byegereye ubutayu bwa Sahara bigaruka kenshi ku bushyuhe budasanzwe buharangwa, abahishoye babura amazi, bagahorana ibikezikezi, bikanga kugera aho ari, haba ishuheri ihora ibuyereza umucanga umeze nkթnyanja, wubaka imisozi, urema imibande; hakaba na harmattan ibazanira imvura igihe kՉmpeshyi. Mu bihugu byiganjemo idini ya kiyisiramu, bagaruka ku myambarire yabo (boubou), ntibatana no kuvuga ibyաbagabo bashaka abagore benshi, abangavu bakatwa ibice bimwe byթgitsina (excision/genital mutilation). Inkuru nyinshi muri Afurika usangamo iyimukacyaro (urubyiruko rwաbahungu nաbakobwa bajya gushakira amaramuko mu migi nաkaga bahura na ko), ubukoroni nթngaruka bwabagizeho, bukaza gusimburwa nյbutegetsi bwթgitugu butuma ubwigenge na demokarasi bikomeza kuba gusa inzozi nթbindi. Biragoye kubona muri iki gihe inkuru ibera mu Burayi itavugwamo ibifasha abantu mu ngendo (ifarasi cyangwa igari rikururwa na yo, imodoka, gari ya moshi, metro) cyangwa amazina yթmihanda.Hari no kuvuga igihe inkuru ibera, haba mu rwego rwաmateka (inkuru yo mu kinyejana cya 17 si kimwe nթyo mu kinyejana cya 20), haba mu kuvuga ibihe bisanzwe bijyana nյrusimburane rwյbushyuhe nյbukonje (ubutita) kuko nko mu Burayi byigaragaza cyane kandi bikagena uko abantu bitwara, imyambarire ndetse nթmikorere. Uko abakinankuru bitwara, ibyo bavuga nubwo aba ari ibihimbano, ntihaburamo akabara gatuma umusomyi yibwira cyangwa yemera ko ibyo umubarankuru cyangwa umuhanzi avuga ari ukuri. Hari igihe bavuga ahantu akumva asanzwe ahazi, bavuga imigenzereze agasanga iri mu byo amenyereye. Icyo gihe kumva ibyo asoma no kubihuza nյkuri kwe biramworohera, agatangira kwisanisha nյmukinankuru. Iyo binyuranye nթbyo azi, na bwo bituma abyibazaho; rimwe na rimwe bikaba byatuma inkuru asoma ayikunda cyangwa ntimushimishe. Bivuga ko buri gihe ibyo umuntu asoma abihuza nթbyo azi, amenyereye, akunda cyangwa yakuriyemo. Mu bijyanye nՕbumenyi nyamuntu nթmibanire, biragoye kuvuga imiterere cyangwa imibereho yաbandi utayigereranyije nթyawe. Abanyaburayi babaye ingenzi za mbere mu kinyejana cya XVI/XVII, batangira ҫuvumburaӠutundi duce twթsi dutuyemo abantu batandukanye na bo. Inshuro nyinshi abo bandi bagiye babita ko ari inyeshyamba ҳauvagesӠkuko wenda basanze bataramenya ibyo kwambara, bagitunzwe no guhiga, bamwe ndetse bakirya inyama mbisi bakinywera nաmaraso. Batangajwe no gusanga basenga ibisozi birebire, izuba nթnyenyeri kuko bo muri ibyo bihe bari barayobotse ubukirisitu ubu butangiye kubashiramo; bakaba bagenda basubira mu byo bitaga ubupagani (gutura ibitambo byաbantu, ubupfumu bwo kuraguza imburungushure zթkirahuri, amakarita, imirongo yo mu biganza cyangwa imiterere yթbyo mu kirere). Byatumye abashakashatsi ku mibereho nթmibanire yաbantu barema amashami abiri atandukanye, bitewe nuko bavuga ibyթwabo mu bihugu bita ko byateye imbere cyangwa ibyo mu bihugu bita ibyթnyeshyamba. Ibyթwabo byitwa ҩygambanireӠ(sociologie/sociology), ibyթnyeshyamba bikitwa kumenya amatsinda yաbantu basigaye inyuma (anthropologie/anthropology), ҩcengerambga mbandamokoӠ(thnologie/ethnology), ҩsseengurambga mbandamokoӠ(thnographie/ethnography).Ubushakashatsi ku muco muri rusangeUbushakashstsi ku muco ni kimwe mu byaranze ishami ryյbumenyamuntu bwibanda ku matsinda yաbantu ngo basigaye inyuma guhera mu kinyejana cya XIX. Abagiye mu mato kureba uko hirya yթwabo hateye, bazanaga inkuru zյko basanze hifashe; bakunganirwa na raporo zաbakoroni nաbamisiyoneri. Nyuma abashakashatsi na bo bagiye bakora ingendo zo kwigerera Ҩirya iyoӠndetse bagena nթbyo bagomba kwitaho mu bushakashatsi bwabo. Muri rusange, ubumenyamuntu kwari ukwiga ibyաndi moko, ni ukuvuga abatari abanyaburayi, bahabwaga amazina anyuranye: ҰrimitifsӬ ҳauvagesӠ(Perrot, 2004), abantu bafatwa nkաbatagira umuco nթvutsabushya ңivilisationӠ(Mauss, 1950) ahanini bashaka kuvuga abantu bataramenya kwandika. Iryo shami ryյbumenyi rero rigenda rihabwa amazina anyuranye bitewe nթbyo bashyiraga imbere mu nyigo zabo, mu bihugu bitatu byթngenzi (u Bufaransa, u Bwongereza na Reta zunze ubumwe zՁmerika). Igice kimwe cyաbashakashatsi kibandaga ku kugaragaza uko abo bantu basanze ahandi bateye (isura: ibara ryյruhu, uko umutwe uteye, iminwa, izuru, umusatsi), igihagararo (indeshyo) nթbindi. Ni byo bise anthropologie physique/physical anthropology cyangwa isesengurabwoko mu Kinyarwanda. Bakabihuza no kwerekana uko ayo moko yաbantu basigaye inyuma agenda yiyuburura, atera imbere; bakabyiga bahereye ku guhinduka mu gihagararo nթsura, Ңava mu gusa nթnyamaswa (ubunyeshyamba), bakagenda basa nաbantu, bagana iterambereӮ Ni byo byiswe volutionnisme/ evolutionism nաbashakashatsi nka Frazer (1903) wize cyane ibijyanye nթmyemerere (imihango, imiziro, ibirangabwoko), avuga ko abantu babanza kugira idini gakondo, nyuma bakemera imana nyinshi mbere yo kuyoboka Imana imwe rukumbi. Yunganirwa na Taylor (1881) uvuga ko muntu abanza kurangwa nթbisa nյbupfumu cyangwa amayobera (maji), agakurikizaho kuyoboka idini mbere yo guhanga ibijyanye nյbumenyi. Morgan (1877) we yize ibyաmasano, ahereye ku Bayindiyosi bՁbayirokwa (Iroquois). Avuga ko abantu babanza kurangwa nյbunyamaswa, batunzwe no guhiga no gusoroma ibyimejeje; nyuma bakaba indwanyi nաbanyarugomo, bakiga guhinga no korora, amaherezo bakaba abantu bazima bafite ubucuruzi, inganda nյbumenyi. Ibyo kandi bigaragarira mu kugenda umuntu atera imbere mu bwenge. Uwitwa Flynn (1984) yitiriwe ikiswe ҥffet Flynn/Flynn effectӠbapimiraho ubushobozi bwյbwonko (QI), abantu bagatera imbere mu bikoresho bifashisha mu buzima bwabo bwa buri munsi, imyambarire, imirire, imihango nթmigenzo bigusha ku iyobamana ryabo, uko bashaka abagore cyangwa abagabo, uko bayobora umuryango mugari babamo; muri make uko babaho, ururimi bakoresha nթbindi. Iyo mihindagurikire yյrubumbambaga ni byo byitwa anthropologie sociale/social anthropology (reba Aug, 2010). Gusa hari nաbayita anthropologie culturelle/cultural anthropology cyangwa ңulturalisme/culturalismӮ Malinowski yakurikiranye ibyթmiterere yյmuryango mu basangwabutaka bo muri Ositarariya (1913), imigenzo (1933) nթbyթgitsina (1929) ahuriyeho na Mead (1928; 1935) witaye ku buryo imibonano mpuzabitsina ikorwa mu moko atandukanye. Inyito zյbwo bumenyi nyamuntu zigenda zitandukana rero bitewe nuko uri mu Bufaransa, Amerika cyangwa u Bwongereza; nyamara ubusanzwe ni kimwe kuko uko abantu babaho nթbibaranga bihariye, cyangwa ibibatandukanya nաbandi (umuco) udashobora kubivangura. Birerekana ko ibyo kuvuga ko iyigamuntu rireba gusa abantu cyangwa amoko atagira umuco nթterambere hari abari bamaze kubirenga, bemera ya mvugo ya Kinyarwanda igira iti: ҡgahugu umuco, akandi umucoӮ Ni byo Amselle (2005) yita ҵniversalit des cultures/cultureճ universalityӬ aho ubu hari urugamba rwo kurengera urwo runyuranyurane rwթmico (indimi, imyemerere, kwidagadura nթbindi.) rimwe na rimwe rugaragara mu gihugu kimwe cyangwa mu rubumbambaga rumwe; bikaba bizwi cyane mu Bwongereza nka ҭulticulturalismӬ mu gihe abantu bamwe mu Bufaransa ndetse na Canada iryo jambo ҭulticulturalismeӠ(Polony, 2015; Bock-Ct, 2016) ritabajyamo. Nyamara ni ngombwa ko buri wese yubaha ibyաbandi (Descola, 2005; Affergan, 1999), ntiyibwire ko ibye ari byo bizima gusa. Hari kandi abiga urubumbambaga bibanda cyane ku byյbukungu, byabyaye anthropologie conomique/economic anthropology (Dupuy, 2011 [2001]), abandi bibanda ku miterere cyangwa imyubakire yթnzego nթbyiciro byաbagize urubumbambaga, ari byo byitwa anthropologie structurale/structural anthropology, byatejwe imbere cyane na Levi-Strauss (1958) na Bourdieu (2015/16). Amashami yageze aho arasandara, inzira ziba urufaya bitewe ahanini nյko byigishwa muri za kaminuza; buri mwarimu cyangwa umushakashatsi agamije kugaragaza umwihariko we. Nka van Gennep (1909), Evan-Pritchard (1951) bibanze ku kugaragaza uko amoko yաbantu agenda ahanga ibyo akeneye, bitewe nաho bari nթgihe bagezemo; babyita Ҧonctionnalisme/functionalismӠnaho Balandier (1982) na Glucksman (1965) bashimangira ingaruka zյbukoroni nթmpinduka zabaye bitewe nuko abantu bagiye bagana ukwishyira ukizana, babyita ҡnthropologie dynamique/ dynamic anthropologyӮ Inzira zթmyigishirize rero zabaye nyinshi muri za kaminuza: mu Bufaransa (Durkheim, 1947; 1975 na Mauss, 1950), mu Budage (Weber, 1922), mu Bwongereza (Fortes, 1953) nաhandi. Umuco nյbuvanganzo muri rusangeUbuvanganzo, cyanecyane nyemvugo, ni umuyoboro ugaragarizwamo umuco wa ba nyirabwo cyangwa bukawuherekeza, kuko bugaragara nka kimwe mu biwugize. Boas (1940, p. 28) avuga ko Ҩari isano ya hafi cyane hagati yյbuvanganzo nyemvugo nթmibereho ya buri munsi yաbantu. [...]. Ibyo bishyika mu buzima, babona ko ari ingenzi, bizigaragaza mu gitekerezo cyangwa bibe imbarutso bubakiraho inkuru. Ibyinshi abantu barenguriraho imibereho yabo mu buvanganzo, uzasanga rwose biganisha ku byo bamenyereye. Byongeye kandi, uburyo bwo kubara inkuru bizerekana neza uko abantu bumva ikiza nթkibi. Ni nkյburyo ubwoko cyangwa umuryango runaka bukoresha mu kwivuga uko bari cyangwa bateyeӶ. Ibyo bemera (iyobokamana), ibyo batinya cyangwa bubaha bakabiziririza, imigenzo bagomba kubahiriza, ijyana nթmibereho cyangwa imirimo yabo ya buri munsi; nkթgihe kթhinga cyangwa isarura. Urugero ni ugutanga imbuto cyangwa ibyakorwaga igihe cyյmuganura mu mihango yյbwiru mu Rwanda. Hari kandi ibiranga ibihe byթngenzi mu mibereho ya muntu: ibyubahirizwa igihe umwana avutse cyangwa apfuye, ahabwa izina, ameze amenyo; yinjizwa mu rwego rwաbakuru, ni ukuvuga abaye umwangavu (hari aho abakobwa bakatwa imyanya imwe yթgitsina, hari aho bahonyorwa amabere) cyangwa ingimbi (bamwe bakorerwaho imihango ibamenyereza kuba umugabo, intwari ndetse bagasabwa gukora ibijyanye no kwigerezaho; ahandi bigishwa ibyթmibonano mpuzabitsina, nթbindi). Byose usanga bifite imvugo nաmagambo, imitongero, indirimbo cyangwa imbyino bibiherekeza. Ntushobora gusesengura umuco uwo ari wo wose ngo uwutandukanye nյbuvanganzo buwushamikiyeho. Umuco na wo ubona mu buvanganzo inzira wisanzuriramo, umenyekana. Nta muco ukurira mu bimenyetso cyangwa ibikorwa gusa, nta jambo ribiherekeza. Urugero nko mu Rwanda, kugangahura, gutsirika, kuvura cyangwa kuroga buri gihe hari imitongero ibiherekeza ari na yo yթngenzi (Bigirumwami, 2004). Uko kuba umuco nյbuvanganzo ari indatana, ni ho hava kwitiranya umuco na folklore (reba van Gennep, 1924). Ni ijambo ryՉcyongereza risobanura uburyo bwo kumenya cyangwa kugira ubumenyi kuri rubanda; rigizwe nթbice bibiri: folk, rubanda (abaturage) na lore (ubumenyi), inkoranya Le Petit Larousse (Cousin, Garnier, & Demay, 1999) isobanura ivuga ko ari ҵburyo bwo kugaragaza ibijyanye nյmuco byose (imyemerere, imihango cyangwa imigenzo, imigani, ibitekerezo nթbikabyankuru, imanza nթminsi mikuru cyangwa ibirori nթbindi.), byյmwihariko, ubuvanganzo nyemvugo mu rubumbambaga rwաbatarangwaho umuco wo kwandika cyangwa se abantu bo mu cyaroӷ. Ubushakashatsi ku muco wifashishije ururimi nյbushakashatsi ku rurimi binyuze mu muco, byombi birajyana; ari na ho haturutse ibyo abahanga bamwe bise sociolinguistique (Hymes, 1964), cyanecyane muri Amerika, ni ukuvuga kwiga ururimi uhereye ku baruvuga (umuco, imibereho); abandi bakabyita ethnolinguistique (Calame-Griaule, 1977), bashimangira ukuntu ҩkiri mu mvugo runaka ntawagitandukanya nթmigirire nյmuco wաbavuga urwo rurimiӸ. Ni mu rurimi rero abantu berekaniramo uko cyangwa uburyo babaho, ibyo bemera, ibigenda bihinduka cyangwa ibibatandukanya muri iyo mibereho, uko umuryango wabo wubatse; mbese ururimi ni nkթndorerwamo yյrubumbambaga, aho abantu babonera ishusho yյmuco wabo. Ni yo mpamvu Sapir (1921) na Whorf (1956) bemeza ko ҡmagambo ururimi rukoresha agaragaza imibereho mu rubumbambaga nյmuco bafiteӹ. Nguko uko usanga kwiga ibyյmuco, urubumbambaga, ubuvanganzo nյrurimi ari ihuriro ryյrujya nյruza rwթngeri zinyuranye zigusha ku bumenyamuntu, ubumenyamibanire, iyigamoko nթmiryango, babihuza nթyigandimi (linguistique/linguistics), cyanecyane agace karyo kթyiganyito (smantique/semantics). Urugero rwյrwo ruvange ni icyo bita ubu ңultural studiesӠusanga bihuza ibyo byose tumaze kuvuga, bibanda cyanecyane ku gisa no guhangana hagati yՒumuco wa rubandaӠnյbutegetsi usanga bufitwe ahanini nաbakomeye. Byavukiye mu Bwongereza muri za 1960, igihe uwitwa R. Hoggart yashingaga ikiswe Center for Contemporary Studies, nyuma bikaza kugera muri Reta zunze ubumwe zՁmerika, bakabihuza nթkiswe French Theory (ubushakashatsi mu bya firozofiya bwa ba Derrida (1967), Foucault (1966) nաbandi); mu Buhorandi bikigishwa byitwa cultural analysis cyangwa isesenguramuco guhera mu 1990.Uko kwiga umuco uranga rubanda cyangwa abaturage basanzwe mu mibereho yabo ya buri munsi, babisesengura bahereye cyanecyane ku itangazamakuru (media studies), byյmwihariko iryifashisha amashusho agaragaza nyine uko abantu babaho, uko bumva ibintu nթngaruka iryo tangazamakuru rigira ku mibereho yabo (Ang, 1990). Nko kwamamaza, amafirimi, bigira ingaruka ku myumvire nթmibereho yաbuhirwa ayo mashusho (visual studies). Abashakashatsi rero basanga abaturage aho bari, bakaganira na bo ngo bamenye icyo babitekerezaho, bagasesengura ibyandikwa. Baracengera kandi, bakagera no mu duce dutuwemo nաbakene, abashomeri, abatarize, abimukira nաbandi Ңasigaye inyumaӬ ngo bamenye imibereho yabo (Zukin, 1995); bakareba uko bagerageza kwihagararaho imbere yթterambere rishaka gusibanganya ҩkibarangaӠcyangwa gukora nkaho batariho (Mattelart & Neveu, 2003). Ubu hari ubushakashatsi bunyuranye ku ҭvugo zihariyeӠ(Messili & Ben Aziza, 2004) zikoreshwa nաbo basigaye inyuma, akenshi usanga banatuye ukwabo ahantu hadashobotse mu migi, bakagira injyana na muzika yihariye ibaranga nka pop music (Adorno, 1941; Mauch, MacCallum, Levy, na Leroi (2015), rockծղoll (Chastagner, 1998), hip hop (Colins, 2006), reggae (Dumerc, 2014), rap (Sberna, 2001), slam (Bourdieu, 1982; Petotin, 2009) nթbindi.Ku rundi ruhande, abakurikirana cultural studies usanga mu bo bavuga ko barengera atari rubanda mu buryo bwթmibereho gusa, nka bimwe bya K. Marx byo kurengera abakozi bo hasi cyangwa abakene banyunyuzwaga na ba nyiri inganda, bakaba baragombaga kwihagararaho (Roach, 1997), bakumvikanisha ijwi ryabo binyuze mu kwigaragambya (Neveu, 2002). Ibyo bifitanye isano kandi nթbyitwa Postcolonial studies (Smouts, 2007). Ahubwo muri cultural studies harimo no kwivumbura ku ndangagaciro na kirazira urubumbambaga rugenderaho. Urugero ni ishusho yյmuryango, ubusanzwe uba ugizwe nյmugabo, umugore nաbana. Imyumvire ikwirakwizwa na cultural studies irimo ҫwigobotora amabwiriza yerekeye umuryango urubumbambaga rugenderahoӺ ibyiswe ҭai 68Ӡmu Bufaransa, irengerabagore (fminisme/feminism) ribangamiye ҵbubyeyiӠbwյmugore nkյko byakwirakwijwe na de Beauvoir (1949), aho bemeza ko umubiri wյmugore afite uburenganzira bwo kuwukoresha icyo yishakiye; gushyingira abahuje igitsina bikemerwa, nkյko bikwirakwizwa na gender studies na za muvoma LGBT. Kwiga ibikoma kuri muntu nյko yagiye atera imbere, yiyungura ubwenge, ahanga ibishya; ibyo ukabisesengura uhereye ku ndimi, imitekerereze nթmikorere ye, aho aba nթbindi, Abanyaburayi ni bo ba mbere bakoze ubushakashatsi ku banyafurika nաndi moko, rimwe na rimwe bakabigoreka (Asante, 2003). Bivuga ko abo banyafurika bagomba gukora ubwabo ubushakashatsi ku mico nթmibereho yabo ngo bakosore ibyo abo bazungu bavuze nabi; bapfa nanone kutagwa mu mutego wo kwitaka no kwishimagiza, nta mpamvu. Uruhare rwթsesenguranyandiko nթjoranganzo Nkյko twabonye ko ubuvanganzo bufitanye isano ya hafi nյrubumbambaga bwavukiyemo cyangwa bugenewe, habaye impaka nyinshi ku buryo ijoranganzo rikwiye gukora, bamwe bashaka kugaragaza isano iri hagati yթbivugwa mu nyandiko nթbyaranze urubumbambaga umwanditsi yabayemo, ubuzima bwe; abandi bashaka kwibanda ku nyandiko gusa, nta kuyitiranya na nyirayo, bakayisesengura mu buryo Ңwa gihangaӠaho kuba ҡmarangamutimaӮ Nyamara nաbahisemo ubwo buryo bwa gihanga, ikigomba kwitabwaho ntibakivugaho rumwe: hari abashyira imbere ibarankuru (umugendo wթnkuru, imivugano, kujya imbu kwաbakinankuru mu bikorwa byabo nթbindi), abandi bakibanda ku kivugwa (ingingo nթbitekerezo), gucukumbura ibitekerezo byihishe byաbakinankuru, abandi bakimika ibyյkuntu inyandiko yakiriwe nաbasomyi (gusomwa, gukundwa no kugurishwa, kujorwa) nթcyo igomba kungura umusomyi mu rwego rwթmibereho na poritiki. Abandi bagasesengura bibanda ku hantu havugwa mu nkuru, bagerageza gusobanura impamvu havugwa, uko havugwa, nթbindi. Izo nzira zose turazivugaho muri make ariko duhamya ko nta nzira kamara, kuko inyandiko ni insobe, ni uruhurirane rwթbyo byose, ku buryo nյmusesenguzi nta cyo yagombye gutonesha cyangwa gusuzugura. Urusobe rwթsesengurirambagaIsesengurirambaga ryita icyarimwe ku kiri mu nyandiko imbere nթbituruka hanze yayo, ni ukuvuga inyandiko ubwayo nթbitayirimo cyangwa ibitayigize ariko bifitanye isano na yo (igihe, ahantu, uko yakozwe). Si ugushakisha imyumvire yյmwanditsi cyangwa gusesengura ibyo ahoza mu kanwa (bisa nթbyamusajije) nkյko tubisanga kwa Bachelard (1942; 1946) cyangwa Durand (1963); si no gusesengura ingengabitekerezo yiganje, nkյko byakozwe na Adorno (2011), Marx 2008 [1859]), Goldmann (1967). Hari isano ya hafi urubumbambaga rufitanye nյbuvanganzo. Imvugo yabaye umugani ngo ҵbuvanganzo ni indorerwamo yյrubumbambagaӠyigaragaza buri munsi kubera ko umwanditsi, mu guhanga kwe no kuranga indi si yiremera ari yo yաbakinankuru be, abo bakinankuru ashobora kubarema ahereye ku bigaragara mu rubumbambaga nաmateka nyayo umuhanzi ubwe yabayemo. Ni cyo gitera Hbert (2001, p. 13) kuvuga ko ҩnyandiko twayifata nkթshusho yյrubumbambaga byitwa ko yerekana, ikimenyetso cyյrubumbambaga yavukiyemo cyangwaɠikirango cyakorewe kandi kigakorwa nյrwo rubumbambagaӱ0 Isesengurirambaga rero ni uruhurirane rwթnzira nյburyo bunyuranye bwo gusesengura inyandiko nkյko tubisanga no mu guhuza ururimi, umuco nյrubumbambaga (ethnolinguistique/ethnolinguistics), isesengurajambo (analyse du discours/discourse analysis) cyangwa isesenguramvugo (pragmatique/pragmatics). Ni iyo mpuzaburyo bwթsesengura ijyana nյbwinshi bwթnzira zo gusoma no kumva inyandiko bugize ipfundo ryթmiyobora (thorie/theory) ya Cros (2003), iyo avuga ngo nta Ңuryo budasubirwaho, rukumbi, ngenderwaho bwo gusomamo cyangwa kumva inyandikoӻ kubera ko iyo usoma inyandiko, uba uri imbere yյruhuri rwթnyito zinyuranye kandi zihindagurika aho kuba igisobanuro ndakuka. Mu nyandiko rero idanaze cyangwa iboshye butambaro, Cros (2000, p. 54) asangamo ҵtuyira tuganisha ku bisobanuro binyuranye ndetse bivuguruzanya, hakaba aho usanga nta kintu gihari, ibisa nյtwobo, ahandi hakaba utuyira twյbusamoӱ1. Twe dusanga ahubwo inyandiko ntawushobora kuyumva cyangwa kuyicengera ngo ayiheze, bitewe nuko yigiramo bimwe abanyabugenge bita ҩbiyoongobezarumuriӠ(trous noirs/black holes), biyongobeza ibisobanuro; maze hakaba amabanga yթnyandiko atazigera amenyekana. Bivuga ko, mu byյkuri, ibyo umusomyi (aba-) ashobora gushyikira nkթgisobanuro, ari nkաkamuri gake karokotse wa mwobo ucuze uburindi. Iyo myobo tuvuga hano, irimo imyumvire byitwa ko igendanye nթgihe, usanga yemera ko ibintu bisomwa cyangwa bikumvwa mu murongo runaka; wabyumva ukundi ugateshwa agaciro. Urugero ni ukuntu ikitwa ҵburenganziraӠcyumvwa muri iki kinyejana cya XX-XXI; nkթyo bavuga uburenganzira bwթgitsina gore byabyaye ҧuhakana ubugoreӬ kwigarama ububyeyi, kuvanamo inda, kubana kwաbahuje igitsina, kwihinduza igitsina nթbindi; uburenganzira bwo gufasha umuntu kwiyahura cyangwa ukamunogonora. Iyo nshoza kandi inahindagurika bitewe nթbyo abafite ingufu bifuza. Muri iki gihe abaherwe, abanyenganda nաbanyemari bashaka kwikubira ubukungu bwթsi, bagenda bakuraho uburenganzira bwաbakozi (umushahara ukwiye, ikiruhuko, kudapfa kwirukanwa nթbindi); byahindutse Үtawuburana nյmuhambaӮ Undi mwobo ni igihe, kubera ko hari inyito nթbisobanuro bigenda bitakara cyangwa biteshwa agaciro uko imyaka igenda ihita. Urugero ni ҵkuriӠkuko ubu bavuga ko nta kuri guhuriweho na bose kubaho, buri wese afite ukuri kwe, agakora icyo yumva kimubereye atitaye ku byաbandi. Hari kandi umuco cyangwa gushaka gusanisha icyo ubwiwe, ikivuye ahandi (nkթndangagaciro) nյmuco wawe, ngo ukigire icyawe ҩnculturationӮ Gusa iyo myobo ni ingenzi cyane kuko yifitemo ҡkamuriӬ igatuma abasesenguzi bagira ishyaka ryo gushakashaka, bakimba ubutarambirwa nkաbacukura mu kirombe ngo bavumbure cyangwa bacengere ibanga rihishe mu magambo kugeza ku kitso nաkaninuriro Ұoint dթronie/irony markӠ(Jobard, 1842); amaherezo bagashirwa bateye muri ka kobo intanga nyito ҳpermesanӠyabo, ngo inyandiko irusheho kurumbuka.Isesengurantego cyangwa isesenguramisusire ryifashisha amahame yթyigandimi mu gusesengura inyandiko. Ryatangijwe na Jakobson (1973) na bagenzi be barimo Troubetzkoy, bari bagize ҃ercle linguistique de MoscouӠmu Burusiya mu myaka ya 1920; nyuma yimukiye i Prague byitwa ҃ercle linguistique de PragueӮ Kuri bo, ubuvanganzo nubwo bufite ikiburanga kihariye, ariko bushingiye mbere na mbere ku mvugo; ari na yo mpamvu, mu isesengura, inyandiko nyirizina ari yo igomba kwitabwaho yonyine; aho kureba igihe, ahantu, amateka, impamvu byaranze abayikoze. Ku basesenguramisusire (formalistes/formalists), inyandiko mvanganzo irihagije, ni yo mpamvu igomba kwigwa cyangwa gusesengurwa bagendeye ku biyigaragaramo nyabugeni, aho kugendera ku biri hanze yayo. Ni cyo gitera Jakobson (1977, p. 16) kuvuga ngo ҩcyo ubuhanga busesengura inyandiko bugomba kwiga si ubuvanganzo, ahubwo ni ҩkiranganganzoӠ(Ҭiteraturnostө, ni ukuvuga igituma inyandiko iba inyandiko mvanganzo12. Uko gushaka kwiga inyandiko ku buryo bwa gihanga, ureba cyanecyane igituma inyandiko runaka yitwa ubuvanganzo nyabugeni, usanga bikora gusa ku nyandiko ya gisizi aho usanga injyana, amahuza, isubirajwi bizana inshurango mu nyandiko, bigatuma yitandukanya nթmvugo isanzwe, tutibagiwe no kuzimiza ukoresheje ishushanyamvugo. Iyo ugerageje gukoresha ubwo buryo ku nyandiko itari iya gisizi, bigusaba kureba uburyo ikivugwa cyangwa inkuru ҦabulaӠyabazwe, bikayiha imisusire nyabugeni ngo bibyare inyandiko yյbuvanganzo. Ni aha usanga ubu buryo buhurira cyane no gusesengura ibarankuru Үarratologie/narratologyӠbyazanywe na Genette muri za 1966. Abacengeranganzo batwawe nթyigandimi rigezweho, bagiye kurivomamo ibikoresho, ibitekerezo nթnzira kugira ngo bavugurure ijoranganzo. Kugeza ubwo ijoranganzo barigira rimwe mu mashami yթyigandimi: ni iyigandimi ryթmvugo rishingiye ku kivugwaho aho gushingira ku nyumve nթnyumvisho. Ni ryo ryabyaye ikeshamvugo, izimburanganzo nթyigabimenyetso.Inshoza yթnsobeke ҳtructureӠimaze imyaka irenga 30 ihindagurika (uje wese abonamo umwanya akayikoresha uko yishakiye). Ubundi insobeke ni ҵrujyaanoӠ(systme/system) rukora rukurikije amategeko yյbwuzuzwe (ikintu kirangiye), ubwuzuzanye nյbufatanye (ikintu kigira icyo gikora ku kindi), kwibogora (ibintu bikisubiza mu mwanya) no guhinduka (ikintu kitari intayega), uburutanwe nյkwigumamo ҩmmanenceӠ(ikintu kikagirwa nաmategeko yacyo bwite). Ikթngenzi mu nsobeke, si akantu kamwe ukwako cyangwa se kureba byose icyarimwe, ahubwo ni amasano ingingo zifitanye. Niba ururimi rugaragara nkյrujyano, ingingo zirugize nta buzima bwite zifitemo. Inyito cyangwa agaciro kazo gashingiye ku mikoreshereze yazo mu rujyano; mu masano izo ngingo zifitanye hagati yazo, mu mumaro nյmwanya zifite mu rujyano. Mu kurondora injyano zթbimenyetso, de Saussure (1995[1916]) ntiyigeze arengurira ku rujyano rwթbimenyetso mvanganzo. Ashingira urujyano ku rurimi, atari ku ijambo (igikorwa cyյmuntu ubwe). Isesengurarurimi rihera ku ndanguruzi ya Jakobson (1963, pp. 209 Р222) yerekeye ubwumvane, rigerageza gushakamo ya mimaro itandatu ndangamvugo. Mu nyandiko ushobora kubonamo imimaro myinshi icyarimwe, ariko ni ngombwa kureba uwiganje kurusha iyindi. Bityo nko mu gisigo, umumaro uganje ni ҮgnamvgoӠ(fonction potique/poetic function), mu nkuru ndende higanje umumaro ҮyrekezoӠ(fonction rfrentielle/referential function) kubera ko inkuru ndende yerekeza ku isi baranga. No mu ndondore higanje umumaro ҮyakubwiirwaӠ(fonction conative/conative function) na nyerekezo. Umuntu yavuga ko amashuri yթbyթcengeranganzo, mu kinyejana cya 20, yasaga nաkomeza kuzenguruka atabizi kuri iyo ndanguruzi13. Ijoranganzo rya kera (mbere ya 1920) ryibandaga ahanini ku mumaro nyakuvuga, ni ukuvuga ko ryitaga ku muhanzi, ubuzima nթmibereho ye nյburyo bwe bwo kubona isi. Ryitaga no ku mumaro nyerekezo (imfutuzi, isi yagaragajwe, ingingo zijyanye nյbuzima nթmibanire cyangwa imibereho, izijyanye nյburyo bwo kubona no kumva ibintu, izijyanye na poritiki nթbindi). Hagati ya 1920 na 1940, cyanecyane muri Amerika, havutse icyo bise ijoranganzo rishya Үew criticismӠryashyize imbere umumaro ngenamvugo.Jakobson (1963, pp. 43 Р67) azanamo nթzindi nshoza nko ҫubyarwaӠno ҫugenderaӮ Iryo gendera rifite umwanya mu myubakire yթnyandiko, aho usanga ibyanditswe mbere [muri iyo nyandiko ku mapaji abanza cyangwa izayibanjirije] bisa nթbiyobora ibiza kwandikwa, rikagira nյruhare mu buryo iyo nyandiko isomwamo (yumvikana). Gusoma bishingiye ku ҩfindaӠ(codification), tuvuge ryթkivugwamo cyangwa ingingo; nyuma hakaba hari irindi finda ҲiriyoboraӠkubera ko ririhatira cyangwa rikarihinyuza bitewe nթzindi mfindo zirimo14 (Bergez et al., 1990, p. 195). Spitzer (1970) mu gitabo yise Etudes de style (1970, p. 368) avuga ko ҩsesenguramisusire atari ukwita ku miterere yթnyuma yթnyandiko ngo wirengagize icyo ihatse, nta cyo byaba bivuze ? ahubwo ni ugufata ikivugwa ubwacyo nkթmisusire isharaze mu rujyano rwթkiriho... Ikթngenzi hano, ni uruhare rwթmiterere mu ԫubaka ikivugwaՓ15. Cros (2003, p. 35) aribaza ati: Ҏi gute kundi umuhanzi wթnyandiko yamenya ukuri kwթbintu atabayemo, nyamara agenda yinjiramo, atari ukuvuga ibyo abayemo icyo gihe yandika cyangwa se agahera ku gutekereza no gusesenguraӿ16Genette (1976[1969], p. 17) muri Figures II, asaba ҧufata igihangano nyandiko cyose, cyangwa agace kacyo, mbere na mbere nkթnyandiko, ni ukuvuga urudanage rwաmashusho mvugo, aho igihe, (cyangwa nkյko bikunda kuvugwa, ubuzima) bwյmwanditsi wandika nյbwյmusomyi usoma byifatanya, bikibohabohanaho ku rupapuro nթgitabo cyoseӱ7Mu ibarankuru, bareba ҡbakrabkorwӠ(actants) kuko umukinankuru arangwa ahanini nթbyo akora mu nkuru. Ni ho haturutse igishushanyo ngaragazabikorwa (schma actanciel/actantial model) cya Greimas kigaragaza uburyo umunyarubuga asabwa nյmugenera gushakisha intego agirira cyangwa ku nyungu zյmugenerwa. Ibyo akabifashwamo nաbunganizi ariko hakaba nաbamwitambika imbere ngo atabigeraho ari bo ba kidobya cyangwa abamurwanya. Ibarankuru kandi ryita ku mubarankuru nyirizina ryiga icyo twise ҩreeberoӬ Genette (1983, p. 9) yita Ұoint de vue/point of viewӮ Ashobora kuba ҲumnyabyoseӠ(omniscient), aba azi byinshi kurusha abakinankuru, bikitwa ko arebera kure (focalisation zero/zero focalisation). Ibi ni byo bikunda kugaragara mu nkuru nyinshi, zaba ndende cyangwa ngufi; aho usanga ahanini ibarwa muri ngenga ya gatatu. Tutibagiwe ko mu nkuru imwe ababarankuru bashobora kuba barenze umwe. Ashobora no kuba azi ibingana nաbakinankuru, akitwa ko arebera imbere mu nkuru (focalisation interne/internal focalization). Ibi tubisanga ahanini mu nkuru zibazwe muri ngenga ya mbere, igihe umubarankuru ari nյmukinankuru. Umubarankuru ashobora kandi kuba azi bike ku bakinankuru bikitwa ko arebera inyuma (focalisation externe/external focalisation). Ibi biba igihe abakinankuru ibyinshi ari bo babyivugira, umubarankuru agasa nյgenda yuzuriza binyuze mu bisa nթntekerezo. Ababarankuru rero bari kwinshi. Ashobora kubara inkuru adakinamo akitwa Ҩtrodigtique/heterodiegeticӠcyangwa ҵmubzi w haanzӻ ni na byo bikunze kugaragara mu nkuru ndende nթngufi. Ashobora kubara inkuru akinamo akitwa Ҩomodigtique/homodiegeticӠcyangwa ҵmubzi w muu mbereӠnkյko ashobora kubara inkuru akinamo ari na we munyarubuga akitwa ҡutodigtique/autodiegeticӠcyangwa ҵmumenyabaangaӮ Uyu mubazi kandi ashobora kubara ibintu byahise, icyo gihe ibarankuru ryitwa ҵltrieure/subsequentӠcyangwa ҩriizanyumaӮIbarankuru rishobora kuvuga ibitaraba, rikitwa ҡntrieure/anteriorӠcyangwa ҭbaanzirizaӮ Hari nթgihe ariko ribara ibiriho biba icyo gihe ngo rikitwa ҳimultane/simultaneousӠcyangwa ҭpuuriranaӮ Ibi bigaragara nkթgihe abanyamakuru babwira cyangwa bereka ababakurikiye inkuru nաmashusho yթbibera ahantu runaka ako kanya (kogeza umupira, gukurikirana ibirori cyangwa indi mihango). Ibarankuru kandi rigendera ku rwego ibivugwa biriho. Hari inkuru nyirizina cyangwa nyamukuru. Igihe ari yo ibarwa, ibarankuru rizitwa ҩntradigtique/ intradiegeticӠcyangwa ҭuu nda yՒnkurӮ Ni byo bikunze kugaragara henshi. Rishobora kubara ibitajyanye nթnkuru nyirizina, bikitwa ҥxtradigtique/ extradiegeticӠcyangwa Ҩaanz yՒnkurӮ Bashobora no kubara ikiri intekerezo ku nkuru nyirizina bikitwa ҭtadigtique/metadiegeticӠcyangwa ҭbandankruӮ Ibi byose tuvuze ku ibarankuru ni byo bigize icyo Genette (1972, p. 252) yita Ҭa voix/the voiceӠ(ijwi) ryյmubarankuru. Genette yagendeye kandi ku mimaro yashyizwe ahagaragara na Jakobson (1963) avuga ko umubarankuru ashobora kugira imimaro ikurikira: narrative cyangwa rubariro, rgie/controlled cyangwa ҭbnezankruӬ agenda agaragaza ibice bikuru byayo nյko igenda itera imbere; umumaro ҮyabwumvaneӠcyangwa Ҥe communication/communicationalӠmu kugaragaza uruhare rwյmugenerwa, umumaro ҲuhamyӠcyangwa Ҵestimonial ~ dաttestation/testimonial ~ proof funtionӬ umubazi agaragaza isano ye nթnkuru abara; hakaba nյmumaro ҮtekerezoӠcyangwa ҩdologique/ideologicalӠurangwa no gutanga ibisobanuro cyangwa kuvuga uko abona ibintu. Muri iri sesengura kandi biga ibijyanye nթgihe biranga ahanini isano hagati yթgihe ibivugwa byabereye koko ukurikije inyurabwenge nթgihe bibera ukurikije uko bivugwa mu nkuru, ukagenda ureba uko bikurikirana (ordre/succession), igihe bimara (dure/duration) nթnshuro bigarukwaho (frquence/frequency). Ku bijyanye nյko bikurikirana, ugenda ureba ibyabaye byթngenzi, ukabishyira ku murongo wifashishije inyuguti nkuru za ҡbacadaӠabandi bita alphabet; hanyuma zikunganirwa nթmibarwa igaragaza uko bikurikirana mu nkuru ibarwa. Inyuguti uzishyira ku gishushanyo uhereye kuri A ugana kuri Z; imibarwa yo ugahera ibumoso ugana iburyo uhereye kuri rimwe (1). Uko ugenda ubihuza biguha ifoto yթmiterere yթnkuru, niba hari aho basubira inyuma (analepses/analepsis), niba hari ibivugwa mbere yuko bishyika (prolepses/prolepsis) nթbindi. Ku birebana nթnshuro, umubarankuru ashobora kubara rimwe ikintu cyabaye rimwe, ashobora kubara inshuro imwe icyabaye kenshi; cyangwa kubara inshuro nyinshi icyabaye kenshi cyangwa inshuro nyinshi icyabaye rimwe. Iyo mu kubara inkuru hajemo ҵkuraangaӠ(description/digression) byitwa ҰauseӠcyangwa ҡkaruhuukoӬ hakaba nթcyo twita ҡkabariroӠ(scne/scene) ari byo gutinda amaso uyahanze ku kintu kiri kuba, abo ubwira bagasa nաbakirebera igihe kimwe nawe. ғommaire/summaryӠcyangwa ҩmpinӠiba igihe ibintu washobora kuvuga mu magambo arambuye kandi wenda bimara igihe kirekire (iminsi, ibyumweru, amezi, imyaka) ubivuga mu nteruro cyangwa igika kimwe gusa aho kurambura. Usesengura areba nթbyo umwanditsi asimbuka bita ҥllipse/ellipsisӠcyangwa kwirengagiza, ҩrkanknaӠiyo urebye umugendo rusange wթbikorwa uko byagombye gukurikirana (Genette, 1972, p. 129). Ikindi bitaho muri ubu buryo ni ukureba niba igikorwa kiri mu nyandiko kivugwa ku buryo buziguye ari bwo bwթbarankuru (diegesis), bukoreshwa ahanini mu nkuru ndende na ngufi cyangwa butaziguye ari bwo mimesis nko mu ikinamico. Tutibagiwe ko mu nkuru ndende nթngufi bashobora kubivanga ariko nta kurenza igipimo. Icyo gihe unareberaho igihe inshinga zitondaguwemo. Ni indagihe isanzwe, ni impitagihe, ni indagihe yթbarankuru, ni imbundo; ukagerageza no gushaka impamvu aha nաha byakoreshejwe bityo. Ahandi ureba umurongo umubarankuru ahitamo, wita nko ku tuntu wakwita duto ariko ukabona atwibandaho cyangwa adutsindagira, hakagira nթbyo anyereraho gusa cyangwa yirengagiza, ugashaka impamvu. Aha ni ho haturuka kuvuga ko umusomyi afatanya nյmuhanzi kwandika inkuru. Isesenguransobeke 	ryunganirwa 	nՒiseseengurabimenyeetsoӠ	cyangwa ҩsseenguramrengaӠҳmiotique/semioticsӠbabihuza nթbigaragara mu mikorere, mu mico, imyumvire ya ba nyiri ubuvanganzo cyangwa abavugwa mu nyandiko. Bikorwa basesengura amagambo mu bigize inyito zayo ҡnalyse smique/semic analysisӬ noneho uko bikorerwa buri jambo bikaba ari byo bikugeza ku gisobanuro rusange kթnyandiko yose. Ibi ariko bisa nթnzozi kuko bishoboka ku kandiko kagufi cyane gusa. Kuko ҩndmanytoӠ(smes/semes) ugomba kubanza kuzihuriza mu ҭbonezangiingoӠ(classmes/classemes), bikakugeza ku magambo (lexmes/lexemes) afite icyo ahuriyeho naho yaba atandukanye mu nyito. Ibi na byo bikakugeza ku mirongo migari yթnsobanuro ziri mu nyandiko, za classmes zikaguha ҩnyto mpamӠ(isotopies/isotopia), bityo bityo. Ibi birenda gusa nթbyo dusangana abitwa Groupe  (1982) yթ Lige mu cyo bise nouvelle rhtorique (Perelman & Olbrechts-Tyteca, 1958) cyangwa inozamvugo rishyashya, rishingiye kuri elocutio (uburyo bwo kuvuga) basesengura ibijyanye nթmivugo cyangwa imizimizo biremye ishushanyamvugo.Ikindi nuko Greimas avuga ko hari inyito mpame zitagaragara ariko zihari, noneho akabangikanya ukuhaba nթmvuguruza bibyara igisobanuro cyuzuzanya. Ni byo yahurije mu gishushanyo kitwa ҭpandeny ntanganytoӠңarr smiotique/ semiotic squareӮ Biragoye ariko kubikoresha nko mu nkuru ndende yose, bisaba gukora ibishushanyo byinshi ugaragaza ingingo zitandukanye.Isesengurirambaga rero ritandukanye no kureba umwanya wյbuvanganzo mu rubumbambaga byakorwaga mbere uhereye ku cyo rigamije, atari gusa kubera ko ryibanda ku buvanganzo risesengura inyandiko, ahubwo kubera ko ikirishishikaje muri ibyo ? binyuranye nթbyo gusesengura imibereho nթmibanire yաbantu ?, ari ikiri imbere mu nyandiko, ni ukuvuga ҵko inyandiko ubwazo zubatse, imikorere yazo nթcyo zihatse, umurego urimo, uruhurirane usangamo rwյbumenyi nթmvugo bitandukanyeӠ(Cros, 2003, p. 37). Iryo sesengura, byitwa ko rireba gusa inyandiko nyirizina cyangwa icyo ihatse, igituma yitwa mvanganzo. Ababyumva gutyo bahamya ko Үiba usanze mu gihangano mvanganzo ibijyanye nթndangagaciro zյrubumbambaga, ibiranga imibereho, uko imyumvire yagiye ihindagurika mu mateka nաho abantu bari nթbindi, ibyo byose birahinduka; umwanditsi agasa nյbisenya ngo yongere abihuze mu buryo bwe; bimwe akabyimura, ibyari ukuri kwաmateka cyangwa ingengabitekerezo akabiha igisobanuro gishya, noneho bikabyara umwihariko, ҵbwigire bwթnyandikoӠcyangwa ibyo Cros yita ҩndangagaciro nyirizina zթgihanganoӱ8Nyamara ni ngombwa guhuza inyandiko mvanganzo nյrubumbambaga ikomokamo ku bijyanye nթmvugo ikoreshwa. Kubera ko ҩmyumvire cyangwa ibitekerezo byagaragajwe nյmusesenguzi akenshi aba ari imvugo ye nթbitekerezo bye bwite kurusha uko ari ibiri mu nyandiko yasesenguweӱ9 (Muka?ovsk?, bivugwa na Zima, 2000, p. 139). Ni yo mpamvu ҂akhtine inyandiko ayinjiza mu mateka nյrubumbambaga abona ko na byo ari inyandiko umwanditsi asoma kandi yibonamo azandikaӲ0 (Kristeva, 1969, p. 144).Guhuza ubuvanganzo nյrubumbambaga kandi ni ҵkureba uko inyandiko yakiriwe (ibikorwa byose ngo igere ku basomyi, ikigero yasomwemo cyangwa uburyo yitabiriwe), ubihuza nյko abayakiriye bamerewe, babayeho, ibyo bakunda nթbibabangamiye nթbindi. [ɝ. Mbese ni ukureba uruhare rwթgitabo mu buzima bwյrubumbambaga nթbijyanye nյbukunguӲ1 (Zima, 2000, p. 213). Ku bwa Goldmann (1964, p. 338), ҩnyandiko ihabwa igisobanuro gishya kiberanye nթbyubahirizwa nթndangagaciro byյrubumbambaga rwayakiriyeӲ2. Ni yo mpamvu Muka?ovsk? na Vodi?ka bavuga ko ҩgisobanuro mvanganzo gihora gitegerejwe, urugendo mpuzanyandiko ruhuza igihe nյko inyandiko runaka yakozwe nթgihe nյko yakiriweӲ3 (bisubirwamo na Zima, 2000, p. 213). Isesengurangingo Ni uburyo bwatejwe imbere cyane nաbantu nka Richard (1964), Starobinski (1970), Poulet (1967[1971]), Rousset (1954), bagendeye ku ҩygamtekererezeӠ(psychanalyse/psychoanalysis). Bamwe barigaya ҫutita ku miterere yթnyandikoӬ ntirigendere ku bintu bifatika, bigaragara (Genette, 1966, pp. 91 Р100). Abarishyigikiye bemeza ko ikivugwa cyangwa ingingo ziri mu nyandiko ari ҩnzoziӠcyangwa ҩndotoӠzյmuhanzi (Bachelard, 1938, 1942, 1943, 1946), wiremera isi ye, akayirota; ari ho hava nyine guhanga (kurotora). Uwitwa Poulet abyita ңogitoӠ(urutekerezo, ikiyumviiro) yյmuhanzi. Uko kwitekerereza isanzure cyangwa isi yihariye, ahereye ku buryo yiyumva ubwe mbere yo gusingira ibimukikije, ni byo bibyara ingingo. Ikarangwa (zi-) mbere na mbere no kugaruka kenshi mu nyandiko imwe cyangwa nyinshi, zaba izյmuhanzi umwe cyangwa abahanzi batandukanye; baba baturuka hamwe (akarere, igihugu) cyangwa barabayeho mu gihe kimwe, baba se batandukanye (ahantu, igihe nաmateka). Nyamara nta ngingo ibaho gutyo gusa, itagendeye ku miterere yթnyandiko. Smekens (1987, p. 68) avuga ko ingingo ari ҡkarango (nyamisusire) kթgihangano cyյmwanditsi runaka cyangwa se izindi nyandiko izo ari zo zose. Ni byo Hjemslev (1971, p. 70) yita ҩmisusire yթkivugwaӠahuriyeho nաbandi nka Meschonnic (1970), basobanura ko ntawushobora gusesengura ingingo cyagwa ikivugwa mu nyandiko abitandukanya nթmisusire cyangwa imyandikire. Ingingo zisobanura impamvu umwanditsi yahisemo kwandika muri ubu buryo (kuzimiza nթshushanyamvugo, amagambo yakoreshejwe, ibihe byթnshinga, kuranga nթbindi.) aho gukoresha buriya; imyandikire na yo ikaberana nyine nթkivugwa. Bitandukanye nթjoranganzo rishingiye ku mateka cyangwa ubuzima bwյmuhanzi abitwa ba Sainte-Beuve bakoraga, igihe yemezaga ko ҩnkomoko ? nթgisobanuro ? kթgihangano nyandiko kiri mu mibereho yյmuntu wagihanze, wacyanditseӠ(Proust, 1954, p. 220)24. Hari abatandukanya ingingo Ҵhme/themeӠnթgitekerezo ҭotif/motivationӬ basa nաberekana ko igitekerezo cyagutse kandi kitagusha ku bifatika cyangwa ibigaragara, mu gihe ingingo ari agace cyangwa uburyo bwo gufutura kurushaho igitekerezo (Ducrot & Todorov, 1972, pp. 283 Р285). Gusesengura ikivugwa mu nyandiko mvanganzo cyangwa isesengurangingo bifitanye isano nյko inyandiko yakirwa nյrubumbambaga cyangwa umusomyi. Abatangije ibyiswe ҵmuyobora wՒyakiiranyandikoӠ(thorie de la rception/ theory of reception) bagendeye ku bitekerezo byաbanyafirozofiya nka Gadamer (1996) mu buryo bwo kumva ibintu, gushaka igisobanuro uhereye ku bisanzwe bizwi (hermneutique/hermeneutics) hamwe no kugaragaza uko wumva cyangwa ubona ibintu/isi, ibigukikije (phnomnologie/phenomenology) bakunze kwitirira umudage Husserl (1950). Kwiga ibyթyakiranyandiko rero byaje kwitirirwa abarimu bo muri kaminuza ya Constance mu 1967; usanga ari uruvange rwթndi miyoboro yabanje nkթsesenguramatwara rya K. Marx kubera ko rigusha ku mibereho, ibijyanye nյburezi nթbindi byյmuhanzi nյmusomyi. Abagendera ku matwara ya K. Marx bahamya ko abasomyi baramutse bahawe ibikoresho bimwe nյbushobozi bungana, inyandiko iyo ari yo yose bayumva kimwe. Ngo mu nyandiko haba harimo ҩgisobanuro gihisheӠumusomyi usesengura agomba gutahura. Icyo gisobanuro bakerekeza cyanecyane ku buryo urubumbambaga rutuma habaho inyandiko ivuga cyangwa igiye mu murongo uyu nյyu; nkյko nթnyandiko na zo zigira uruhare mu guhindura isura yյrubumbambaga. Ni byo bituma Sartre (1947) yibaza uwo umuhanzi agenera inyandiko ye igihe yandika; agashimangira ko ari umwanditsi, ari umusomyi, bagomba kugira uruhare rugaragara muri poritiki; ni ukuvuga guharanira guhindura ibintu mu rubumbambaga. Jauss (1978) na Iser (1985) ni bo bagerageza kubivugurura berekana ko abantu badashobora kumva inyandiko kimwe cyangwa ngo bayishime/bayinenge ku buryo bumwe. Iser ahuza na Cros twabonye haruguru mu kuvuga ko mu nyandiko habamo uduce tutanditseho, utwobo umusomyi agenewe kuzuza cyangwa gutaba ngo yumve neza ukuntu ibiri ku rupapuro byuzuzanya; bitabujije ko inyandiko ubwayo isa nթyobora umusomyi mu buryo agomba kuyisoma no kuyumva. Hari igisobanuro ikongorera cyangwa igutungira agatoki, ariko amaherezo ukihitiramo ikikubereye. Barthes (1973) we yibanda ku munezero umusomyi akura mu gusoma inyandiko runaka. Araruhuka, agatwarwa, akishima ariko akanakoresha ubwonko. Inyandiko zinezeza ngo ni izigoye kumva, umusomyi akaba agomba ԫwiremeraӠigisobanuro; ngo zituma atekereza ku ҭayobera ya kamere muntuӮ Uko gushyushya ubwonko Umberto Eco abyerekeza ku gushakisha inyito nթbisobanuro byաmagambo nթmvugo umwanditsi yakoresheje, mu nkoranya nթntango zթbisobanuro birambuye (encyclopdie/encyclopedia); nuko umusomyi akimena umutwe, agashakisha, akavumbura binyuze mu gusigura. Ibyo bikamuha kwishima kuko nyine hari icyo yagezeho.Bakhtine (1978) avuga ahanini ku kiganiro kiba hagati yյmwanditsi nյmusomyi kiyongera ku kiba hagati yյmwanditsi nաbakinankuru ndetse nաbakinankuru hagati yabo (dialogisme/dialogism). Umusomyi rero ni we utuma iryo ҨuzamjwiӠ(polyphonie/polyphony) rijya ahagaragara. Bifite aho bihurira nթsesengurangingo ndetse nթsesengurirambaga, kuko abթ Constance bemezaga ko inyandiko itagira uburyo bumwe rukumbi yumvikanamo. Bizaterwa nյmwuka uranga ahantu, igihe umusomyi arimo nյko amerewe igihe asoma kimwe nյmwanditsi ubwe nթbyo umusomyi amuziho. Inyandiko yյmwanditsi wթcyatwa, ukomeye, wabonye ibihembo mpuzamahanga, bigisha mu mashuri na za kaminuza; umwanditsi umusomyi aba hari izindi nyandiko ze yasomye, akunda, si kimwe nթnyandiko yյmuntu abonye bwa mbere, atazi imyandikire ye (amagambo cyangwa imvugo akunda gukoresha, uburyo asetsa, aca igikuba, atera amatsiko nթbindi). Mu yandi magambo, umuco wյmusomyi nթkiciro abarirwamo mu rubumbambaga ni byo bimuha igisobanuro kթbyo asoma; mbese igisobanuro ntikiri mu nyandiko nyirizina, ahubwo kiri mu buryo isomwa. Barsky, (2012, p. 148) akongeraho ko ҵmunezero uva mu nyandiko igihe uyisoma, ari nkյwo dusanga mu buzima busanzwe; ni imvange iryoshye yթbyo udashobora guteganya, ibipfa kwizana, ugatungurwa ndetse ntunamenye iyo biganaӲ5.Isesengurarari Rishingiye ku bitekerezo bya Sigmund Freud twavuga ko ryatangiye mu kinyejana cya XIX, ku bijyanye nթnzozi, agerageza gusobanura avuga ko akenshi zivuga ku buryo bwաmarenga ibyifuzo bihishe umuntu yapfuritse kure iyo mu bwonko, mu cyo twakwita ҩntbiziӠ(lթnconscient/unconscious) yanga ko byajya ahagaragara, bikamukoza isoni kuko urubumbambaga yarerewemo rutabyemera. Freud rero yasesenguraga inyandiko mpangano zյbuvanganzo harimo nթbikabyankuru. Avuga ko intabizi igira uruhare runini mu myitwarire ya muntu, cyanecyane nթbyifuzo bishingiye ku gitsina. Ibi bigera no mu buvanganzo, bimwe Roland Barthes yise kwishimishiriza mu gusoma. Ikibazo nuko mu gusesengura hari ubwo umusomyi yitirira umwanditsi ibyifuzo bye bwite ndenguriragitsina. Freud avuga ko intabizi irimo ibice bitatu: ҩnkuruziӠ(a/id), hakaba ҩngeӠcyangwa ego, isa nյmuhuza hagati yթnkuruzi nՒinkmiriziӠ(surmoi/superego) kugira ngo bya byifuzo bigayitse bitazamuka. Ibi nanone bigendana nթbigero biranga uko umuntu agenda akura. Freud avuga ko hari ibigero bitatu, buri gihe abihuza nթrari ryյmubiri: ҭbonezakanwaӠ(stade oral/oral stage), ҭbonezanyumaӠ(stade anal/anal stage) na ҭbnezagtsinaӠ(stade phallique/phallic stage); bigakurikirwa nթgihe twakwita ҩsiinzirizaӠ(priode de latence/latency period) hagati yթmyaka itanu nՒimbanzirizabgimbiӠ(pradolescence/preadolescence), bigasozwa nՒubukanguragtsinaӠ(stade gnital/ genital stage). Buri kigero kigira ҩbiterapfnweӠ(complexes) binyuranye, ari byo bya byifuzo bihishe mu ntabizi nkթcyo bitirira Τipe, uvugwa mu migani ya kigereki, cyo kwica se ngo arongore nyina (complexe dՎdipe/Oedipeճ complex) banita ipfunwe ryՒubwiyuumvakneӠ(complexe de castration/castration complex), ni ukuvuga ko umwana umaze kugimbuka bakamubuza kwikuba kuri nyina cyangwa bashiki be, aba yumva ararikiye, ari nko kumukona. Freud asobanura ko gutsikamira ibyo byifuzo ubibuza kuyobora ibitekerezo nթbyifuzo byawe ari byo bizana iterambere nթvutsabushya mu bantu, ariko bikagira nթngaruka ku myifatire imwe nթmwe nko gushakira ibyishimo mu kwibabaza (masochisme/masochism) cyangwa mu bugome no kubabaza abandi (sadisme/ sadism). Hari ariko no kwikinisha, gukora amahano ari yo mibonano yաbafitanye amasano ya hafi nթbindi. Iyo bitabaye ibyo, za ngufu nturukarari ugerageza kuziyobora mu bindi wishimishirizamo ari byo guhanga, kubaka, gukina, ubushakashatsi, ubuvanganzo nթbindi. Nkյko bigaragara, Freud agerageza gusobanura imyifatire, imigirire yաbantu agendeye gusa ku byifuzo mbonezarari ribarimo. Isesengurarari rero ryifashisha ibyo bitekerezo bya Freud mu gucengera inyandiko iyo ari yo yose. Hari ibyo Freud yita condensation (ikintu gishobora guhagararira ikindi kihishe inyuma yacyo, hakaba icyo yita dplacement/displacement (akantu kadafite agaciro gashobora kuduhishurira ikindi kintu gikomeye), hakaba na refoulement/repression (uburyo bwo kwirwanaho ngo utagaragariza bose ibyթrari rikurimo). Jacques Lacan (Lemaire, 1977, pp. 237 Р252) umwigishwa wa Freud, yavuze ko intabizi ikoze nkթmvugo. Dplacement avuga ko yenda gusa cyane nյmuvugo wթyitirira (mtonymie/metonymy), condensation akayigereranya nթhwanisha (mtaphore/metaphor). Ntawahakana ko ubu buryo bushobora gufasha kumva ibintu bimwe na bimwe byerekeye umuhanzi mu buzima bwe no mu byo yandika, ariko kugendera ku irari ryihishe muri muntu ngo usobanure ibimwerekeye byose, ukanabikoresha mu nyandiko zose ni ugukabya. Ni uburyo bwo gushakira ibisobanuro mu byo umuntu agaragaza ku bushake cyangwa se atabishaka, no mu buryo umuhanzi ubwe akirigitwa. Usanga harimo ibisa nյbuhanga bwթcengeramuntu, birengagiza akamaro kթngufu nzima ziramira umuntu. Ibyatangijwe na Freud, bikamamazwa na Mauron (1976), banabyita ҩygamyumvireӠ(psychocritique/psychocriticism). Ni ugusesengura ingingo umuhanzi akunda kugarukaho, yimakaje, rimwe na rimwe atanabizi. Ni yo mpamvu abahanga muri iryo sesengura bahamya ko igihangano icyo ari cyo cyose umuntu yakigereranya nթnzozi zujujwe, umuhanzi tukamubona yiyerekana uko ari, agasa nյwivamo. Cya gihangano kikamera nkթndorerwamo areberamo ishusho ye. Bati umuhanzi agira ibyifuzo, imigambi akomeyeho, ibishuko cyangwa rukuruzi/irari ashaka gushimisha cyangwa gushira abinyujije mu gihangano ke. Ntitwiriwe tuvuga ibyo gusesengura ahantu havugwa mu nkuru (imigi cyanecyane) nթndenguro yաmagambo cyangwa amazina ajyana na byo, bamwe bita ҧocritique/ geocriticismӬ abandi bakavuga Ҏcocritique/ecocriticismӠbitewe nuko bavuga ahantu gusa cyangwa babihuza no kurengera ibidukikije; byatangijwe na Westphal (2005). Twirengagije kandi ibyo kugereranya inyandiko, byaba ku muhanzi umwe cyangwa benshi, mu bihe, ahantu nթndimi bitandukanye (Claudon & Haddad-Wotling, 1992). Ubwo buryo bunyuranye bwթjoranganzo usanga bimwe ari udushami twթbindi abashakashatsi bagiye batandukanya, bashaka ҫwandika izinaӬ ngo byitwe ko bavumbuye uburyo bushya. Ni byo Compagnon (1999) yita Ҭe dmon de la thorieӠcyangwa shitani yo gushakisha imiyobora ku ngufu. Igisubizo dusanga kiri mu guhuriza hamwe ibifitanye isano, ari byo twise isesengura rikomatanya Ұolycritique/ polycriticismӠcyangwa rijyanisha ҳystmique/systemic approachӠ(Nkejabahizi, 2018b); ribarirwamo iryibanda ku kurengera igice iki nթki cyաbantu. Ubu hakaba hazwi cyane ҩrengerabgorӠ(fminisme/feminism) rigendana nՒireengerantiinganyiӬ abihinduza igitsina, ҡbasangiragre/gaboӬ bahuriye mu ishyirahamwe ryitwa LGBT26; ҩrengerabiraburaӠ(ngritude/negritude) nթbindi. Ariko birengagiza ko hari nաbana, abamugaye, abasaza, imbabare, abakozi nաbandi. Guhuza ibyo byiciro byose mu buvanganzo nթjoranganzo ni byo twise ҩsseengura mvganiziӠ(plydroitisme/polydroitism)27.Umuco, ubushakashatsi nթkoranabuhanga Ubuvanganzo nյbushakashatsi bigira, byanze bikunze, akarango gashingiye ku muco wյwabukoze naho yagerageza kutabogama ate, ntikaburamo. Ni ngombwa ko habaho umuco wյbushakashatsi, ҵtaratera imbere mu RwandaӠkandi ari bwo ҳoko yյbumenyi nթnkingi yթterambere rirambyeӮ Abanyaburayi bo barabimenyereye (babigize umuco), ni yo mpamvu ari bo usanga barafashe iya mbere mu kwandika ku mibereho nթmibanire byաbandi batuye isi, bagakora ubushakashatsi ku ndimi zihavugwa bazisesengura, bakandika ibibonezamvugo, bagatangiza ibyo kwigisha gusoma no kwandika muri izo ndimi mu mashuri abanza. Kwari ukugira ngo zibafashe gushyikirana na ba nyirazo no gucengera imibereho yabo binyuze mu biganiro bagiranaga, kuko ayo makuru nta ho bari kuyasoma handi. Ibyo ahanini babyandikaga mu ndimi zabo, ku buryo aho Abanyafurika bajijukiye, amakuru aberekeye bajya kuyashaka muri izo nyandiko zաbazungu. Rimwe na rimwe bagasanga barabavuze uko batari, ibyo bikabababaza (Cheikh Anta, 2000a; 2000b) ). Igihe Abanyafurika ubwabo batangiye kwikorera ubushakashatsi ku biberekeye (umuco, amateka), bisanga barigishijwe mu ndimi zաmahanga, ari zo bumva ziboroheye mu gusobanura ibitekerezo byabo. Bigafasha ba banyaburayi, bakomeza kwivomera amakuru kuri bo aho kugirira akamaro ba nyiri ubwite ari bo banyafurika. Ni yo mpamvu gukora ubushakashatsi mu rurimi runaka bikungahaza ba nyirarwo. Ubwenge bwabo burafunguka, ubumenyi bafite bukaguka, bikaba byatuma uwo ari we wese agira uruhare kuri ubwo bumenyi; agatanga igitekerezo ke mu mvugo cyangwa mu nyandiko, yumva adahejwe, yisanzuye kandi nta pfunwe. Ururimi kandi rwakozwemo ubushakashatsi ruraguka kuko rwunguka amagambo nթnshoza bishya rutari rusanganywe; umuco wաbaruvuga ukaboneraho kwivugurura no gukura, kuko nyine ҵbwenge burarahurwaӮ Ibyo utari uzi bikwizanira ku mbehe kuko biri mu rurimi rwawe wumva, bikakungura ibitekerezo nթmikorere. Ibirebana nյbuhinzi nյbworozi bya kijyambere, kwirinda indwara, ibiza, ikoranabuhanga, iyaba byageraga ku muturage mu rurimi rwe kavukire; yabyumva, bikamugirira akamaro, na we akabigiramo uruhare kurushaho. Ni yo mpamvu ibyavuzwe mu ntangiriro yթgitabo ko ҭuri iki gihe, abashakashatsi bo mu Rwanda bakunze gukora ubushakashatsi bifashishije indimi mvamahanga, cyanecyane Icyongereza nՉgifaransa; ibyo bigakorwa mu gihe mu Rwanda abaturage barenga 99.4% bazi gusa Ikinyarwanda nkյrurimi bashobora kumva no kuganiramo, ari na rwo rurimi rwabo kavukireӬ ari ibyo kuvugururwa, nubwo atari ubwa mbere bivugwa ariko ntihagire igihinduka. Ururimi ni nkյmukaya, iyo rudakoreshejwe ruranyunyuka, ingufu zigatakara. Ibi bisobanura ko indimi zitagendana nթgihe tugezemo kթkoranabuhanga, ngo zishakemo amagambo aryerekeye, zizasigara inyuma ari nta kamaro; amaherezo zikazapfa, zigasigara gusa mu mateka. Ikoranabuhanga tuvuga si ugukoresha terefone ngendanwa gusa, si me to you na mobile money; ni no kwinjiza mu muco, ni ukuvuga imibereho ya buri munsi, ibijyanye no gukoresha ҢwaanguӠ(mudasobwa), ariko cyanecyane abantu bagashobora kubyikorera. Urugero ni ҩngazabugeengeӠҬogiciels/softwareӠzinyuranye, kwifashisha iryo koranabuhanga mu buvuzi, mu buhinzi nյbworozi no kubyaza umusaruro ibiboneka nթbyera mu gihugu. Aha ni ho hagaragara akamaro ko gushyira ingufu mu guhindura mu Kinyarwanda ibyanditse mu ndimi zաhandi, bigaragara ko ari ingenzi mu iterambere ryՁbanyarwanda.Dutanga urugero ku bintu bimwe na bimwe Abanyarwanda bagombye gusobanurirwa kurushaho imiterere cyangwa imikorere yabyo kugira ngo biyungure ubumenyi, bitewe nթcyo buri wese akora; babe baheraho mu guhanga udushya kuko ni yo nzira rukumbi yթterambere rirambye. Ibyo ni nkթmiterere yթbihingwa (ikigori, igisheke nյko kivamo isukari) mu buhinzi; indwara ya kanseri, imikorere yՒumuyborabtumwӠmu mubiri ҳystme nerveux/nervous systemӬ isuzumirashusho nyarukuruzi (IRMN/MRI) mu buvuzi; tereviziyo mfindishamibare (TNT) mu itumanaho; ururangabihe ubu ruvugwa cyane kubera ko imihindagurikire yarwo igira ingaruka zikomeye ku mibereho yաbaturage, harimo nթbiza; kuremera urusoro hanze yյmubiri (FIV) ku bijyanye nթmyororokere nթbindi. Ubwo bumenyi bwose Abanyarwanda bakeneye kubugira kuko, byanze, bikunze, bizagira ingaruka ku mibereho nյmuco byabo. Nta kundi bizabageraho nibidasobanurwa mu rurimi rwabo kavukire28. Umusozo Ubushakashatsi ku bumenyi nyamuntu buri mu byatumye inyoko muntu itera imbere mu nzego zinyuranye kuko kumenya muntu kurushaho (umuco we, uko agenda yiyungura ubwenge nյbumenyi, ibimuranga, ibyo akunda cyangwa akeneye, bitewe nաho ari mu gihe runaka), biri mu bituma habaho ivutsabushya nթterambere. Iyi nyandiko iragaragaza akamaro ko gukora ubushakashatsi ku muco, binyuze no mu buvanganzo; nյkuntu abakora ubwo bushakashatsi inzira banyura ari nyinshi. Ibyo bigaterwa nթbyo baha agaciro kurusha ibindi nթbibashimisha. Biratangaje kuba, kugeza ubu, anthropologie/anthropology ubusanzwe bivuga ubuhanga busesengura ibyerekeye muntu (anthropos) muri rusange, hari abagikomeza kubyita ko bireba gusa imiryango yաbantu bitwa ko bakiri inyuma mu majyambere. Birakwiye rero ko Abanyafurika nՁbanyarwanda byյmwihariko basobanurirwa mu rurimi rwabo ibyյbwo bumenyi kandi bakabigiramo uruhare kugira ngo barusheho kwimenya, kujijuka no gutera imbere.Ubuvanganzo na bwo ni bumwe mu buryo bwo kugaragaza imyumvire, imico nթterambere ku bantu aba nաba nթmiryango. Ni yo mpamvu hariho guhuza ubuvanganzo nյrubumbambaga bwavukiyemo nաbo bugenewe, hakaba nթngeri zյbuvanganzo zishyira imbere cyane imibereho nթmiterere yյrubumbambaga uru nյru. Umuco nյbuvanganzo rero ni magirirane, maze kubusesengura bikaba ingirakamaro mu bumenyi nyamuntu. Gusa rero inzira zabaye urufaya, akenshi bibanda ku kantu kamwe; bihinduka nka bimwe byաbahigi benshi bayobya imbwa uburari. Twe tukaba dusanga ubwo buryo bwose bukwiye guhurizwa hamwe, umusesenguzi akaba ufasha abasomyi kurushaho kunurirwa na bwa buvanganzo; kuko inyandiko ari urubera rwաmabara menshi, maze kuyagaragaza mu rusobe rwayo igihe usesengura, bikaba ari byo bituma inyura abayakira. Mu Rwanda natwe dukeneye kwimakaza umuco wյbushakashatsi nյbushakashatsi ku muco; kuko ari inkingi yթterambere rirambye nkյko bigaragara cyanecyane mu bihugu byo muri Aziya kandi nաbahanga banyuranye bakaba badasiba kubishimangira, harimo nՉshami ryՕmuryango wՁbibumye ryita ku Bumenyi, Ubuhanga nՕmuco (UNESCO). Ni ingenzi kandi gukora ubushakashatsi mu ndimi kavukire (ari yo mpamvu muri iyi nyandiko hagaragaramo amagambo menshi tutamenyereye mu Kinyarwanda), kugira ngo Abanyarwanda batazasigara inyuma, ngo bahezwe cyangwa biheze muri rya sango rya ҭpanguheӠinyoko muntu ihuriyeho. IndangasokoAdorno, T. -W. Les rites de passage: Etude systmatique des rites de la porte et du seuil, de lըospitalit, de lաdoption, de la grossesse et de lաccouchement, de la naissance, de lեnfance, de la pubert, de lթnitiation, de lկrdination, etc. Paris: Picard. van Gennep, A.
