(2000 ). Manuel de sociocritique. 2me d. Paris: LՈarmattan.Zukin, S. (1995). The cultures in cities. Oxford: Backwell.UMUTWE 4 AMAHAME NGENGAMYITWARIRE MU BUSHAKASHATSI Pierre Canisius Ruterana IntangiriroBuri bushakashatsi bugomba gukurikiza amahame ngengamyitwarire ajyanye na bwo. Aya mahame yerekeranye nյko umushakashatsi agomba kubanza kubaza ko abantu bazagira uruhare muri bwo niba bemera gukorana na we, kugabanya ibyago nթngorane abazagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi bahura na byo, kutamenyekanisha amazina yabo no kubagirira ibanga, kwirinda imikorere irimo uburiganya, no guha abazagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi uburenganzira bwo kwivana mu bushakashatsi (Swedish Research Council, 2017; Bryman, 2008) guhera mu gihe kթmbata yյbushakashatsi, mu ikusanyamakuru, mu isesenguramakuru no mu gihe cyo kugaragaza ibyavuye mu bushakashatsi. Uyu mutwe wa 4 wՠiki gitabo urareba ibibazo bijyanye nաmahame ngengamyitarire bibaho mu byiciro bitandukanye mu bushakashatsi, kandi bishingiye ku bintu bibiri byթngenzi, ari byo: uburyo ukora ubushakashatsi agomba gufata abantu akoraho cyangwa akorana na bo ubushakashatsi ndetse nթbikorwa umushakashatsi agomba cyangwa atagomba gukora mu mibanire ye na bo. Ni ngombwa ko abakora ubushashatsi bamenyeshwa ibijyanye nյko ukora ubushakashatsi yitwara kugira ngo bafate ibyemezo bazi ibyo bakora kandi bamenye ingaruka zաmahitamo bikoreye ubwabo. Kubera izo mpamvu, abashakashatsi bagomba kubahiriza amahame ngengamyitwarire nta kuyarengaho uko biboneye. Muri iki gice, turishingikiriza ku moko atanu yթngenzi yաmahame ngengamyitwarire yagaragajwe na Bryman (2008), Diener na Crandall (1978) akomoka ku mahame shingiro arimo (1) guteza ingorane abagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi, (2) kwemera ku bushake kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi, (3) kwinjira mu buzima bwite bwյmuntu, (4) gukoresha uburiganya nՠ(5) uburenganzira bwo kwikura mu bushakashatsi.Guteza ingorane abagira uruhare mu bushakashatsiIkintu cya mbere kթngenzi umushakashatsi agomba kwitwararika ni uko imigendekere yյbushakashatsi yaba ishobora guteza ingorane iyo ari yo yose (ingorane iriho cyangwa ishobora kuzabaho) abazabugiramo uruhare. Abantu benshi bafata ubushashatsi bigaragara ko bushobora guteza ingorane abazabugiramo uruhare nkյbutemewe. Bryman (2008) asobanura ingorane nkթbyago bikora ku mubiri, ku mutungo, ku mubabaro ushingiye ku mitekerereze cyangwa imibanire nաbandi, ku buzima bwite no kugaragaza umwirondoro byաbagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi, bishobora kubaho, byaba ku buryo buziguye cyangwa butaziguye, mu gihe kթkowa ryյbushakashatsi. Ikindi kandi, ni ingenzi gukemurana ubushishozi kandi neza ibyo abantu batandukaniraho bishingiye ku muco, idini, politiki, imibanire nաbandi, igitsina cyangwa ibindi abazagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi batandukaniraho bishobora kubateza ingorane runaka ku byiciro byose bigize ubushakashatsi. Ku bwa Diener na Crandall (1978, p. 19), ingorane zikubiyemo ibintu byinshi harimo ingorane zթbabazamubiri, kubangamira iterambere ryաbagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi, kwitakariza ikizere (ikibazo kթmitekerereze no kumva utamerewe neza), kubangamirwa nաbo mubana, umuhangayiko nթkindi kintu cyose cyatuma abagira uruhare mu bushashatsi bakorerwa ibikorwa bibi kandi bigayitse.Ibishobora guteza ingorane abagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi birebwa kandi nաmategeko ngengamyitwarire aho bisaba ubwitonzi nյbushishozi mu kubika ibanga ryաmakuru yatanzwe mu gihe cyյbushakashatsi. Ibi bisobanuye ko umwirondoro nաmajwi yafashwe byաbantu bigomba kugirwa ibanga. Iri hame risobanuye kandi ko hagomba ubushishozi bwinshi igihe cyo gushyira ahabona ibyavuye mu bushakashatsi kugira ngo hizerwe ko umwirondoro wաbabugizemo uruhare utagaragara cyangwa ngo ube wavumburwa. Kimwe mu bibazo byerekeranye nթhame ryo guteza ingorane abagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi ni uko biba bidashoboka kumenya mu bihe byose ko iyo ngorane ishobora kubaho, nյbwo ibi bitagomba gufawa nkթbitavuze ko nta mpamvu yo gushaka uburyo bushoboka bwo kubarinda ingorane bahura nazo. Bityo rero, mu rwego rwo kugabanya ibyago byabateza ingorane, ukora ubushakashatsi agomba gutekereza uburyo abazagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi babimwemerera, uburyo yarinda uburenganzira bwabo bwo kutamenyekana no kugirirwa ibanga, uburyo bwo kwirinda imikorere irimo uburiganya mu gihe arimo gukora imbata yյbushakashatsi ndetse no gutanga uburenganzira bwo kwikura mu bushakashatsi igihe icyo ari cyo cyose.Kwemera ku bushake Nkյko Ikigo cyՕbushakashatsi cyo muri Suwedi (Swedish Research Council, 2017) kibivuga, mu ihame ryo kwemera ku bushake, abagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi bagomba kugezwaho amakuru ahagije arebana nյbwo bushakashatsi, nյburyo bushobora kubagiraho ingaruka. Ahangaha, kwemera ku bushake bisobanura ko abantu bagomba gusobanukirwa neza ko barimo kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi nթcyo ubwo bushakashatsi bubasaba. Kubera iyo mpamvu, bagomba guhabwa amakuru mu buryo bwumvikana hakoreshejwe imvugo bumva, bagasobanukirwa neza. Hanyuma, bagomba kwizezwa uburenganzira no guhabwa umwanya uhagije byo gutekereza niba bazagira uruhare muri ubwo bushakashatsi cyangwa niba batazarugiramo, bityo bikagabanya kuba hakoreshwa agahato, igitutu kitari ngombwa cyangwa itoteza. Abazagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi rero bagomba guhabwa hakiri kare amakuru arebana nթbijyanye nթmyitwarire ifitanye isano nյbushakashatsi, aha twavuga nkթntego zյbushakashatsi, uburyo buzakoreshwa, ibishobora kuva muri ubwo bushakashatsi ndetse nթbintu bitandukanye busaba, ingorane, imbogamizi nթbyago ababugizemo uruhare bashobora guhura na byo, uruhushya rwanditse wahawe nթnzego bireba rwo gukora ubushakashatsi bwawe, izina ryawe nթkigo ubarizwamo, nյkuntu ibikoresho bizifashishwa mu bushakashatsi bizafatwa ndetse nյko ibizava mu bushakashatsi bizakoreshwa. Byongeye kandi, iri hame risobanura ko abashobora kuzagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi bagomba guhabwa amakuru menshi akenewe kugira ngo bafate ikemezo bazi impamvu bashaka cyangwa badashaka kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi. Uburyo buhishira ukora ubushakashatsi uwo ari we ntibuba bwubahirije iri hame kuko abagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi badahabwa amahirwe yo kwanga gukorana nյkora ubushakashatsi. Igihe cyose bishoboka, kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi byagombye gushingira ku kwemera kuvuye mu bushake bwաbakorerwaho ubushakashatsi. Ibi byerekana ko ukora ubushakashatsi afite inshingano yo kubasobanurira ku buryo bwuzuye kandi bunoze: icyo ubwo bushakashatsi bugamije, ukora ubushakashatsi nյbutera inkunga, impamvu bugiye gukorwa nյko bugomba gushyigikirwa. Mu byյkuri, ibi ni byo Erikson (1967) ashaka kuganishaho igihe avuga ko iyo haramutse habayeho guteza ingorane abagize uruhare mu bushakashatsi, nibura ntibazijujutira ko bashutswe cyangwa batahawe amakuru ahagije: ԉyo bibayeho ko duteza ingorane abantu bemeye gukorerwaho ubushakashatsi, dushobora nibura kwisobanura tuvuga ko bari bafite icyo bazi ku byago bushobora guteza ɕ (Erikson, 1967, p. 369).Ikindi gice kirebana no kwemera ku bushake ni ihame ryյko abagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi bagombye kuba abakorerabushake, bakabikora badahaswe cyangwa ngo bashukwe. Aho bidashoboka ko abantu bemera kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi, ugomba gutanga impamvu yյko byagenze. Ugomba kumenya kandi ko hari aho kwemera ku bushake biba ngombwa ko kudakenerwa cyangwa kukaba gukeneye koroshywa. Ku rundi ruhande, ubushakashatsi ku bana bari munsi yթmyaka 16, ubusanzwe ni ngombwa ko ababyeyi babo ari bo basabwa kubemerera kubugiramo uruhare cyangwa se abandi barezi bateganywa nաmategeko. Urubyiruko rufite imyaka 16 no hejuru yayo rufatwa muri rusange nkյrushobora kwemera ku bushake, ariko nanone ibi bihinduka bitewe nյbwoko bwյbushakashatsi. Gusaba umuntu ku giti ke kwemera kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi bishobora kutaba ngombwa mu bikorwa byյbushakashatsi bimwe na bimwe, nkյbushakashatsi ku mibereho yաbaturage busa nkաho bukorwa mu ibanga (urugero, ubushakashatsi busaba kwitegereza imyifatire rusange yաbaturage). Kwiga ku bantu mu ibanga ndetse nյburyo bukoreshwa mu gutara amakuru ya bene ubwo bushakashatsi bishobora guteza ingorane umuntu agomba gutekerezaho. Abashakashatsi bashishikarizwa kugisha inama inzego zibishinzwe zifite aho zihuriye nյbwo bushakashatsi batekereza gukora. Aha ni ho basaba ubuyobozi bwաho bashaka gukorera kuborohereza kugera ku kigo runaka ndetse bakanasaba kwemererwa kuvugana cyangwa gukorana ubushakashatsi nաbakozi bթcyo kigo. Nkյko Cohen, Manion na Morrison (2000) babivuga, ngo ubu buryo bwթmikorere ni bwiza cyane kubera ko bitera ishema, bikanatanga icyizere ku bashakashatsi kuko biyumvamo ko ari abacukumbuzi bakomeye kandi bubahiriza amahame ngengamyitwarire. Gusa hari ahantu biba bitoroshye kwemererwa kuhakorera ubushakashatsi, nko mu mashuri (yaba ayթncuke, abanza, ayisumbuye ndetse nաmakuru), mu nganda, kwa muganga, nաhandi. Bisaba ko abakora ubushakashatsi bemeza ba nyiri ibigo ku buryo budashidikanywaho ko ari abashakashatsi bahamye kandi bubaha ikiremwamuntu kugira ngo babemerere kugira icyo bakora mu bigo byabo. Ikindi kandi ni ngombwa kugirana ubucuti cyangwa umubano mwiza nաho wifuza gukorera ubushakashatsi bwawe. Ni byiza ko abemeye kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi bagira ubwisanzure ku mushakashatsi. Urupapuro rwo kwemera ku bushakeUbusanzwe abashakashatsi bahitamo kugaragaza ko abantu babemereye kugira uruhare mu bushakashashtsi bwabo babasinyisha impapuro zo kwemera ku bushake. Urugero, mu bushakashatsi Peel (2004) yakoze ku batinganyi bաbagore nաbաbagabo, yakoresheje urupapuro rwo kwemera ku bushake rwagaragazaga intego zյbushakashatsi ndetse nթmvano byabwo. Urwo rupapuro rwamenyeshaga abazabazwa ko kugira uruhare muri ubwo bushakashatsi ari ubushake bwabo, ko bafite uburenganzira bwo kwanga gusubiza ikibazo icyo ari cyo cyose, ko bashobora guhagarika ikiganiro igihe icyo ari cyo cyose kandi ko bashoboraga gukuramo amakuru batanze mu byumweru bibiri nyuma yթkiganiro.Yabamenyesheje kandi ko ikiganiro kizafatwa amajwi, ko nta muntu uzacyumva uretse we nյmuyobora mu bushakashatsi, ko ibice bike byacyo bishobora kumvwa nաbandi bantu bake, ko kizashyirwa mu nyandiko ariko ko amakuru yose agaragaza umwirondoro wabo azavanwamo. Hanyuma abari kubazwa basabwaga gushyira umukono wabo ku rupapuro rwo kwemera ku bushake kugira ngo bagaragaze ko bemeye kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi ku bwende bwabo. Akamaro kթmpapuro nkթzi ni uko ziha ababazwa amahirwe yo kumenyeshwa ku buryo bwuzuye uko ubushakashatsi buteye ndetse nթngaruka kubugiramo uruhare bishobora guteza bikiri mu ntangiriro. Ikindi kandi, ukora ubushakashatsi aba afite impapuro zo kwemera ku bushake ziriho umukono haramutse habaye impungenge ababugizemo uruhare bagaragaje cyangwa zigaragajwe nաbandi. Ikibazo gikomeye ni uko kuba ababazwa basabwa gusinya urwo rupapuro bishobora gutera impungenge ku ruhande rwabo aho kuzoroshya ku buryo birangira banze kugira uruhare muri ubwo bushakashatsi. Impapuro ngengamyitwarire zo kwemera ku bushake zigomba kuba zifite ibice bine: imvo nթmvano yյbwo bushakashatsi, ibintu abazabugiramo uruhare bashobora gusabwa, ibibazo ku kwemera ku bushake nաmagambo make asoza ukwemera ku bushake. Mu mvo nթmvano yյbushakashatsi, umushakashatsi ashyiramo amakuru akurikira: umutwe wյbushakashatsi, ikigamijwe, uburyo ubushakashatsi buzakorwamo, ndetse nթbishobora kuzabuvamo. Ni byiza gutanga iyi mvo nթmvano mu gika kimwe gusa, ntibitware igihe cyաbasubiza. Ku byerekeye ibyo ababazwa bashobora gusabwa, ukora ubushakashatsi agomba kugaragaza neza ibyo basabwa bijyanye no kugira uruhare kwabo muri ubwo bushakashatsi. Ibi bikubiyemo igihe cyabo bagomba gutanga, ibishobora kubabangamira nթbishobora gutuma bumva batamerewe neza. Ukora ubushakashatsi agomba kandi gusobanura icyo azakora kugira ngo agabanye ingaruka zթbi bintu basabwa (urugero, uburyo azarinda umwirondoro wabo kumenyekana). Ku birebana nթbibazo ku kwemera ku bushake kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi, urupapuro ngengamitwarire rwo kwemera ku bushake ruba rurimo ibibazo byinshi byemeza ko ubazwa yasomye kandi yasobanukiwe amakuru yթngenzi umushakashatsi yatanze arebana nյbushakashatsi bwe. Byongeye kandi, ababazwa bamenya ibyo basabwa gukora nթcyo umushakashatsi yakoze kugira ngo agerageze kugabanya ingaruka zabyo. Hanyuma rero, ababazwa bagomba kuba bemeye kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi ku bushake kandi bamenye ko bashobora kubihagarika igihe icyo ari cyo cyose. Urugero rwa bimwe mu bibazo wabaza:1. Usobanukiwe neza intego yյbu bushakashatsi? (Yego/Oya)2. Wasomye kandi wasobanukiwe neza icyo ubu bushakashatsi bugusaba? (Yego/Oya)3. Wasobanukiwe ko ushobora guhagarika kubugiramo uruhare igihe icyo ari cyo cyose? (Yego/Oya)Ku byerekeye amagambo make asoza ukwemera ku bushake, igice giheruka urupapuro ngengamyitwarire rwo kwemera ku bushake kigomba kugira amagambo agaragaza ko ababazwa bemeye kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi bwawe ku bwende bwabo kandi ko basobanukiwe nթcyo basabwa gukoramo (ni ukuvuga, kwemera ku bushake). Mu mpera yյrupapuro rwo kwemera ku bushake ugomba kuhasiga umwanya ugenewe abagize uruhare mu bushakashatsi bwawe nյmwanya wawe (umushakashatsi) kugira ngo hashyirweho itariki nյmukono. Urugero rwթbikubiye mu rupapuro rwo gusaba kwemera ku bushakeTwagira ngo tugusabe kuganira natwe kuri ubu bushakashatsiɠ(umutwe wabo) kuko dutekereza ko ushobora kuba ufite amakuru wadusangiza. Intego yյbu bushakashatsi ni... Ntituguhatira kuganira natwe kuri ubu bushakashatsi niba utabishaka. Niba wiyemeje kubugiramo uruhare, turagusaba kuganira natwe mu gihe kiyingayinga isaha ku birebanaɠNtiduteganya ko hazabaho ingaruka kuri wowe bitewe nյko waganiriye natwe. (Ntabwo) turi bugufate amajwi cyangwa ngo tuzagaragaze amazina yawe muri ubu bushakashatsi, kandi amakuru uzaduha azagirwa ibanga. Ushobora gusimbuka ibibazo ibyo ari byo byose udashaka gusubiza kandi ushobora no guhagarika ikiganiro turi kugirana igihe icyo ari cyo cyose. Inyungu iri mu kugira uruhare muri ubu bushakashatsi ni uko ushobora gufashaɮ Ntabwo uzahemberwa kuba waganiriye natwe kandi nta nաmafaranga usabwa gutanga. Ibizava muri ubu bushakashatsi bishobora gutangarizwa mu nama zitandukanye cyangwa se mu binyamakuru bitandukanye ariko nta zina ryawe tuzagaragaza.Kwinjira mu buzima bwite bwյmuntuIgice cya gatatu kթmpungenge zijyanye nթmyitwarire yյkora ubushakashatsi ni ikirebana no kwinjira mu buzima bwite bwյmuntu bishobora gukorwaho. Uburenganzira ku buzima bwite ni ihame benshi muri twe bakomeyeho kandi kwica iryo hame mu izina ryյbushakashatsi ntabwo abantu babibona nkթbyemewe. Rifitanye isano nթgitekerezo cyo gusaba kwemera ku bushake. Impamvu ni uko ikigero ubazwa atangaho ukwemera ku bushake bwe hashingiwe ku gusobanukirwa neza icyo kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi bishobora kumusaba, ni na cyo amenyaho mu buryo runaka ko yatanze uburenganzira ku buzima bwite bwe kubera impamvu runaka.Ku birebana nյbuzima bwite bwյmuntu ndetse nթbanga, abashakashatsi bagomba kugirira ibanga abo bakorana mu bushakashatsi bwabo (Bryman, 2008). Abashakashatsi bagomba no kwirinda ibiranga umwirondoro wյmuntu bishobora gutuma hamenyekana ababajijwe, nkաmazina, muri raporo zյbushakashatsi zabo. Israel na Hay (2004) bafata ibanga nkթhame ngengamyitwarire rikomeye. Nkյko babivuga, abantu batagize ibanga ryթbyo babwirwa, Ԯi nde wazavugana na bo mu gihe kizaza?ՠ(Israel & Hay, 2004, p. 94). Ikindi kandi, uretse kuba kutabika ibanga bidakwiriye, bigaragara ko bishobora guteza ingorane abashakashatsi bթgihe kizaza. Ku birebana nյmutekano wabo, abagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi bagomba kwizezwa ko amakuru yakusanyijwe atazatangazwa ku mugaragaro mu buryo bwatuma umuntu uyu nյyu amenyekana. Ni muri urwo rwego ibirango nkթbi bikurikira: ushaje/ ukiri muto, umwana/ ukuze, utuye mu mujyi/ mu cyaro, igitsina gore/ gabo, ukorera Leta/ uwikorera, nթbindi ari byo bigomba gukoreshwa mu kugaragaza amagambo yatoranyijwe yavuzwe nաbabazwa. Ku bwթbyo, kugira ngo wirinde kwica inshingano yawe yo kurinda ibanga ryաbagize uruhare mu bushakashatsi bwawe, ni ingenzi: (a) kubona uruhushya rwo gutanga amakuru nթbimenyetso bigaragaza umwirondoro wյmuntu, cyanecyane amagambo yavuzwe nյmuntu, mbere yo gushyira ahabona ayo makuru; (b) kwereka abagize uruhare mu bushakashatsi bwawe ibyo uzagaragaza maze bakaguha uruhushya rwo kubikoresha; (c) kubasaba kwemeza imyanzuro yavanywe mu makuru batanze cyangwa se gutandukanya ku buryo bugaragara ibitekerezo byawe nթbyo batanze igihe cyo kubyandika; no (d) gukoresha amazina atari ayյkuri ku bantu/imiryango yagize uruhare mu bushakashatsi bwawe ku buryo batabasha kumenyekana. Muri make, abashakashatsi bagomba kwigengesera kugira ngo barinde ibanga ryաmakuru yatanzwe ku rwego rwյmuntu ku giti cye ndetse no ku rwego rwթmiryango. Umwirondoro wաbabajijwe ntugomba kugaragazwa keretse bahaye umushakashatsi uruhusa mu nyandiko mbere yյko ubushakashatsi butangira. Igihe ibiranga umwirondoro wյmuntu byakoreshejwe mu bushakashatsi, abakora ubushakashatsi bagomba gusobanura impamvu ibi ari ngombwa nյko ibanga rizarindwa. Igihe bishoboka, ababajijwe bafite umwirondoro wagaragajwe bafite uburenganzira bwo kureba ayo makuru yerekana umwirindoro wabo mbere yյko akwirakwizwa. Abashakashatsi bagomba kumenya ibyago byaterwa no kumenyekanisha amazina yյmuntu no kwinjira mu buzima bwite bwe bivuye ku buryo bwose bwo kubika amakuru no kuyatunganya, harimo mudasobwa nաmadosiye, ibyabitswe kuri imeli (email), ibyafotowe, gasete zibikwaho amajwi nաmashusho cyangwa andi makuru ayo ari yo yose ahita agaragaza umwirondoro wյmuntu. Gukoresha uburiganyaBryman (2008) avuga ko gukoresha uburiganya bibaho igihe abashakashatsi basobanura ubushakashatsi bwabo mu ishusho yթkintu kitari icyo buri cyo. Iyo babigenje gutyo, abashakashatsi baba bashaka kugabanya uko ababazwa bumva icyo ubwo bushakashatsi bugamije kugira ngo babashe kubasubiza ku buryo busanzwe. Nkյko abahanga bamwe babivuga (Israel & Hay, 2004; Peel, 2004; Swedish Research Council, 2017), gukoresha uburiganya hari ubwo biba ngombwa mu bushakashatsi bukorwa mu ibanga, bikaba bishobora gusobanurwa mu ngero zimwe na zimwe. Ubushakashatsi bukorwa mu ibanga bivuga ubushakashatsi aho (a) umwirondoro wյbukora cyangwa se (b) intego yյbushakashatsi bitazwi nաbabugiramo uruhare. Ingero zաho wahitamo gukora ubushakashatsi bwo mu ibanga zirimo izi zikurikira: (1) igihe bidakunda ko wamenyesha buri wese icyo urimo gukora bitewe nաhantu hihariye urimo gukorera ubushakashatsi bwawe. Urugero, igihe ubushakashatsi ukora bwerekeranye no kwitegereza cyanecyane ahantu ha rusange cyangwa kuri murandasi. (2) Igihe kwitegerereza ahabona cyangwa kumenya neza intego yյbushakashatsi bwawe bishobora kugira ikintu kihariye bihindura ku kibazo kirimo gukorwaho ubushakashatsi, izi zikaba ari impungenge nyamukuru ku ireme ryթbizava mu bushakashatsi bwawe.Abashyigikiye imigenzereze yյburiganya mu bushakashatsi basobanura bavuga ko ababazwa bemera kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi gusa iyo batabwijwe ukuri. Mu byյkuri, umuntu yavuga ko ubushakashatsi bukozwe mu ibanga ndetse nթmigenzereze yյburiganya bifite umwanya mu bushakashatsi cyanecyane aho bikoreshwa byagambiriwe nյbwo bibonwa nkթbintu bikurura impaka. Dufashe nkյrugero rwյbushakashatsi aho ushaka gusobanukirwa neza ibanga nյmuco wo gukorera hamwe mu ruganda uru nյru. Ubundi wiyumvisha neza ko gukoresha kwitegereza abakozi nթbikorwa byaba uburyo bukwiriye bwo gukoresha muri ubwo bushakashatsi bwawe. Ariko kandi, uratekereza ko abakozi nibaramuka bamenye ko urimo kubitegereza, no kubacunga, bashobora kwitwara mu buryo butandukanye nյko bisanzwe. Ni yo mpamvu, washobora kuba wahawe uruhushya rwo kubikora mu ibanga cyangwa se ukababwira inkuru itari iyյkuri igamije gusobanura impamvu uri ahongaho. Mu buryo bwemewe, kuvugisha ukuri bigomba kuba ishingiro ryթsano iri hagati yաbakora ubushakashatsi, ababazwa nաbandi bashaka kubugiramo uruhare. Gukoresha ubushakashatsi bukozwe mu ibanga cyangwa kubeshya ababazwa bigomba gusobanurwa neza kandi bigatangirwa uruhushya nթnzego zibifitiye ububasha. Iyo bibaye ngombwa ko ubushakashatsi bukorwa mu ibanga cyangwa bukoresha uburiganya, ababazwa bagomba gusobanurirwa impamvu nyuma yյbwo bushakashatsi igihe bikwiye. Abashakashatsi ntibagomba gushishikarira kubeshya ababazwa cyangwa kubayobya kubera ko bibwira ko batazemera kubafasha. Abashakashatsi bagomba kugaragaza impamvu zumvikana zյko ubwo bushakashatsi bwo mu ibanga bugomba gukomeza abatanga amakuru batagombye kubyemera, nյburyo inyungu zizava muri ubwo bushakashatsi ari ingirakamaro kurenza kure kuba abakorerwaho ubushakashatsi batemeye kuganira na bo.Gutanga uburenganzira bwo kwikura mu bushakashatsiUretse ingero zյbushakashatsi bwo mu ibanga aho bidakunda ko buri wese uri kugenzurwa amenya icyo urimo gukora, abagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi buri gihe bagomba kugira uburenganzira bwo kwikura mu bushakashatsi ku rwego bwaba bugezeho urwo arirwo rwose. Igihe ababazwa bahisemo kwikura mu bushakashatsi, ntibagomba gushyirwaho igitutu cyangwa guhatirwa kutavamo hakoreshejwe uburyo ubwo aribwo bwose. Ababazwa bagomba guhabwa amakuru yerekeye uburyo bwo kwikura mu bushakashatsi ndetse nթgihe biba bitagishoboka gukuramo amakuru batanze (urugero, nka nyuma yo gushyira ahabona ibyavuye mu bushakashatsi).Andi makuru yթngenzi ajyanye nյburenganzira bwաbagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi ni arebana nաgahimbazamusyi. Ibikorwa byo kureshya ababazwa, urugero nko kubaha serivisi zihariye cyangwa kubishyura amafaranga (bitari ukubishyurira amafaranga yյrugendo, cyangwa se rimwe na rimwe, ayթgihe batanze) no gushyiraho agahimbazamusyi kadakwiye, ubusanzwe bigomba kwirindwa. Abagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi bagombye kwiyemerera kugerwaho nթngorane zishobora guterwa no kugira uruhare muri ubwo bushakashatsi ndetse nթgihe nta gahimbazamusyi bahawe. Kwishyura ibyo ababazwa batanze kugira ngo bitabire, urugero nkաmafaranga yյrugendo, bipfa kuba atari amafaranga bahabwa mu rwego rwթgihembo, birakorwa. Abakora ubushakashatsi bagomba gushishoza ku ihame ryo kwemera kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi ku bushake iyo abatangamakuru bafite aho bahuriye mu kazi cyangwa se bafitanye isano yo mu muryango nյmushakashatsi. Ingero: gukorana nաbanyeshuri uri umwarimu wabo, gukorana nաbakozi uri umukoresha wabo, gukorana nաbarwayi uri umuganga wabo, kukorana nաbavandimwe muvukana, nթbindi. Birashoboka ko ubushake bwաba bantu bwo kugira uruhare mu bushakashatsi bushobora guturuka ku nyungu runaka baba babutegerejemo cyangwa se ku gutinya ingaruka zishobora kubabaho igihe batemeye kugira uruhare muri ubwo bushakashatsi. UmwanzuroIki gice cyarebanaga nթbibazo bijyanye nաmahame ngengamyitwarire mu bushakashatsi bishobora kubaho igihe umuntu arimo gukora ubushakashatsi. Ibi bibazo byerekeranye nթmyitwarire akenshi bifitanye isano nթngorane abagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi bashobora kugira bitewe nյruhare bagize mu bushakashatsi, kudasobanurira neza ababazwa ibyյbwo bushakashakatsi ngo bemere kubugiramo uruhare ku bushake, kutagaragaza umwirondoro wabo, kubagirira ibanga no kwinjira mu buzima bwite bwabo, gukoresha uburiganya no gutanga uburenganzira bwo kwikura mu bushakashatsi. Uburyo bwose buzakoreshwa mu bushakashatsi bugomba gusobanurirwa neza abazabugiramo uruhare, mu rurimi bumva kandi ku buryo bworoshye. IndangasokoBryman, A. (2008). Social research methods (3rd edition). Oxford: Oxford University Press.Cohen, L., Manion, L., & Morrison, K. (2000). Research methods in education (5th edition). New York: RoutledgeFalmer.Diener, E., & Crandall, R. (1978). Ethics in social and behavioural research. Chicago: University of Chicago Press.Erikson, K. T. (1967). A comment on disguised observation in sociology. Social Problems, 14(4), 366 Р373.Israel, M., & Hay, I. (2004). Research ethics for social scientists. London: Sage.Peel, E. (2004). Gaining informed consent. In S. Becker, & A. Bryman, Understanding research for social policy and practice: Themes, methods, and approaches (pp. 56 Р88). Bristol: Policy Press.Swedish Research Council. (2017). Good research practice. Stockholm: Swedish Research Council. Ibi rero bigira ingaruka mbi mu gutuma badashobora guhererekanya ubumenyi. Iyo umushakashatsi adahereye ku byաbandi banditse, biragoye kugira ngo abone ifatiro ryյbumenyi bushya. Ntashobora kumenya niba hari igishya azanye mu bisanzwe bizwi cyangwa se ngo amenye niba hari ibisobanuro byթnyongera ashyize ahagaragara kugira ngo ibyari bisanzwe bizwi birusheho kumvikana. Abasoma ibyo yanditse na bo ntibiborohera kumenya niba hari icyuho aje kuziba mu bumenyi busanzwe buzwi. Ni yo mpamvu iki gice cyo gusesengura ubushakashatsi bwakozwe mbere (literature review) ari ingenzi. Kigamije rero kwerekana imirongo migari ishobora gufasha umushakashatsi gusesengura no kujora ibyanditse mbere hifashishijwe ingero zifatika.Urugero rwթsesengura ryթbyanditswe mbereReka duhere ku rugero rwatanzwe na Mukama (2014, pp. 127 Р128):Imishinga yo kwiga bakoresha ikoranabuhanga҉nyigo ku mishinga yo kwiga bakoresha ikoranabuhanga yakozwe na Scheiderman (1998) mu nyandiko yashyize ahagaragara, ayita ҇usanishaРGuhangaЇutanga: uburyo bwo kwigisha/kwiga bakoresheje ikoranabuhangaӠ(Relate РCreate РDonate: a teaching/learning philosophy for the cyber-generation). Nյbwo yabyize ahereye ku burambe mu kwigisha no mu kwitegereza uko abanyeshuri be biga aho gukoresha inzira yյbushakashatsi, Scheiderman (1998, p. 25) afite umwihariko wo kugaragaza ko abanyeshuri bashobora kwiga bafatanyije mu matsinda imishinga ijyanye nյbuzima bwabo bwa buri munsi, ibategura kwinjira mu kazi kandi ishingiye ku ikoranabuhanga. Shneiderman asobanura ko umushinga wo kwiga bakoresheje ikoranabuhanga ushingiye ku ntambwe eshatu zikurikira: Gusanisha: kuri iyi ntambwe abanyeshuri bibumbira mu matsinda maze bakungurana ibitekerezo kugira ngo basobanure, bacengere kandi bumve umushinga wo kwiga bagiye gukoraho. Byongeye, bafatira hamwe gahunda yյko uwo mushinga bazawushyira mu bikorwa. Guhanga: kuri iyi ntambwe abanyeshuri bakora ubushakashatsi ku mushinga wabo, bakagerageza gushaka igisubizo umuntu ari wenyine cyangwa afatanyije nաbandi. Gutanga: aha abanyeshuri bashyikiriza umushinga bakoze ba nyiri ukuwushyira mu bikorwa cyangwa bakawuha abaturage. Morgan (1983) kimwe na Shneiderman (1998) bemeza ko kwiga bishingiye ku mishinga bihabwa agaciro nթnzira abanyeshuri banyuramo mu gukora umushinga nյmusaruro uva muri uwo murimo. Ibi biruzuzanya nյbushakashatsi bwakozwe na Mukama na Andersson (2008) aho berekana ko kugira ngo abarimu bashya bakire impinduka zibereye mu kwiga gushingiye ku ikoranabuhanga bagomba guhabwa uburyo bwo guhanga ibintu bishya nյbwo gukemura ibibazo bahura na byo mu buzima bwabo bwa buri munsi. Byongeye bagomba guhabwa umwanya wo kugaragaza ibyo bavumbura nթbyo bunguka mu kwishakira ibisubizo. Ubundi bushakashatsi bwakozwe ku kwigira kuri mudasobwa abanyeshuri bafatanyije bwerekana ko bidahagije gushyira abanyeshuri mu matsinda ngo wizere ko bazasenyera umugozi umwe mu kubaka ubumenyi bishimiye bose nkաbagize itsinda. Mercer (1995) ashishikariza abanyeshuri gukorera mu matsinda mato no kwifashisha ikiganiro gisesengura kuko ari byo bibafasha kubaka ubumenyi bafatanyije. Iki kiganiro gisaba ko ibitekerezo byյmuntu bisesengurwa, ugitanze agahabwa umwanya wo kugisobanura, abandi na bo bagashobora kukijora, kucyubakiraho cyangwa se kukivuguruza iyo bibaye ngombwa. Bityo abanyeshuri bakagenda baterana inkunga mu bitekerezo kugera aho bafatiye imyanzuro bumvikanyeho.Gukoresha imishinga yo kwiga byizweho nաbashakashatsi benshi. Urugero ni nkաho ChanLin (2008) agaragaza ko kwiga gushingiye ku mishanga bishobora gutuma abanyeshuri biyungura ubushobozi bwo gukora inshamake, ubwo kubakira ku byigwa, nյbwo gukora imirimo isaba isesengura. Aha, ChanLin avuga ko mwarimu aba afite umurimo wյbutoza kandi uyu murimo ukaba ari ingenzi mu gutuma abanyeshuri bagera ku ntego yabo. Abashakashatsi Ayas na Zeniuk (2001) bemeza ko imishinga yo kwiga ishobora gutuma abanyeshuri bahinduka abafatanyabikorwa mu bitekerezo hagati yabo. Aba bashakashatsi basobanura ko kugira ngo ubu bufatanyabikorwa bushinge imizi bugomba kuba bufite ubuyobozi buhamye kandi bwubakiye ku kemezo cya buri wese cyo gushigikira ko busugira. Naho Krajcik, Blumenfeld, Marx na Soloway (1994) bashimangira ko gukoresha ikoranabuhanga mu mishinga yo kwiga siyansi bifite imimaro myinshi harimo gutuma abanyeshuri bakemura ibibazo nyakuri bahura na byo mu buzima bwabo bwa buri munsi. Ikindi kandi iyi myigire yungura abanyeshuri ubushobozi bwo gukorera hamwe cyanecyane mu bushakashatsi bukorerwa muri laboratwari. Danford (2006) yandika ko kwiga bishingiye ku mishinga bifasha abanyeshuri kunguka ubumenyi nyakuri bukenewe mu kazi, ibigo biharanira inyungu bigashobora kubona abakozi badahenze (abanyeshuri) nթnzobere mu bumenyi runaka (abarimu). Nյbwo uburyo bwo kwiga bishingiye ku mishanga bwakoreshejwe na benshi, Hanney na Savin-Baden (2013) bemeza ko ubu buryo butaragira ihange(theory) rifatika. Basobanura ko ubu buryo butarasobanurwa ku buryo bwemewe na bose kandi ko butaragira ihangiro (framework) rimwe. Ni muri urwo rwego rero, ubu bushakashatsi bugerageza gutanga umusanzu wabwo mu kuziba icyo cyuho mu ruhando rwթkoranabuhangaӲ9.Muri uru rugero, kugira ngo umushakashatsi akore isesengura ryթbyanditswe mbere, biragaragara ko agomba kubanza gusoma ubushakashatsi bwakozwe mbere ku gitekerezo shingiro ashaka kwigaho. Ibi ni ingenzi cyane kuko bituma ubushakashatsi bugira ireme nյbwizerwe.Umumaro wթsesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbereIsesengura nթjora ni inshamake si ukurondora abakoze ubushakashatsi ngo ube wagira uti ҵyu yavuze biriya nյriya avuga biriyaӠmaze urekere aho. Ni ugucengera ibyanditswe mbere ukibaza impamvu abakoze ubwo bushakashatsi babukoze ku buryo runaka ntibabukore ukundi. Ibyo ushobora kubirebera ku iyoboramikorere (methodology); aho bwakorewe (context), ku ihangiro (theoretical framework), no ku byagezweho nյbushakashatsi (findings/results).Gusoma ubushakashatsi bwakozwe nաbandi, ukabusesengura, ukabujora kandi ukabwandika mu nshamake, bituma umushakashatsi yunguka ibitekerezo bishya ku buryo ashaka gukoramo ubushakatsatsi bwe. Byongeye, bituma ashobora kwerekana aho ubushakashatsi bwe bwuzuzanya cyangwa aho butandukanira nյbwաbandi. Mu yandi magambo, gukora isesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbere bigomba kuba bifite intego. Muri izo ntego umuntu yavuga izթngenzi zikurikira (Hart, 2001; Knopf, 2006): Kwerekana inshamake yթbyanditswe mbere ku gitekerezo shingiro kigiye kwigwaho. Iyo umushakashatsi azi ibyakozwe mbere, bituma adata umwanya yongera gushakashaka ibyarangije kuvumburwa mbere yթgihe (reinventing the wheel).  Kwerekana ibitarakozweho ubushakashatsi ku gitekerezo shingiro kigiye kwigwaho.  Kwerekana niba ubushakashatsi bwakozwe mbere bufite inenge mu ihangiro ryabwo cyangwa se mu iyoboramikorere (methodology) maze ukerekana uburyo ubugiye gukorwa kuzabifutura ku buryo bwimbitse. Kwerekana ko ubushakashatsi bugiye gukorwa buje kuziba icyuho (gap); kwibanda ku bitaritaweho (silence) cyangwa gukosora amakosa cyangwa imyumvire itari yo ku gitekerezo shingiro kizibandwaho.Kubera ko isesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbere rigaragaza imbago (limitations) ryabyo, umushakashatsi ni ho ahera yerekane umusanzu we mu bushakashatsi agiye gukora. Ashobora kuvuga icyo aje kongera ku bumenyi busanzwe buzwi cyangwa se icyo aje guhinduraho. Ni ukuvuga ko mu byյkuri ibibazo byյbushakashatsi cyangwa inkeneragihamya (hypothesis) byagombye guturuka mu isesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbere. Iyo ni yo mpamvu abashakashatsi benshi bakunda kugaragaza ibibazo byյbushakashatsi cyangwa inkeneragihamya nkաgace kagize isesengura nթjoro ryթbyanditswe mbere. Isesengura nթjora ryթbyanditse mbere rishobora gukoreshwa nkաhantu hatatu hatandukanye: Aha mbere, isesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbere rishobora kuba inyandiko yihariye kandi yihagije. Ikigamijwe aba ari nko kumva aho ubumenyi bugeze ku kibazo cyangwa ku gitekerezo shingiro runaka. Ikթngenzi si ukugaragaza amakosa yյbushakashatsi bwakozwe mbere gusa, ahubwo ni ukwerekana na none amasomo umuntu yakwigira ku byagaragajwe na bwo no ku myanzuro yabuvuyemo. Aha kabiri isesengura nթjoro ryթbyanditse mbere rikunze gukoreshwa ni aho rikorwa mu ikubitiro ryյmushinga wյbushakashatsi bashaka gukora. Urugero ni nkյbushakashatsi bukorwa nաbanyeshuri basoza amashuri makuru. Hari nյbwo iri sesengura nթjora rikorwa mu mishinga yյbushakashatsi kugira ngo iterwe inkunga yաmafaranga. Ikigamijwe ahanini muri iri sesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbere ni ukugaragaza ko ubushakashatsi bugiye gukorwa nta wundi wabukoze. Umushakashatsi aba ashaka kandi kugaragaza ko hari ikintu gishya aje kongera cyangwa guhindura mu bumenyi busanzwe buzwi. Hari nթzindi ntego umushakashatsi ashobora kuba agamije nkյko zavuzwe hejuru. Aha gatatu isesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbere rikunze gukoreshwa ni igihe barikoze nkթgice kigize raporo yյbushakashatsi bwarangiye. Akenshi na kenshi iki gice kiba kije kuzuza isesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbere ryakozwe mu mbanzirizamushinga. Iri sesengura nթjora rifasha kwerekana isano iri hagati yթmyanzuro yյbushakashatsi nյbumenyi bwari busanzwe buzwi kugeza icyo gihe.Kugaragaza umusanzu wյbushakashatsiIsesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbere riba rigamije kuvuga muri make aho ubumenyi buba bugeze ku gitekerezo shingiro muri icyo gihe umushakashatsi agiye gukora ubushakashatsi bwe. Iri sesengura nթjora kandi rifasha umushakashatsi kwerekana uruhare rwe mu kongera cyangwa mu guhindura imyumvire kuri ubwo bumenyi. Reka twifashishe urugero twabonye hejuru. Mukama (2014, p. 128) aragira ati: Nյbwo uburyo bwo kwiga bishingiye ku mishanga bwakoreshejwe na benshi, Hanney na Savin-Baden (2013) bemeza ko ubu buryo butaragira ihange (theory) rifatika. Basobanura ko ubu buryo butarasobanurwa ku buryo bwemewe na bose kandi ko butaragira ihangiro (framework) rimwe. Ni muri urwo rwego rero, ubu bushakashatsi bugerageza gutanga umusanzu wabwo mu kuziba icyo cyuho mu ruhando rwթkoranabuhanga.Muri uru rugero, Mukama arerekana ko icyuho kiri mu nyigo zakozwe mbere ari uko imyigire ishingiye ku mishinga idafite ihange nթhangiro ryemeranyijweho nաbashakashatsi. Mukama aravuga ko umuganda wյbushakashatsi bwe ari ukugira uruhare mu kurema ihange nթhangiro ryթmyigire ishingiye ku mishinga nթkoranabuhanga. Kuziba icyo cyuho ni uburyo bwo kungura ubumenyi. Ijambo ubumenyi rivugwa hano si ukuri kudakuka. Mu burezi kimwe no mu ngeri zindi zishamikiye ku bumenyi nyamuntu no ku mibanire yաbantu nաbandi, ubumenyi ni imyumvire igaragaza uko ibintu bigenda bahereye ku bushakashatsi bwakozwe. Ubwo bumenyi rero bushobora kuba bufite ikigero cyյbwizerwe (degree of confidence) runaka. Nko mu bushakashatsi bwa Mukama (2014), biragaragara ko ishuri ryթbitekerezo yubakiraho ubushakashatsi bwe ari irishingiye ku mibanire yաbantu nթmico yabo (sociocultural perspective). Ubumenyi busobanurwa hakurikijwe ishuri ryթbitekerezo (school of thought) runaka. Mu gusesengura no kujora ibyanditswe mbere, umushakashatsi rero agerageza kwibaza ku bisobanuro bitangwa nաbandi bashakashatsi nթgihamya babitangira maze akareba ko ibimenyetso batanga bifite imbaraga zihagije zo kubyemeza. Ibisobanuro kandi bishingira ku ishuri ryթbitekerezo ubushakashatsi bwakozwemo. Ubwo rero umusanzu wյmushakashatsi ushobora kugaragara mu buryo bunyuranye: ese imyumvire ku byanditswe mbere nաbashakashatsi runaka umuntu yayemera? Ese yayemera ku ruhe rwego: arayemera cyane, cyangwa se byթgice cyangwa se na none ntayemera habe na mba? Ese hari ubundi bushakashatsi bwakorwa kugira ngo ubumenyi abandi bagaragaje busobanuke neza, bwumvikane kurushaho, bukosorwe cyangwa se bwaguke? Ubushakashatsi bwakorwa bukazana ibisobanuro byisumbuye ibisanzwe, ibikosora imyumvire isanzwe iriho, ibizana imyumvire mishya itari isanzwe izwi, ibyo byose ni umusanzu mu kongera ubumenyi cyangwa imyumvire ku gitekerezo shingiro runaka. Niba hari amakuru mashya ubushakashatsi buzanye atuma urwego rwթkizere ku myumvire isanzwe izwi rwiyongera cyangwa se rugabanuka na byo ni uburyo bwo kongera ubumenyi. Uko isesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbere rikorwaKugira ngo umushakashatsi ashobore gusesengura no kujora ibyanditswe mbere ni ngombwa ko abikora kuri gahunda, ni ukuvuga ahereye ruhande kandi afite ikerekezo. Hari ingingo zթngenzi zamufasha kubigeraho: Guhitamo igitekerezo shingiro cyյbushakashatsi Gukusanya ibyanditswe mbere Kwinjira mu isesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbere Kugaragaza intego nyamukuru yյbushakashatsi Gutegura ibibazo byյbushakashatsi Kugena umwanya wթsesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbere muri raporo bushakashatsiGuhitamo igitekezezo shingiro, intego nթbibazo byյbushakashatsiUko umushakashatsi agenda acukumbura ibyanditswe mbere, ni ko agenda abona ko hari ibishobora kuba bitaranditswe ku nsanganyamatsiko ari kwigaho. Ashobora no gusanga ibyanditswe bitarasobanuye ku buryo bwimbitse ingingo runaka. Birashoboka ko ashobora no gusanga hari ingingo ikocamye noneho akiyemeza kuyigaho. Iyo rero umushakashatsi amaze kubona icyuho agiye kuziba, cyangwa se ingingo agiye gukosora, cyangwa se kuyigaho kuko itavugwa mu byanditswe mbere, yandika igitekerezo shingiro kandi agategura ibibazo byյbushakashatsi.Amagambo ҩgitekerezo shingiroӠ(research idea) akoreshejwe muri iki gitabo asobanura ikerekezo cyյbushakashatsi cyangwa se izingiro ryթbikorwa bijyanye nյbushakashatsi bugiye gukorwa. Abanyeshuri kimwe nաbandi bashaka gukora ubushakashatsi ku nshuro ya mbere bakunda kwibaza bene ibi bibazo: ҍbese nzavana he igitekerezo shingiro cyյbushakashatsi bwange?Ӡ҅se nabwirwa nթki ko ubushakashatsi nshaka gukora abandi batabukoze?ӠKwibaza ibibazo nkթki ni ingenzi. Impamvu bikenewe turayibona twifashishije ingero. Akenshi na kenshi abashakashatsi bagira igitekerezo shingiro runaka bakunda kwibandaho. Iyo usesenguye neza igitekerezo shingiro, ushobora gusanga hari ibindi bitekerezo bito bigikubiyemo. Isesengura ryթgitekerezo shingiro rituma umushakashatsi agana ku ngingo nyamukuru ubushakashatsi bwibandaho. Ni ukuvuga ko igitekerezo shingiro cyo ku rwego rwa mbere ushobora kugisesengura kikumvikana kurushaho ku rwego rwa kabiri, nթcyo ku rwego rwa kabiri kikumvikana byisumbuyeho ku rwego rwa gatatu. Iryo sesengura rirakomeza kugeza igihe umushakashatsi agereye ku ngingo nyamukuru yo kwigaho.Reka dufate urugero rwթgitekerezo shingiro cyo ku rwego rwa mbere tukite ҋuzamura ireme ryյbureziӮ Umushakashatsi ahita yibaza ati: ҅se ireme ryյburezi rireberwa hehe?ӠAbashakashatsi bamwe bashobora guhita batekereza ibikorwa kugira ngo ireme ryյburezi ribeho. Ingero: guhugura abarimu, guhuza integanyanyigisho nթsoko ryյmurimo, politiki yյburezi, imiyoborere myiza yաmashuri, igenamigambi nթmicungire yթmari, imyigire yաbanyeshuri, imyigishishirize yաbarimu nթbindi. Abandi bashakashatsi bashobora gutekereza ko ireme ryյburezi rigaragarira mu ngaruka zյko uburezi buhagaze. Ingero: abakozi bakora akazi kinyamwuga, umusaruro wյmukozi warangije kwiga, iterambere ryթgihugu, ubushobozi bwo gukemura ibibazo byաbaturage, ihangwa ryթmirimo ugereranyije nթbyo abanyeshuri bize nթbindi. Ireme ryյburezi rero ni igitekerezo cyo ku rwego rwa mbere. Impamvu zitera ireme ryյburezi nյmusaruro wյburezi bufite ireme biragaragaza igitekerezo shingiro cyo ku rwego rwa kabiri.Ku rwego rwa kabiri, buri gitekerezo shingiro muri ibyo tumaze kuvuga haruguru, na cyo gishobora gusesengurwa kikavamo ibindi bitekerezo shingiro bito birushijeho gusobanuka. Reka dufate urugero rwթgitekerezo shingiro twavuze haruguru ku rwego rwa kabiri ҩmyigire yաbanyeshuriӮ Nkյko tuzabibona mu gice cyթkusanyamakuru nթsesenguramakuru, iyo agiye gukora ubushakashatsi, umushakashatsi yibaza ibibazo bibiri byթngenzi mu bushakashatsi bwյbumenyi nyamuntu nթmibanire yաbantu: ҩki?Ӡna ҧute?Ӡ(what and how). Mu gusesengura igitekerezo shingiro ҩmyigire yաbanyeshuriӬ umushakashatsi ashobora kwibaza ati: Ҏi iki kigwa cyangwa se ni nde wiga?Ӡҕmunyeshuri yiga ate?ӠIbyo bibazo rero bishobora gutuma umushakashatsi yibanda kuri bimwe muri ibi bitekerezo shingiro bigaragaza imyigire yաbanyeshuri: gukoresha ikoranabuhanga mu kwiga, kwiga ibiteganyijwe mu nteganyanyishisho, ikoreshwa ryթmfashanyigisho mu kwiga, imikoreshereze yյrurimi rwաmahanga mu myigire, ibaza nթbazwa, ubufasha bwաbarimu mu kwiga cyangwa mu kwiyigisha, ubufatanye hagati yաbanyeshuri, ingaruka zo kurya cyangwa kutarya saa sita mu myigire yաbana, gutsinda no gutsindwa, kuba umuhungu/kuba umukobwa mu myigire yթkoranabuhanga na siyansi, uruhare rwաbabyeyi mu myigire, kwigana nաbanyeshuri benshi/bake, kwiga isomo ryihariye (kubara, gusoma, inyunguramagambo, ikibonezamvugoɩ nթbindi. Iri sesengura ryթmyigire yաbanyeshuri riragaragaza ibitekerezo shingiro byo ku rwego rwa gatatu. Rirerekana ko ikigwa kigenda gisobanuka kurusha ibindi bitekerezo shingiro byabanje.Buri gitekerezo shingiro tumaze kuvuga ku rwego rwa gatatu na cyo gishobora gusesengurwamo ibindi bito kurushaho kugeza ubwo umushakashatsi agera ku ngingo ashaka kwigaho ku buryo ugisoma na we ashobora kwiyumvisha ko gikorwa mu gihe runaka, mu buryo runaka, ahantu runaka nաbantu runaka. Igishushanyombonerahamwe 1 kirerekana uburyo igitekerezo shingiro kimwe gishobora gusesengurwamo ibindi bito byinshi bigishamikiyeho.Gukusanya ibyanditswe mbereUmushakashatsi akora umurimo wo gushakisha no kwegeranya ibyanditswe mbere yifashishije amagambo yթngenzi (keywords) avanye mu gitekerezo shingiro. Nko mu rugero rwթgitekerezo shingiro ҫwiga gushingiye ku mishinga nթkoranabuhangaӮ Amagambo yթngenzi ari muri iki gitekerezo shingiro ni abiri: ҋwiga gushingiye ku mishingaӠndetse nՠҩkoranabuhangaӮ Muri ibi bihe tugezemo, amasomero menshi asigaye akoresha ikoranabuhanga mu itumanaho nթsakazabumenyi. Umuntu ashobora kwifashisha murandasi agashakisha inyandiko zashyizwe ahagaragara yifashishije amagambo yթngenzi ari mu gitekerezo shingiro cyյbushakashatsi. Iyo ayo magambo yթngenzi ayanditse mu mashakiro akoresha iryo koranabuhanga, ashobora guhita abona raporo zյbushakashatsi bwashyizwe ahagaragara buhuriye kuri icyo gitekerezo shingiro. Kugeza magingo aya ariko, ibyanditswe mbere byinshi biri mu rurimi rwթcyongereza. Niba ntabyanditswe mbere mu rurimi rwթkinyarwanda biri mu bubiko bwa 	Urwego 1	Urwego 2	Urwego 3	Urwego 4	Urwego 5	Urwego 6Ikoranabuhanga nյmuco wթgihuguKwigira kuri mudasobwa imwe abana ari benshi mu itsindaPolitiki yյburezi	Gukoresha imfashanyigishoImiyoborere yթshuriUrurimi rwաmahanga Igenamigambimu kwiga  Imyigire Kurya/Kutarya yաbanyeshuriku ishuri mu   myigire yաbanyeshuriIreme ryյbureziImyigishirize yաbarimuIbaza nթbazwaUbushobozi bwյmukozi Gukoresha 	ukirangiza kwiga	ikoranabuhanga Ubufatanye mu kwiganաbandi mu   iyakure Uruhare rwաbarangije Kuba kwiga mu umuhungu/Gushaka no iterambere umukobwa mu gusobanukirwa ryթgihugumyigire amakuru yo kuri murandasiUbushobozi bwo 	Uruhare kwihangira akazi 	rwաbabyeyiKwigira isomo ku barangije runaka kuri kwigaKwigana mudasobwanաbayeshuri benshi/bake mu Kwiga uri Kwiga ufatanyije ishuri rimwewenyine nաbandi buri ukoresheje wese akoresha Kwiga isomo telefoni telefoni 	(imibare, igendanywaigendanywa	Uko abanyeshuri lcyongereza, bahanga ubumenyi ibidukikije ɩ	Kwiga ufatanyije 	Kwiga bishingiye  bushya mu myigire 	nաbandi ku mishinga 	ishingiye ku  bakoresha nթkorana- mishinga ikoranabuhangabuhanga nթkoranabuhangaIgishushanyo-mbonerahamwe 1:  Uburyo bwo gusesengura igitekerezo shingiro cyյbushakashatsimurandasi byaba byiza umushakashatsi abishatse nko mu cyongereza cyangwa mu zindi ndimi mpuzamahanga. Mu cyongereza, ayo magambo yթngenzi azaba aya akurikira: Ұroject-based learningӠ+ ҴechnologyӠniba umushakashatsi ashaka kubona amakuru ku bushakashatsi bwakozwe mbere ku ҭyigire ishingiye ku mishinga nթkoranabuhangaӮHari ubwo umushakashatsi ashobora gukoresha amagambo yթngenzi abiri cyangwa se atatu ariko akabona ibyanditswe mbere bike cyane. Icyo gihe ashobora kwagura ishakisha. Urugero: niba mbere yari yakoresheje amagambo yթngenzi abiri, ashobora kuyagabanya akandika rimwe ҵbushakashatsi bushingiye ku mishingaӮ Aha abona ibyanditswe byinshi kurusha mbere kuko araba ashatse ibyanditswe mbere ku ҭyigire ishingiye ku mishingaӠbitarimo ҩkoranabuhangaӠgusa. Iyo noneho mu ishakisha akoze abonye ibyanditswe mbere byinshi cyane, biba ngombwa ko agabanya ubunini bwթgitekerezo shingiro. Niba igitekerezo shingiro cya mbere cyari ҩmyigire ishingiye ku mishinga nթkoranabuhangaӬ ashobora kuyihindura atya ҵko abanyeshuri bahanga ubumenyi bushya mu myigire ishingiye ku mishinga nթkoranabuhangaӮ Ubwo amagambo yթngenzi ariyongera: ҧuhanga ubumenyi+imyigire ishingiye ku mushinga+ikoranabuhangaӮ Mu cyongereza amagambo yթngenzi yaba aya akurikira: ҫnowledge construction+project based learning+technologyӮ Ibyanditswe mbere biraba birimo ubushakashatsi bwakozwe burimo uko ubumenyi bwubakwa, imyigire ishingiye ku mishinga nթkoranabuhanga. Mu gukusanya ibyanditswe mbere, umushakashatsi akwiye kwita kuri izi ngingo: Ibyanditse mbere bikwiye gutoranywa mu bushakashatsi bwarangiye kandi bwashyizwe ahagaragara. Ibyanditswe mbere bishobora kuba ari ibitabo, igice kimwe cyangwa se byinshi mu bigize igitabo (book chapters); ubushakashatsi bwashyizwe ahagaragara mu bitangazamakuru byյbumenyi bwasomwe kandi bukemezwa nաbahanga (peer reviewed journals), inkoranyamagambo, raporo zյbushakashatsi bwashyizwe ahagararaga nkթbitabo birangiza amashuri makuru nթbindi. Cyakora hari ubwo umushakashatsi ashobora kwifashisha raporo zյbushakashatsi bwarangiye ariko zitarashyirwa ahagaragara iyo izo raporo zizewe rwose. Biba byiza gukoresha ibyanditswe mbere nաbashakashatsi bafite ubunararibonye ku gitekerezo shingiro runaka. Ibi byongererera agaciro ubushakashatsi burimo gukorwa.  Umuyobozi wյbushakashatsi ashobora kugira inama abanyeshuri be zաho bashakira ibyanditswe mbere byizewe.  Ni ngombwa cyane gukoresha ibyanditswe mbere bishya kubera ko ubushakashatsi bwubakira ku bundi kandi bugahora buhinduka. Kimwe mu byafasha kumenya ubushakashatsi bushya ni nko kwitabira inama zյbushakashatsi, zaba izihuza abashakashatsi bake cyangwa se benshi mu mashuri makuru, mu gihugu imbere cyangwa se ku rwego mpuzamahanga. Cyakora hari aho biba bikenewe ko umushakashatsi akoresha ibyanditswe mbere bya kera nko mu nyigo zաmateka, cyangwa se ashaka kwerekana isoko muzi yթgitekerezo runaka. Umushakashatsi ashobora kwifashisha indangasoko yյbushakashatsi bwashyizwe ahagaragara. Ibyo bishobora kumufasha kumenya abandi bashakashatsi banditse ku gitekerezo shingiro na we ashaka kwigaho.Ese umushakashatsi yakusanya ibyanditswe mbere kugeza ryari? Mu gihe umushakashatsi akibona andi makuru mashya cyangwa se izindi ngingo nsha zivuguruzanya ku gitekerezo shingiro ke, akomeza gushaka ibyanditswe mbere. Ariko mu gihe nta gishya akibona, icyo gihe ntaba agikeneye gukomeza gukusanya ibindi byanditswe mbere. Cyakora ibyagezweho nյbushakashatsi bishobora gutuma akenera kongera gushaka andi makuru mu byanditswe mbere kugira ngo arusheho kubyumva no kubisobanura. Iyi ngingo tuzayigarukaho mu gice kթyoboramikorere / iyoboranzira.Kwinjira mu isesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbereGusesengura ibyanditswe mbere ni umurimo wo gucukumbura amakuru ariko kandi bigakorwa kuri gahunda. Gucukumbura amakuru ntibigenda umujyo umwe ngo ube wakwibwira ko ikibazo ubonye mu nyandiko ya mbere usanga igisubizo cyacyo mu nyandiko ikurikiyeho. Ahubwo ushobora gusanga igitekerezo cyatanzwe nյmushakashatsi umwe gifitanye isano nթnyandiko yarondoye mu ndangasoko. Icyo gihe ushobora guhita ujya gushaka izo nyandiko ukaba uretse gusoma izindi wari wateguye. Ku rundi ruhande ni ngombwa ko umushakashatsi asoma ibyanditswe mbere kuri gahunda. Iyi gahunda tuvuga hano ni iyo kumenya uko yandika ibitekerezo byթngenzi yagiye asanga muri buri nyandiko. Mbere na mbere, byaba byiza umushakashatsi abanje gusoma inshamake (abstract) yթnyandiko agiye gusoma kugira ngo ashobore guhitamo izifite aho zihuriye rwose nթnsanganyamatsiko ashaka kwigaho. Ibyo bimurinda kandi guta umwanya no gusoma ibyo abonye byose. Mu gusoma rero inyandiko yatoranyijwe, hari abashakashatsi bakunda guca imirongo ku gika babonyemo igitekerezo kibashishikaje ku buryo mu gihe cyo kwandika bazakigarukaho. Akenshi aba bakunda kwifashisha ikaramu yթgiti cyanecyane iyo baca imirongo mu gitabo kugira ngo nibiba ngombwa bazayisibe. Hari abahitamo gukora inshamake yթgitekerezo nyamukuru kivugwa mu nyandiko bamaze gusoma. Ibi bishobora kubafasha kugenda basesengura kandi bajora buri nyandiko. Dore bimwe mu bibazo bishobora kuyobora umushakashatsi mu gusesengura no kujora ibyanditswe mbere kuri gahunda:  Ese ibibazo ubu bushakashatsi bwashakaga gusubiza ni ibihe? Byarasubijwe se? Ese aho ubushakashatsi bwabereye ni hamwe cyangwa se haratandukanye?  Ese iyoboramikorere / iyoboranzira hari aho rihuriye nթryakoreshejwe mu bundi bushakashatsi?  Ese ibyagezweho nյbushakashatsi biravuga iki? Ese imyanzuro yյbushakashatsi hari aho ihuriye nթyanditswe mu nyandiko zasomwe mbere? Ese iruzuzanya cyangwa irabusanye?  Ni uwuhe mwanzuro cyangwa se ni iki gishya ubushakashatsi bwazanye mu bumenyi? Ni iki kitavugwa muri ubu bushakashatsi? Ni iki gishobora gukosorwa muri ubu bushakashatsi?Kwibaza no kwisubiza bene ibi bibazo mu gihe umushakashatsi asoma ibyanditswe mbere bituma ashobora kubisesengura no kubijora. Umushakashatsi rero ashobora kwandika inshamake yթsesengura nթjora kuri buri nyandiko yյbushakashatsi asomye mu byanditswe mbere akurikije ibyo bibazo byo hejuru. Ibi bituma umushakashatsi atibagirwa ibyo yasomye kandi bimufasha kugereranya ibyanditswe mbere uko agenda abisoma. Cyakora nta tegeko ntakuka ririho rivuga intambwe ku yindi uko umushakashatsi agenda akusanya ibitekerezo asoma mu byanditswe mbere. Buri mushakashatsi ashobora gukoresha uburyo bumunogeye. Icyo umushakashatsi atagomba kwibagirwa ni ukwandika isoko yաho yakuye amakuru: umwanditsi, umwaka, umutwe wթnyandiko ye, igitabo/igitangazamakuru cyյbushakashatsi, nimero yթgitangazamakuru, nimero yթcapwa, amapaji inyandiko iherereyeho. Niba ari igitabo, agomba kugaragaza izina ryթcapiro nյmugi cyacapiwemo. Mbere yo kwandika isesengura ryթbyanditswe mbere byaba byiza umushakashatsi, cyanecyane ku mutangizi, abanje gusoma izindi nyigo zakozwe nաbandi bashakashatsi kugira ngo acengere uko bakoze uwo murimo. Byaba byiza kandi umushakashatsi wյmutangizi agishije inama abayobozi bյbushakashatsi bwe kugira ngo bamubwire inyigo zifite isesengura nթjora ryթbyakozwe mbere bafata nkթntangarugero.Si ngombwa ko ibyasomwe byose bigaragara mu isesengura ryթbyanditswe mbere. Iri sesengura rigomba kuba ririmo amakuru afitanye isano nյbushakashatsi buri gukorwa kandi agomba kuba hari icyo yungura mu kubwumva no kubusobanura. Mu yandi magambo, isesengura ryթbyanditswe mbere rigaragaza imyumvire ivugwa mu bushakashatsi ku gitekerezo shingiro. Imyumvire isa igomba kubumbirwa mu bika byegeranye. Umushakashatsi ashobora no kwerekana aho imyumvire yasomye mu nyandiko imwe bibusanira nթyanditswe mu zindi nyandiko. Ni ngombwa kwerekana ibyibagiranye cyangwa ibitavugwa ariko hagamijwe gusobanura uko ubushakashatsi bugiye gukorwa buje kuziba icyo cyuho (Vithal & Jansen, 1997). Aha ni ho umushakashatsi ahera asobanura igishya ubushakashatsi bwe buje kongera mu bumenyi busanzwe buzwi.Kugaragaza intego nyamukuru yյbushakashashatsiIgitekerezo shingiro gito ni cyo umushakashatsi aheraho kugira ngo agaragaze intego nyamukuru ashaka kugeraho mu bushakashatsi bwe. Igitekerezo shingiro gito kigaragara mu Gishushanyo-mbonerahamwe 1 ni ҋwiga gushingiye ku mishinga nթkoranabuhangaӮ Dore rero imwe mu mpamvu nyamukuru umushakashatsi ashobora kugenderaho:Urugero 1: Impamvu nyamukuru yյbu bushakashatsi ni ugusesengura uko abanyeshuri bahanga ubumenyi bushya mu myigire ishingiye ku mishinga nթkoranabuhangaMuri iyi mpamvu nyamukuru yյbushakashatsi hari ingingo zթngenzi ziyigize: Inshinga igaragaza igikorwa cyյbushakashatsi: ҧusesenguraӮ Iyo nshinga yerekana imiterere yյbushakashatsi. Hari ubushakashatsi bushingiye ku miterere yթbintu cyangwa se imimerere yabyo, iyiga nyamimerere/ nsesengurabitekerezo (qualitative studies). Hari nաbandi bakora ubushakashatsi bushingiye ku ibarura ryթbintu cyangwa ingano yabyo mu mibare, iyiga barurishamibare (quantitative studies). Ibyo bikorwa byose bishobora kugaragazwa nթnshinga yakoreshejwe mu mpamvu nyamukuru. Ingezo zթnshinga zishobora gukoreshwa mu iyiga nyamimerere: kwiga, gusobanura, kugaragaza isano nթzindi. Ingero zթnshinga zishobora kugaragaza ubushakashatsi bushingiye ku iyiga barurishamibare: kubarura, kugereranya, nթzindi.  Igikorwaho ubushakashatsi (Object): ҵko abanyeshuri bahanga ubumenyi bushyaӮ Ikigwa kiragaragazwa nթgisubizo kթkibazo: ҩki?ӍAbafite uruhare mu bushakashatsi (participants/subjects): ҡbanyeshuriӮ Abatanga amakuru yյbushakashatsi baravugwa. Aho ubushakashatsi bubera (context): ҭu myigire ishingiye ku mishinga nթkoranabuhangaӮ Ni igisubizo kuri cya kibazo: ubushakashatsi burabera hehe? Mu mpamvu nyamukuru, birumvikana ko abanyeshuri bahanga ubumenyi bushya mu buryo bwihariye bubera mu ҭyigire ishingiye ku mishinga nթkoranabuhangaӮ Akenshi na kenshi, impamvu nyamukuru yյbushakashatsi iba ari imwe. Cyakora hari ubwo usanga hari abashakashatsi bagaragaje impamvu nyamukuru nkեbyiri cyangwa eshatu nյbwo atari benshi babikora batyo.Dore izindi ngero zigaragaza impamvu nyamukuru yյbushakashatsi:Urugero 2: Impamvu nyamukuru yյbu bushakashatsi ni ugusobanura ibitekerezo byաbanyeshuri bo mu mashuri makuru ku myigire yabo yթyakure.Urugero 3: Impamvu nyamukuru yյbu bushakashatsi ni ukugereranya ubwitabire bwաbakobwa nաbahungu mu mashami ya siyansi mu mashuri yisumbuye.Ikitonderwa: Inshinga zose zigaragaza igikorwa si ko zikoreshwa mu kwandika impamvu nyamukuru yյbushakashatsi. Рɠgusura amashuri yաbikorera ku giti cyabo.Inshinga ҧusuraӠnթzindi nko ҫuvugaӬ ҧusaruraӠntabwo zerekana igikorwa cyյbushakashatsi. Ntabwo zigaragaza cyangwa ngo zisubize cya kibazo shingiro cyյbushakashatsi: ni ibiki bibera hano? Biri gukorwa gute? Inshinga yakoreshejwe igomba kumvikanisha ku buryo busobanutse igikorwa cyյbushakashatsi atari ukubishakisha. Urugero: ese iyo minisitiri wյburezi asuye ishuri, ikiba kimujyanye ni ugusura ishuri gusa cyangwa se agirana ibiganiro nաbayobozi baryo ndetse nաbanyeshuri? Uko ni ugushakisha.Impamvu nyamukuru yյbushakashatsi ntigomba kugaragaza mbere yթgihe umwanzuro: Рɠkugaragaza ko kwiga imibare bikomera. Impamvu nyamukuru yյbushakashatsi ntigomba gutanga ibisobanuro byթgikorwa, uko gikorwa nաbagikora. Ntigomba kandi kugaragaza ibibazo byյbushakashatsi:Рɠkwiga imitsindire yաbanyeshuri bաbanyarwanda barya gatatu ku munsi, mu gitondo, saa sita na nimugoroba mu masomo yթbinyabuzima atangirwa aho inyamaswa zituye.Gutegura ibibazo byյbushakashatsiIyo umushakashatsi amaze kubona igitekerezo shingiro nթntego nyamukuru byյbushakashatsi bwe, aba ashobora noneho gutegura ibibazo byյbushakashatsi. Ibyo bibazo bigaragaza ingingo zթngenzi zikubiye mu ntego nyamuru. Reka twifashishe ingero zifatika nթntego nyamukuru byubakiyeho.Intego nyamukuruImpamvu nyamukuru yյbu bushakashatsi ni ugusesengura uko abanyeshuri bahanga ubumenyi bushya mu myigire ishingiye ku mishinga nթkoranabuhanga.Ibibazo byյbushakashatsi Ni ubuhe bufasha umunyeshuri akenera kugira ngo yibande ku kigwa mu myigire ishingiye ku mishanga nթkoranabuhanga? Ese gutekereza ku myigire yabo ishingiye ku mishinga nթkoranabuhanga bifasha iki abanyeshuri mu kunguka ubumenyi bushya?  Abanyeshuri bafatanya bate mu guhanga ubumenyi bushya mu myigire ishingiye ku mishanga nթkoranabuhanga? Iyo witegereje neza ibi bibazo uko ari bitatu, usanga hari ibyangombwa byujuje kugira ngo byitwe ibibazo byյbushakashatsi: Ibyo bibazo byose uko ari bitatu bifitanye isano nթntego nyamukuru yյbushakashatsi. Bigamije gusesengura iyo ntego.Ibyo bibazo uko ari bitatu bifitanye isano kandi hari amagambo yթngenzi bihuriyeho. Urugero, ibi bibazo bihuriye ku ҭyigire ishingiye ku ikoranabuhangaӮ Buri kibazo gishobora kwigwaho no gushakirwa igisubizo ku giti cyacyo. Buri kibazo kandi kirihagije kandi amakuru gitanga ntaba asubiza ibindi bibazo bitandukanye nթcyo nyine.Birashoboka ko umuntu ashobora kubaza ibibazo byinshi byյbushakashatsi ariko mu rwego rwo gushyiraho imbago zյbushakashatsi byaba byiza umushakashatsi abajije ibibazo byյbushakashatsi bitatu gusa. Cyakora ibyo si itegeko. Kwiga ku ngingo nkeya zisobanutse bituma umushakashatsi azicukumbura ku buryo bwimbitse. Umwanya wթsesengura ryթbyanditswe mbere muri raporo bushakashatsiNkյko umusomyi ashobora kubyibonera ubwe mu bitangazamakuru byյbushakashatsi, raporo zյbushakashatsi mu binyamakuru byյbushakashatsi zikunze kugabanywamo ibice bikurikira: Iriburiro akenshi na kenshi usanga rikubiyemo imvo nթmvano, impamvu nyamukuru nթntego zյbushakashatsi Isesengura ryթbyanditswe mbere Iyoboramikorere / iyoboranzira (ikusanyamakuru nթsesenguramakuru) Ibyagezweho nյbushakashatsi Isobanura bwite (discussion) UmwanzuroIgice kթsesengura ryթbyanditswe mbere gifite umwanya wթbanze kuko aba ari nkյmusingi ibindi bice byose byubakiyeho. Nյbwo ari igice kihariye, hari ubwo usanga isesengura nթjora ryթbyanditswe mbere riza no mu iyoboramikorere. Icyo gihe umushakashatsi ashobora kuba agamije kwerekana urwego rwթmikorere (paradigm) runaka nթmpamvu ari rwo yahisemo gukoresha. Ashobora ndetse no kugaragaza uko abandi bashakashatsi bakoresheje iyoboramikorere yahisemo, imbaraga nթntege nke zaryo. Ikindi kandi, ashobora kwerekana uko ubushakashatsi bwe buzakemura icyuho gishobora kuba kiri mu iyoboramikorere yashyize imbere.UmwanzuroGusesengura no kujora ibyanditswe mbere ni umurimo usaba kuvuga muri make ibitekerezo byթngenzi bikubiye mu nyandiko zinyuranye zյbushakashatsi ku gitekerezo shingiro runaka. Uwo murimo usaba kugereranya no gucengera ingingo zashingiweho nաbashakashatsi kugira ngo bagere ku myanzuro yabo. Ni umurimo usaba gupfundura ingingo zapfunditswe nաbandi kugira ngo rirusheho kumvikana, gusesengurwa no kujorwa. Ibyo byose umushakashatsi abikora atagamije kwerekana aho ubushakashatsi bwe buhurira nյbwakozwe mbere gusa, ahubwo aba ashishikajwe cyanecyane no kwerekana igishya agiye kongera ku bumenyi busanzwe buzwi ku gitekerezo shingiro runaka. IndangasokoHart, C. (2001). Doing a literature search: A comprehensive guide for the social sciences. London: Sage Publishing.Knopf, W. J. (2006). Doing a literature review. PS: Political Science and Politics, 39(1), 127 Р132. Mukama, E. (2014). Bringing technology to studentsՠproximity: a sociocultural account of technology-based learning projects. International Journal for Research in Vocational Education and Training, 1(2), 125 Р142.Vithal, R., & Jansen, J. (1997). Designing your first proposal. Lansdowne, Cape Town: Juta & Company Ltd.UMUTWE 6 GUTORANYA ITSINDA NKESHWAMAKURUEvode Mukama, Anne Marie Kagwesage, Dieudonne Uwizeye na Jean Baptiste NdikubwimanaIriburiroKugira ngo ubushakashatsi mu bumenyi nyamuntu no mu mibanire yաbantu bugire ireme, ni ngombwa ko amakuru atanzwe aba yavuye ku bantu bayafite kandi akaba yizewe. Guteganya uko uzatoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru (sampling) bikorwa kare, mu gihe cyo gutegura umushinga wյbushakashatsi. Byongeye, umushakashatsi agomba kumenya ibiranga itsinda nshingirwaho (population) rigizwe nաbantu cyangwa ibintu bitoranywamo itsinda nkeshwamakuru (sample). Zimwe mu mpamvu zituma umushakashatsi ahitamo itsinda nkeshwamakuru, aho gutara amakuru ku bantu bose bayafite, harimo ubushobozi, ari ubwթmari cyangwa ubwյmwanya, cyangwa se ubwo kugera kuri buri mutangamakuru wese aho ahererereye hose. Itsinda nkeshwamakuru rero ni ikoraniro ryաbantu bake (ibintu bike) ritoranywa mu itsinda nshingirwaho rigizwe nաbantu benshi (ibintu byinshi) bahuje ibirango kugira ngo batange amakuru ku nsanganyamatsiko runaka yigwaho. Uyu mutwe wթki gitabo ugiye kwibanda ku buryo bwo gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru no guhitamo ingano yaryo.Uburyo bwo gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuruAbashakashatsi nka Cohen, Manion na Morrison (2000), Carlson na Hyde (2003), Kombo na Tromp (2006), Bryman (2008) hamwe na Kellstedt na Whitten (2013) bemeza ko habaho uburyo bubiri bwթngenzi bwo gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru: irishingiye kuri tombora (probability sample) nթrishingiye ku guhitamo (nonprobability sample). Mu itsinda nkeshwamakuru rya tombora buri muntu wese wo mu itsinda nshingirwaho aba afite amahirwe angana nաya mugenzi we yo gutoranywa. Ni yo mpamvu turyita tombora kuko buri wese tombora ishobora kumugwaho. Naho mu itsinda nkeshwamakuru rishingiye ku guhitamo (baryita kandi itsinda nkeshwamakuru rishingiye ku mpamvu), igice kimwe cyաbantu bagize itsinda nshingirwaho bagihitamo, ikindi gice bakakireka kubera impamvu runaka. Buri wese ntabwo aba afite amahirwe angana nաya mugenzi we mu gutoranywa. Tugiye kureba uko batoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru muri ubwo buryo bwombi.Amatsinda nkeshwamakuru ya tombora (Probability samples)Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru mu buryo bwa tombora bikoreshwa cyanecyane iyo umushakashatsi ashaka kwitirira ibyavuye mu bushakashatsi abantu bose bahuje ibirango nաbatanze amakuru (generalization). Ni ukuvuga ko itsinda nkeshwamakuru rigomba kuba rihagarariye abantu bose bahuje ibirango ari bo twise itsinda nshingirwaho (population). Buri muntu wese ugize itsinda nkeshwamakuru rya tombora aba yatoranyijwe ku bwաmahirwe, bigendeye gusa ko ari muri iryo tsinda nshingirwaho. Habaho ubwoko butandukanye bwթtsinda nkeshwamakuru rya tombora nkյko tugiye kubibona mu bika bikurikiyeho.Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru rishingiye kuri tombora yoroheje (Simple random sampling)Reka duhere ku rugero. Turashaka gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryաbanyeshuri 80 mu itsinda nshingirwaho ryաbanyeshuri 100. Dushobora kwandika ku gapapuro izina rya buri munyeshuri muri abo 100 maze tukadushyira mu nkangara tuvangavanze. Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryաbanyeshuri ku buryo bwa tombora yoroheje birasaba kuvana muri iyo nkangara udupapuro tungana nյmubare dukeneye muri iryo tsinda ari wo 80. Kugira ngo ibi bishoboke, bisaba ko umushakashatsi aba afite urutonde rwաbagize itsinda nshingirwaho bose. Iyi ishobora kuba imwe mu mbogamizi zo gukoresha itsinda nkeshwamakuru rishingiye kuri tombora yoroheje kuko hari ubwo gukora urutonde rwաbaturage bose bagize itsinda nshingirwaho bigorana.Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru rya gahunda (Systematic sampling)Ubu ruryo bwo gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru rya gahunda busaba ko habanza gukorwa urutonde rwթtsinda nshingirwaho noneho buri muntu agahabwa nimero. Urugero: umushakashatsi akeneye gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru rigizwe nաbanyeshuri 25 mu rutonde rwթtsinda nshingirwaho ryաbanyeshuri 100. Buri munyeshuri wa kane ashobora gutoranywa akajya mu itsinda nkeshwamakuru. Dore uko ushobora kumenya umubare uhitamo kuri gahunda:f = snN f = Intera N = Umubare wաbaturage bose bagize itsinda nshingirwaho sn = Umubare wաbantu bagize itsinda nkeshwamakuruMuri urwo rugero twatanze hejuru, kugira ngo umenye intera ( f ) ufatiraho umuntu ushyira mu itsinda nkeshwamakuru wabikora utya: = 4Ni ukuvuga ko buri munyeshuri wa kane atoranywa akajya mu itsinda nkeshwamakuru rya gahunda. Kugira ngo abakobwa nաbahungu bagaragare mu itsinda nkeshwamakuru, byaba byiza ubanje gutondeka abakobwa bose hamwe, ukabona gukurikizaho abahungu. Nյbwo baba bakurikiranye ari abakobwa ukwabo nաbahungu ukwabo, urwo rutonde rukorwa ku buryo bwa tombora, kandi umuntu wa mbere uheraho mu gutangira gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru rya gahunda atoranywa na we kuri ubwo buryo bwa tombora. Ibi bituma buri muntu wese akomeza kugira amahirwe yo gutoranywa angana nաya mugenzi we ariko bikozwe kuri gahunda.Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryաmatsinda ahuje ibirango (Stratified sampling)Duhere ku rugero rwյmushakashatsi ushaka kwiga imyumvire yաbanyeshuri bo mu mashuri yisumbuye ku ruhare rwյrubyiruko mu kwihangira imirimo. Icyo gihe itsinda nshingirwaho ni abanyeshuri bo mu mashuri yisumbuye. Umushakashatsi ashobora rero kubashyira mu matsinda atandukanye akurikije icyo bahuriyeho. Urugero: itsinda ryաbakobwa nթryաbahungu. Aya matsinda yombi agomba kuba na none ahuje ibirango nթtsinda nshingirwaho: ari abakobwa ari nաbahungu bahuriye kuba bose ari abanyeshuri bo mu mashuri yisumbuye. Byongeye, buri tsinda rifite ikirango ryihariye rihuje: kuba bamwe ari igitsina gore abandi ari igitsina gabo. Aha ni ho twahereye tuyita amatsinda ahuje ibirango. Niba rero umushakashatsi amaze kumenya ingano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru, ashobora kwemeza umubare wաbanyeshuri akeneye muri buri tsinda rihuje ibirango noneho akabatoranya ku buryo bwa tombora cyangwa se kuri gahunda nkյko twabisobanuye mu gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru rishingiye kuri tombora yoroheje cyangwa ku rishingiye kuri gahunda. Mu kwemeza ibirango ngenderwaho mu kurema amatsinda ahuje ibirango, Cohen, Manion na Morrison (2000) bagira inama abashakashatsi yo gufata ibirango bike kuko byoroshya gukora itsinda nkeshwamakuru no gusesengura amakuru.Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru rishingiye ku dutsiko twաhantu (Cluster sampling)Dufate urugero rwյmushakashatsi ushaka kwiga uko abanyarwanda bafatanya mu guhangana nթngaruka zթbiza. Tuzi ko abagezweho nթngaruka zթbiza ari abantu benshi kandi banyanyagiye hirya no hino mu gihugu. Aha rero, umushakashatsi ashobora guhitamo umubare runaka wյduce tumwe twթgihugu (urugero: utugari cyangwa se imirenge), maze agakora ubushakashatsi ku itsinda ryաbagezweho nթbiza bose bo muri utwo duce (clusters). Bene ubu bushakashatsi bukorerwa ahantu hato bukunze gukorwa cyane kabone nթyo ikibazo kigwa kiba kiri ahantu hagari. Ntibizagutangaze rero ko ushobora kubona abashakashatsi bakora ubushakashatsi mu duce runaka kandi ubusanzwe icyo bigaho kibera mu gihugu hose. Ibi bikunze kugaragara nko mu bushakashatsi bukorerwa mu mashuri.Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryթbyiciro (Stage sampling)Itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryթbyiciro ni nkթgice kisumbuyeho ku itsinda nkeshwamakuru rishingiye ku duce twաhantu. Mu yandi magambo, umushakashatsi atoranya ku buryo bwa tombora ibice bike bizakorerwamo ubushakashatsi mu hantu hagari; noneho muri ibyo bice, agatoranyamo ibindi bice bito kurushaho, no muri ibyo bice bito agatoranyamo abantu akeneye gukoraho ubushakashatsi. Ibyo byose bigakorwa ku buryo bwa tombora. Duhereye ku rugero twatanze haruguru rwյmushakashatsi ushaka kwiga uko abanyarwanda bafatanya mu guhangana nթngaruka zթbiza, ashobora guhitamo akarere kamwe kabayemo ibiza muri buri ntara. No muri utwo turere yahisemo, ashobora gutoranyamo imirenge ibiri; muri buri murenge agatoranyamo utugari tubiri. Hanyuma muri utwo tugari ashobora gutoranyamo umubare runaka wաbantu bagezweho nթngaruka zթbiza. Ikigamijwe ni ukugera ku mubare runaka wաbantu bagezweho nթngaruka zթbiza mu gace kաhantu runaka. Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryթbyiciro binyuranye  (Multi-stage cluster sampling)Mu rugero tumaze kuvuga hejuru rwյmushakashatsi ushaka kwiga uko abanyarwanda bafatanya mu guhangana nթngaruka zթbiza, mu kiciro cya mbere yabanje gutoranya uduce twթgihugu bahereyemo (clusters). Mu kiciro cya kabiri ahitamo abantu bagezweho nթngaruka zթbiza. Mu kiciro cya gatatu ashobora kubahitamo ahereye ku byiciro byյbudehe bigaragaza ubukungu bwa buri muntu. Mu kiciro cya kane ashobora kubahitamo ahereye ku mashuri bize, gutyo gutyo. Mu yandi magambo, impamvu yo guhitamo itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryթbyiciro binyuranye kuri buri kiciro igenda ihinduka.Amatsinda nkeshwamakuru ashingiye ku guhitamo  (Non-probability samples)Umushakashatsi ashobora guhitamo itsinda nkeshwamakuru atagamije kwitirira ibyagaragaje nյbushakashatsi abantu bose ahubwo agamije kumenya byimbitse ibijyanye nթryo tsinda nkeshwamakuru yakozeho ubushakashatsi. Aha ahitamo uzamuha amakuru kubera ko nyine ari we ayashakaho nta wundi. Mu gihe mu matsinda nkeshwamakuru ashingiye kuri tombora buri muntu aba afite amahirwe yo gutoranywa ngo arishyirwemo, aha ho umuntu runaka bamutoranya babizi neza kandi babishaka ko ari we nyirizina bashaka ko atanga amakuru. Habaho amoko atandukanye yթtsinda rishingiye ku guhitamo. Ayo moko ni yo tugiye kureba mu bika bikurikiyeho.Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryյmuhuro (Convenience sampling)Duhere ku rugero rwյmushakashatsi ushaka kwiga uko ababyeyi batwite bakoresha telefoni igendanywa mu kwitabira serivisi zibafasha kubungabunga ubuzima bwabo nյbwյmwana uri mu nda. Aha, uyu mushakashatsi ashobora kujya kwicara ku kigo nderabuzima, akajya yakira umubyeyi uje kwipimisha, akamusaba kuba yatanga amakuru akenewe. Ibyo arabikomeza kugeza igihe aboneye umubare akeneye muri iryo tsinda nkeshwamakuru ryյmuhuro. Uyu muhuro uba ku buryo butateganyijwe, ntabwo umushakashatsi aba yateganyije guhura nյmutangamakuru runaka, ahubwo akorana nաbo abonye hafi kandi babyemeye kugeza yujuje umubare wa ngombwa. Abatanga amakuru ku nsanganyamatsiko yյbushakashatsi ni abo umushakashatsi ahuye na bo bwa mbere nko mu ngero zikurikira:  Niba umushakashatsi ashaka gusesengura imyumvire yաbagenzi kuri serivisi bahabwa mu gice cyյbwikorezi, ashobora kubaza abagenzi 30 ba mbere ahuye na bo mu kigo cya Nyabugogo abagenzi bategeramo imodoka. Niba hari ubushakashatsi bwo kumenya uko gahunda yo gukingira abaturage yakozwe, umushakashatsi ashobora kujya ku bitaro bikuru bya Kigali akabaza ababyeyi ba mbere 40 baje gukingiza abana.  Niba umushakashatsi ashaka gusesengura uko abasoreshwa bumva politiki yյmusoro mu Rwanda, ashobora kwinjira muri Banki akabaza usora wese waje kwishyura umusoro, ibihano bahabwa ku birarane ku musoro kuko ari bo bumva uburemere bwյmusoro ku ikubitiro.  Niba umushakashatsi ashaka kumenya icyo ababyeyi batekereza kuri gahunda yթminsi ya mbere 1000 yo kwita ku mwana yatangijwe na Ministeri yՕbuzima mu Rwanda, ashobora kubaza ababyeyi ba mbere 20 bonsa baje ku kigo nderabuzima ibyթyo gahunda.Birumvikana ko umushakashatsi ataba agamije kwitirira ibyavuye mu bushakashatsi abantu bose bahuje ibirango, ahubo aba agamije inyigo yizweho ku buryo bucukumbuye kuri abo bantu bakoranye (case study). Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryթringaniza (Quota sampling)Iringaniza rikorwa iyo mu itsinda nshingirwaho (population), haciwemo amatsinda ahuje ibirango (strata) nkյko twabivuze haruguru ku itsinda nkeshwamakuru rihuje ibirango. Ikigamijwe mu gukora itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryթringaniza ni uko guhitamo abatanga amakuru bishingira ku iringaniza ryաmatsinda yaremwe bitewe nյmubare wաbo bahuje ibirango mu itsinda nshingirwaho. Buri tsinda muri ayo yaremwe riba rigizwe nթgice cyangwa umugabane wաbantu hakurikijwe iringaniza (Burchinal, 2008). Urugero: umushakashatsi arashaka kwiga impamvu zituma abanyeshuri bakomoka mu mugi nաbo mu cyaro bahitamo kwiga amashami ajyanye nթkoranabuhanga mu mashuri makuru. Niba uyu mushakashatsi ahisemo gukorana nթtsinda nkeshwamakuru ryաbanyeshuri 48 kandi akaba azi ko 75% byաbanyeshuri bose bakomoka mu cyaro naho 25% bakaba bakomoka mu mugi, mu guhitamo abo 48 batanga amakuru, arasabwa gukora iringaniza agendeye ku mugabane wթngano ya buri tsinda.Abatanga amakuru bakomoka mu cyaro: 75100 * 48 = 36Abatanga amakuru bakomoka mu mugi: 25100 * 48 = 12Ibi biragaragaza ko uyu mushakashatsi akora itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryթringaniza rigizwe nաmatsinda abiri yաbanyeshuri 36 bakomoka mu cyaro na 12 bakomoka mu mugi, bose hamwe bakaba abatangamakuru 48.Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryթringaniza bigena abazatanga amakuru ashingiye ku bantu bari mu byiciro bitandukanye nkթgitsina, ubwoko, igice cyթmyaka yյbukure, ikiciro cyյbudehe abantu babarirwamo, idini, aho abantu batuye cyangwa amakuru ashingiye ku ihuzwa ryթbyo byiciro nթbindi. Guhitamo abatanga amakuru ntibishingira kuri tombora ahubwo umushakashatsi ni we ubihitiramo. Mu kugena iringaniza, umushakashatsi atoranya abamuha amakuru muri buri tsinda akurukije ubwiganze bwabo mu itsinda nshingirwaho. Aho ni ho hava nyine rya ringaniza. Birumvikana ko ubu buryo bunengwaho ko amakuru avuyemo adashobora kwitirirwa abantu bose bo mu itsinda nshingirwaho. Ibi biterwa nյko guhitamo abatanga amakuru biharirwa umushakashatsi kandi rimwe na rimwe ashobora kugendera ku kimenyane nյko asanzwe aziranye nաbantu (Bryman, 2008).Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru rishingiye ku mpamvu  (Purposive sampling)Tuvuge ko umushakashatsi ashaka kwiga uko abafite ubumuga bwo kutabona bakoresha amakuru yo kuri murandasi. Aba mbere na mbere bafite amakuru yizewe yյko bakoresha ayo makuru ni abafite ubumuga bwo kutabona ubwabo. Niba umushakashatsi ashaka kwiga uko abagore bari mu nzego zifata ibyemezo bahangana nյmunaniro ukabije baterwa nաkazi bakora, aba mbere bafite ayo makuru nաbo bagore nyine. Mu gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru rishingiye ku mpamvu rero, umushakashatsi ahitamo abazamuha amakuru kandi yizeye ko bayafite koko kurusha abandi. Ni uburyo bushingiye ku bushishozi bwe. Impuguke mu byյbushakashatsi Kumar (2005) abisobanura avuga ko umushakashatsi ashaka abantu ahamya ko bafite amakuru akenewe kandi abo bantu bakaba bafite ubushake bwo kuyatanga. Iri tsinda nkeshwamakuru rishingiye ku mpamvu rero, nkյko Kumar abishimangira, rikoreshwa iyo umushakashatsi ashaka gucukumbura ukuri gushingiye ku mateka no gusobanura ibintu abantu batari bafiteho amakuru ku buryo bwimbitse. Kimwe nյbundi buryo bwose bwo gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru hadakoreshejwe tombora, ubu buryo bwo gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru rishingiye ku mpamvu bunengwaho ko amakuru yյbushakashatsi adashobora kwitirirwa abantu bose bahuje ibirango nաbayatanze.Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryյruhererekane  (Snowball sampling)Itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryյruhererekane ritangira kubakwa rihereye ku muntu cyangwa abantu bake bujuje ibirango umushakashatsi yifuza. Uyu muntu rero cyangwa abo bantu bake ni bo baba abatangamakuru fatizo bageza umushakashatsi kuri bagenzi babo bahuje ibirango. Aba na bo bagenda batanga amakuru atuma agera ku bandi bari mu rwego rumwe, gutyo gutyo. Aho rero ni ryo fatizo ryթjambo uruhererekane. Ubu buryo bukunda gukoreshwa aho insanganyamatsiko yigwaho isaba ubwitonzi no kwigengesera cyangwa se iyo kugera ku batanga amakuru bigoranye. Ingero: indaya, arubyiruko rufata ibiyobyabwenge, abakobwa bakuyemo inda cyangwa babyariye iwabo, abanyeshuri biga cyane, nթbindi. Reka dufate urugero rufatika rwյmushakashatsi ushaka kwiga uko abahoze mu mwuga wյburaya bitwara iyo bamaze kubona akazi mu buzima busanzwe. Aha umushakashatsi akora umurimo ukomeye wo kubona umuntu wavuye mu buraya kandi wabonye akazi. Iyo amaze kumubona, uyu na we amuha amakuru yաbandi bameze nka we. Nյbwo amakuru atanzwe nթtsinda nkeshwamakuru ryյruhererekane atitirirwa abantu bose, ashobora gutuma umushakashatsi acukumbura ikibazo runaka ari kwigaho ku buryo bwimbitse mu mbago zաbamuhaye amakuru. Ingano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuruIkibazo ku ngano yթtsinda nkeshwankuru kibazwa mu bushakashatsi ubwo ari bwo bwose. Iki kibazo kandi nta gisubizo ntakuka kigira kuko kwemeza ingano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru biterwa nթmpamvu nyinshi kandi zinyuranye. Zimwe muri izi mpamvu zishobora kuba igihe nաmikoro. Bryman (2008) yemeza ko kongera ingano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru bishobora gutuma ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi bihagararira itsinda nshingirwaho: uko ingano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru yiyongera, ni na ko ikosa ryթryo tsinda rigabanuka. Ikosa rishobora kugaragara mu gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru risobanuye ku buryo bwimbitse mu gitabo cya Cohen, Manion na Morrison (2000) no mu cya Bryman (2008).Indi mpamvu ishobora gutuma hafatwa ikemezo ku ngano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru ni abantu badasubiza cyangwa bahitamo kutagira uruhare mu bushakashatsi kandi bari mu itsinda nshingirwaho. Bryman (2008) agira abashakashatsi inama yo kongera umubare wթtsinda nkeshwamakuru kugira ngo bakemure ikibazo cyաbadasubiza. Urugero: niba umushakashatsi ateganya kukoresha iganirabaza (interview) abanyeshuri 300, kandi asanzwe azi ko abadasubiza bakunze kuba ari hafi ya 25%, icyo gihe ashobora gutoranya itsinda ryաbanyeshuri 400 kugeza kuri 450. Ibyo bishatse kuvuga ko niba 25% batashubije (ari bo bangana nաbanyeshuri 100), nibura ba bandi yifuzaga 300 baraba bashubije. Birumvikana ko ibi bigira ingaruka ku gihe no ku mikoro. Ibi na byo umushakashatsi agomba kuba yabitekerejeho.Guhuza/gutandukanya ibirango kwաbagize itsinda nshingirwaho (homogeneity/ heterogeneity of the population): iyo abagize itsinda nshingirwaho bahuje ibirango si ngomba ko itsinda riba rinini. Urugero: abanyeshuri bաbahungu bigana mu isomo ryթmibare kandi batuye hamwe. Iri tsinda nkeshwamakuru rihuje ibirango kandi rishobora kuba rito kuko rihuriye ku mibereho isa. Nyamara hari ubwo itsinda nshingirwaho rishobora kuba ritandukanyije ibirango rwose. Dufashe urugero rwաbanyeshuri bաbahungu nաbakobwa bari mu kigero kթmyaka kuva kuri 16 kugeza kuri 20 biga isomo ryթmibare, iryթbinyabuzima nթryաmateka. Iri tsinda rikunze kuba rinini kugira ngo imfatashusho (variables) zose za ngombwa zibe zihagarariwe.Isesengura rigamijwe nյbwoko bwյbushakashatsi bugiye gukorwa na byo bishobora kugira ingaruka ku ngano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru. Burchinal (2008) asanga ingano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru iterwa nյko itsinda nkeshwamakuru nyirizina ryatoranyijwe ku buryo bwa tombora (probability sample) cyangwa bwo guhitamo (non-probability samples). Mu matsinda nkeshwamakuru ya tombora, ingano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru igomba gushingira kuri iki kibazo: ese amakuru nabonye ashobora guhagararira abaturage bose (itsinda nshingirwaho)? Iyo ngano bayibona bifashishije amahame yթbarurishamibare (Kellstedt & Whitten, 2013). Hari abakoresha ijanisha mu kugena ingano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru. Nka Burchinal (2008) avuga ko ku baturage 1000 ingano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru ari 30% yabo; ku baturage 10000 ikaba 10%, naho 1% ikabarwa ku baturage 15000 cyangwa hejuru yabo. Burchinal avuga ko itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryաbantu 2000 na 2500 rihagije ku baturage bagera kuri miliyoni. Hari abashakashatsi bakoze imbonerahamwe zigaragaza ingano zաmatsinda nkeshwamakuru nաmatsinda nshingirwaho bijyanye. Abo ni nka Krejcie na Morgan (1970) na Cohen, Manion na Morrison (2000). Bene izi mbonerahamwe zishobora gufasha abashakashatsi kugena ingano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru batiriwe bajya mu ibarurishamibare. Mu matsinda nkeshwamakuru ashingiye ku guhitamo, ingano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru igerwaho hashingiwe kuri ibi kibazo: ҅se amakuru yakusanyijwe ku buryo ntacyakongerwaho ku kibazo kiri kwigwa?ӠNiba umushakashatsi abona amakuru yakusanyijwe ahagije, ko nta cyakongerwaho, icyo gihe aba yanyuzwe nաmakuru amaze kubona maze agahagarika gushaka andi. Mu byյkuri nta ngano yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru nyirizina izwi igenwa mu buryo ubu nյbu, ahubwo iterwa nյko umushakatsi yumva yanyuzwe nաmakuru yabonye. UmwanzuroNkյko twabigarutseho, guteganya uko gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru bikorwa ni umurimo wթngenzi mu bushakashatsi. Uwo murimo ukorwa mbere yթgihe mu gutegura umushinga wյbushakashatsi. Umushakashatsi ateganya uko uzatoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru kubera impamvu (fitness for purpose). Gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru ku buryo bukwiye biri mu byubaka ireme ryյbushakashatsi, ari ku ruhande rwյbubonere (validity) ndetse no ku bwizerwe (reliability) byabwo. IndangasokoBryman, A. (2008). Social research methods (3rd edition). Oxford: Oxford University Press.Burchinal, L. G. (2008). Methods for social researches in developing countries. Arlington: Ahfad.Carlson, M. J., & Hyde, S. M. (2003). Doing empirical political research. Boston: Houghton Mifflin Company.Cohen, L., Manion, L., & Morrison, K. (2000). Research methods in education (5th edition). New York: RoutledgeFalmer.Kellstedt, P. M., & Whitten, G. D. (2013). Fundamentals of political science research (2nd edition). Cambridge: Cambridge University Press.Kombo, K. D., & Tromp, L. A. (2006). Proposal and thesis writing. An introduction. Nairobi: Paulines Publications Africa.Krejcie, R. V., & Morgan, D. W. (1970). Determining sample size for research activities. Educational and Psychological Measurement, 30, 607 Р610.Kumar, R. (2005). Research methodology: A step-by-step guide for beginners (2nd edition).
