London: Sage Publication.UMUTWE 7 IYOBORAMIKORERE: IKUSANYAMAKURU NՉSESENGURAMAKURUTlesphore Ngarambe, Charline Mulindahabi na Evode MukamaIriburiroKugira ngo ubushakashatsi bugere ku musaruro wifuzwa, hari inzira zթngezi zigomba gukurikizwa. Uhereye ku gitekerezo kiba cyatumye umuntu abona ko ari ngombwa gukora ubushakashatsi kugeza igihe habonekeye amakuru agasesengurwa ku buryo busubiza ibibazo byari byayoboye ubushakatsitsi, ni ngombwa ko umushakashatsi akurikira iyoboramikorere risobanutse. Byյmuwihariko, muri uyu muntwe wթgitabo, turerekana ibintu byթngenzi umushakashatsi yitaho mu gihe cyo gukusanya amakuru ndetse no kuyasesengura. Haba ari mu bushakashatsi nyamimerere cyangwa ubushakashatsi nyamubaro, ibikorwa byթkusanyamakuru nթsesengura ryayo byubakira ku itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryatoranijwe. Amakuru yյbushakashatsi ashobora gukusanywa hakoreshejwe uburyo butandukanye. Ubwթngenzi turi bwibandeho ni iganirabaza, urutonde rwթbibazo, no kwitegereza. Iyo amakuru amaze kuboneka umushakashatsi akurikizaho kuyasesengura. Bitewe nթmiterere yյbushakashatsi, hari ubwoko bubiri bwթngenzi bukoreshwa mu isesenguramakuru: 	isesenguramimerere 	nթsesengura 	nyamubaro. Isesenguramimerere rikoreshwa iyo umushakashatsi asesengura amakuru ari mu nyandiko zanditse cyangwa yaturutse mu bisubizo byatanzwe ku bibazo bifunguye. Naho isesenguramakuru nyamubaro rikunze gukoreshwa ku bibazo bifunze ku buryo umushakashatsi abarura inshuro igisubizo runaka kigaragara mu batanze amakuru: inshuro amakuru runaka yasubiwemo cyangwa umubare wաbatanze amakuru asa. IkusanyamakuruMuri rusange mu bushakashatsi bwa gihanga habaho ubwoko bubiri bwաmakuru. Hari amakuru yթbanze nաmakuru yunganira. Amakuru yթbanze ni amakuru umushakashatsi yishakira ku giti ke akayahabwa nթtsinda nkeshwamakuru yatoranije. Iri tsinda rishobora kuba rigizwe nթnyandiko, abantu, inyamaswa ndetse nթbindi biremwa byakorwaho ubushakashatsi. Amakuru yunganira yo ni amakuru umushakashatsi agenda akura mu nyandiko ku bushakashatsi bwakozwe nաbandi zijyanye nթgitekerezo cyangwa ikibazo arimo gukoraho ubushakashatsi. Nkյko twabivuze hejuru, tugiye kureba bumwe mu buryo umushakashatsi ashobora kwifashisha mu gukusanya amakuru. Gutegura ikusanyamakuruMbere yյko umushakashatsi akusanya amakuru, abanza guhitamo ikerekezo nyamukuru ashaka guha ubushakashatsi bwe. Ategura uburyo nթbikoresho azifashisha mu kuyakusanya ashingiye ku mpamvu atekereza ko ubwo buryo ari bwo buboneye kandi ari bwo buzamuha amakuru yizewe. Ateganya aho azakura amakuru nաbazayamuha ndetse nթgihe azayakusanyiriza.Muri iyi nyandiko, ikerekezo nyamukuru cyյbushakashatsi ni nkթnyigo icukumbuye ku kintu runaka (case study), inyigo ku buzima bwյmuntu (life story research), ubushakashatsi ku masano yթbintu (correlational research) nթbindi. Reka dufate urugero rwթnyigo icukumbuye umushakashatsi ashaka gukora ku kuntu abarimu bo mu mashuri yisumbuye bakiriye impinduka ziri mu ikoreshwa ryթbitabo bishya mu isomo ryյbutabire.Dore ibibazo byյbushakashatsi umushakashatsi ashobora kwibaza:1. Abarimu bo mu mashuri yisumbuye bakoresha bate ibitabo bishya mu isomo ryյbutabire?2. Ni izihe ngorane abarimu bo mu mashuri yisumbuye bahura na zo mu ikoreshwa ryթbitabo bishya mu isomo ryյbutabire?3. Ni iki abarimu bo mu mashuri yisumbuye bifuza ko cyakorwa kugira ngo imikoreshereze yթbitabo bishya irusheho kunoga mu isomo ryյbutabire?Kuri buri kibazo cyյbushakashatsi, ni ngombwa gutegura uko ikusanyamakuru rizakorwa. Turifashisha urugero ku kibazo cya mbere cyյbushakashatsi. Ikerekezo nyamuru cyյbushakashatsi: Inyigo icukumbuyeIkibazo cyյbushakashatsi: Abarimu bo mu mashuri yisumbuye bakoresha bate ibitabo bishya mu isomo ryյbutabire?Ibibazo bifasha mu gutegura ikusanyamakuruUko ikusanyamakuru rizakorwaNI UKUBERA IKI amakuru akusanyijwe?Kugira ngo hamenyekane inzira ikoreshwa muri iki gihe nաbarimu bաmashuri yisumbuye mu gukoresha ibitabo bishya mu isomo ryյbutabire.NI UBUHE BURYO buzakoreshwa mu gukusanya amakuru?Hazagoreshwa iganirabaza mu gukusanya amakuru.NI BANDE bazatanga amakuru? Amasoko azaturukamo amakuru NI AYAHE?Iganirabaza rizakorerwa abarimu bigisha isomo ryյbutabire mu mashuri yisumbuye. Abazatanga amakuru ni BANGAHE? / Amasoko azaturukamo amakuru ni ANGAHE?Abarimu bo mu mashuri yisumbuye umunani bazakorerwa iganirabaza, babiri kuri buri kigo muri bine byatoranyijwe.NI HEHE amakuru azakusanyirizwa?Abarimu bo mu mashuri yisumbuye umunani bazakorerwa iganirabaza, babiri kuri buri kigo muri bine byatoranyijwe mu mugi wa Kigali.Amakuru azakusanywa INSHURO ZINGAHE?Amakuru azakusanywa inshuro imwe nyuma yյko abarimu bazaba barangije kwigisha nibura inshuro imwe isomo ryյbutabire bakoresheje ibitabo bishya.Amakuru azakusanywa GUTE?Amakuru azakusanywa hakoreshejwe iganirabaza rifunguye igice hari nաkuma gafata amajwi ndetse nյmushakashatsi azaba yandika inshamake yթbyo yumva nթbyo abona muri iryo ganirabaza (field notes).ISOBANURAMPAMVU ryթyi gahunda yթkusanyamakuru (kubera iki ubu buryo ari bwo bubereye ikusanyamakuru kuri iki kibazo cyյbushakashatsi?)Gukoresha iganirabaza bituma abarimu batanga amakuru bahagazeho bo ubwabo. Byongeye iganirabaza rifunguye igice rizatuma umushakashatsi ashobora kubaza buri wese ibibazo bisa ariko akaba yakongeraho nթbindi bibishamikiyeho kugira ngo abone amakuru acukumbuye. Abarimu umunani, babiri kuri buri kigo muri bine byatoranyijwe mu mugi wa Kigali bahagarariye bagenzi babo.Vithal na Jansen (1997) bashyize hamwe ingingo zթngenzi zafasha umushakashatsi gutegura ikusanyamakuru. Muri izo ngingo harimo izi zikurikira:1. Mu gutegura uko ikusanyamakuru rizakorwa, umushakashatsi ashobora guhanga uburyo bukwiye azakoresha mu gutara ayo makuru. Byongere, umushakashatsi agomba kuzirikana ko buri buryo ashobora gukoresha mu gutara amakuru bugira ibyiza byabwo ariko na none bukagira inzitizi bwihariye. 2. Uburyo bwo gukusanya amakuru yյbushakashatsi bugomba kuba bugamije gusubiza ibibazo byյbushakashatsi. Isano hagati yյburyo bwo gukusanya amakuru nթbibazo byյbushakashatsi igomba kugaragazwa. Ikibazo runaka cyյbushakashatsi gishobora gukenera uburyo runaka bwo gukusanya amakuru. Buri kibazo ni umwihariko nյbwo kigomba kuba gifitanye isano nթbindi mu bushakashatsi runaka.3. Umushakashatsi ashobora guhanga ibikoresho azakoresha mu gutara amakuru; ashobora gukoresha ibyahanzwe nաbandi bashakashatsi; ashobora kandi no kubakira ku bikoresho byakozwe nաbandi.4. Ibikoresho byյbushakashatsi bikenera kubanza kugeragezwa kugira ngo umushakashatsi amenye niba ibibazo byubatse ku buryo bwumvikana kimwe ku batangamakuru bose. Ibi umushakashatsi ashobora kubigeraho, agerageza ibikoresho byo gukusanya amakuru ku itsinda ryաbantu bake ariko bahuje ibirango nթtsinda nkeshwamakuru.5. Uburyo burenze bumwe bushobora gukoreshwa mu gukusanya amakuru ku kibazo kimwe cyյbushakashatsi. Gukomatanya uburyo bwo gutara amakuru bifite akamaro kanini kuko bituma umushakashatsi acengera kurushaho ingingo iri kwigwa. Byongeye ibyagaragajwe nյburyo bunyuranye bwo gutara amakuru byongera ubwemerwe.6. Mu guteganya uko amakuru azakusanywa, ni ngombwa no guteganya ingingo zijyanye no kubahiriza amahame yյbushakashatsi. Ibi bikubiyemo ingingo zijyanye no kudatangaza amazina yյwaguhaye amakuru, gusaba abatangamakuru uruhushya rwo kwemera ku bushake kujya mu itsinda nkeshwamakuru, guteganya uburyo uzafasha abatangamakuru bashobora guhungabanywa nաmakuru batanze nթbindi.Nkյko twabivuze hejuru, habaho uburyo bwinshi bwo gukusanya amakuru. Reka turebe bumwe muri bwo bukunze gukoreshwa cyane mu bushakashatsi ku bumenyi nyamuntu nթmibanire yաbantu: iganirabaza, ibaza rishingiye ku rutonde rwթbibazo no kwitegereza. Iganirabaza Iganirabaza ni bumwe mu buryo bwթngenzi bukoreshwa mu gukusanya amakuru byaba ari mu bushakashatsi nyamubaro cyangwa ubushakashatsi nyamimerere. Iganirabaza rikorwa mu buryo butandukanye:a. 	Iganirabaza rigiye umujyo umweMuri ubu bwoko bwթganirabaza, ubaza akoresha ibibazo byateguwe bitondetse kuri gahunda. Intego yթri baza ni ukugira ngo buri wese mu itsinda nkeshwamakuru ahabwe amahirwe angana yթbazwa. Iyo ababazwa bahawe amahirwe angana yo kumva ibibazo kimwe byongera igipimo cyյbwizerwe bwթbisubizo byաbagize itsinda nkeshwamakuru bose. Ubaza asoma ibibazo akurikije urutonde rwabyo uko bikurikirana kuri gahunda. Muri rusange, ibyo bibazo biba byihariye kandi akenshi bikabyara ibisubizo bitangwa ku buryo budahinduka. Ibibazo biteye gutya byitwa ibibazo bifunze. Iyo ni yo mpamvu ituma abashakashatsi bakora ubushakatsi bushingiye ku ibaza bakunda iganirabaza rigiye umujyo umwe kuko butuma ibaza nթyandikwa ryթbisubizo bigendera ku gipimo kizewe. b. 	Iganirabaza rifunguye igice Muri iri ganirabaza ubaza aba afite urutonde rwթbibazo biteye ku buryo bwa rusange kandi akaba ashobora kubibaza adakurikije uburyo bitondekanijemo ikibazo ku kindi. Aha ubaza aba afite uburenganzira bwo kubaza nթbindi bibazo biri hanze yթbyari byashyizwe ku rutonde. c. 	Iganirabaza rifunguyeIri ganirabaza rikorwa ubaza afite gusa urutonde rwթbitekerezo bishingiye ku kibazo cyյbushakashatsi bikamubera gusa nkթfashabwonko. Akenshi ubu buryo bwo kubaza bukoreshwa ku buryo bwo kwiganirira bisanzwe kandi imiterere yթnteruro nյrukurikirane rwթbibazo biba biteye ukwabyo bitewe nյbaza. d. 	Iganirabaza ryթtsindaIri ganirabaza rikoresha akenshi ibibazo bifunguye. Ibibazo ryifashisha biba bishingiye ku ngingo yihariye ireba itsinda runaka cyangwa ikabaza iki nթki gihangayikishije umushakashatsi. Urugero ni nkյmushakashatsi waba ushaka kumenya ibibazo byթngutu byugarije urubyiruko rwյ Rwanda muri iki gihe. Ashobora kugena ibibazo bireba byյmwihariko urubyiruko rwաbahungu cyangwa urwաbakobwa. Icyo gihe akora amatsinda atandukanye buri tsinda akaribaza ukwaryo. e. 	Iganirabaza ryթbarankuruUbu ni uburyo bwթganirabaza rifunguye cyangwa rifunguye igice. Ubazwa asabwa kwibuka igikorwa cyabaye kera akagerageza kugitangaho ibitekerezo. Akenshi ibitekerezo bitangwa bigendera ku rutonde rwթbibazo cyangwa ibikorwa byabaye kera akabihuza nթgihe runaka kizwi mu mateka ku buryo umushakashatsi agira ishusho nyayo yյko byagenze. f. 	Iganirabaza rishingiye ku mateka yյbuzimaNi kimwe nթganirabaza ryթbarankuru. Aho bitandukaniye gusa ni uko intego yթganirabaza rishingiye ku mateka yյbuzima ari ugukusanya amakuru ku mibereho yose yյbazwa. Ibaza rishingiye ku rutonde rwթbibazo Mu gukora urutonde rwթbibazo, umushakashatsi agomba gufata intego zihariye zյbushakashatsi bwe akazihinduramo ibibazo byihariye bizatanga ibisubizo ku bibazo byթbanze ubushakashatsi bwashingiyeho. Hari ubwoko butandukanye bwթbibazo bitewe nթmisusire ndetse nթnyito yabyo. a. 	Ubwoko bwթbibazo bushingiye ku nyitoInyito yթkibazo ni kimwe mu bigize urutonde ryթbibazo bikoreshwa mu bushakashatsi bushingiye ku ibaza.Ibibazo bishingiye ku makuru afatika Ubu ni ubwoko bwթbibazo bigamije kubaza amakuru ku bintu byabaye bifatika. Ibyo bibazo bishobora gufasha umushakashatsi kumenya amavu nաmavuko yթbintu cyangwa umuntu, ahantu runaka ndetse nթmyitwarire. Urugero: umushakashatsi ashobora kubaza nkթbibazo byթmimerere kugira ngo amenye amavu nաmavuko yյmuntu; ibyo bituma hari igice runaka umuhererezamo. Akenshi uko kumushyira mu gice runaka bituma haboneka ibisobanuro ku myitwarire iranga umuntu uyu nյyu. Ingero zթbibazo bishingiye ku makuru afatika ziteye ku buryo bukurikira: Toranya umubare werekana ikiciro cyաmashuri warangije kwiga: 1. Amashuri abanza2. Amashuri yisumbuye 3. Ikiciro giciriritse cya kaminuza4. Ikiciro gihanitse cya kaminuza5. Ikiciro kթkirenga cya kaminuzaUbundi bwoko bwթbibazo nkթbi ni ibiba bibaza nko ku mibereho ikikije umuntu. Urugero: Ni bande mubana mu rugo? Ubundi buryo bukoreshwa ni ububaza ku buryo bwifashishwa mu ngendo. Urugero: Ugera ku kazi gute? Ibindi bibazo bigafasha ku kumenya amakuru ku bikorwa byթmyidagaduro. Urugero: Ujya muri sinema inshuro zingahe? Ibibazo bireba umuntu ku giti keIbibazo bireba umuntu ku giti ke ni ibibazo byerekeye imimerere, imyitwarire, ibyiyumvo ndetse nթbitekerezo byյbazwa. Ibi bibazo bifasha umushakashatsi gucukumbura imyitwarire ijyana nթkerekezo rusange gishobora gutuma umuntu akora cyangwa agahindura imigirire mu buryo ubu nյbu iyo ahuye nթmbarutso iyi nթyi. Urugero rukurikira ruragaragaza imyitwarire ku kibazo cyo gukuramo inda: Byaba bishoboka ko mu Rwanda itegeko ryaha umugore uburenganzira bwo gukuramo inda igihe abaganga bagaragaje ko umwana afite ibyago byinshi byo kuzavukana ubumuga bukomeye. 1. Yego 2. Oya3. Simbizi4. Nta gisubizo mfiteb. 	Uburyo bwթbibazo bushingiye ku misusireUretse inyito, iyo umushakashatsi ategura ibibazo agomba kwita ku misusire yթkibazo nթmiterere yթtsinda ryթbibazo bijyana na byo. Muri uru rwego amoko yթbibazo amenyerewe ni atatu: ibibazo bifunze, ibibazo bifunguye, ibibazo biteganya, ibibazo bigerura. Ibibazo bifunzeMuri ubu bwoko bwթbibazo, usubiza ahabwa urutonde rwթbisubizo hanyuma agasabwa gutoranyamo ikirusha ibindi kwegera neza igitekerezo ke. Urugero: umushakashatsi ushaka kumenya uko umuntu yishimiye imibereho ye mu muryango we, ashobora kubaza ikibazo gikurikira:Shyira akamenyesto ku mubare werekana uko wumva wishimiye imibereho yo mu muryango wawe: 1. Bihebuje cyane2. Bihebuje 3. Mu rugero 4. Gake5. Gake cyane 6. Nta na gake 7. Simbizi 8. Nta gisubizo Hari nյbwo ibisubizo ku kibazo gifunze bishobora kuba birambuye cyane kurusha uru rugero twatanze. Urundi rugero ni nkյmushakashatsi ushaka kumenya icyo abantu batekereza ku cyakorwa kugira ngo abana bo mu muhanda bawuvemo burundu. Muri icyo gihe ashobora kubaza ikibazo giteye gutya: Mu gukemura ikibazo cyաbana bo mu muhanda bamwe batekereza ko cyakemurwa na Leta naho abandi bagatekereza ko ibyo bitareba Leta. Ibi ubyumva ute? 1. Leta igomba gukora ibishoboka byose ikavana aba bana mu muhanda igakurikirana imibereho yabo2. Iki kibazo ntikindeba cyane nta mwanya mfite wo kwibaza uwagikemura3. Ibi ntibireba Leta Nkյko bigaragara, ibibazo bifunze ntibigora kubibaza kandi no kubisubiza birihuta cyane. Ikindi kandi ari ubaza cyangwa usubiza ntibakenera kwandika ibintu byinshi kandi isesengura ryթbisubizo riroroha. Gusa inenge ikomeye abashakashatsi nka Frankfort-Nachmias na Nachmias (2008, p. 233) na Bryman (2008, pp. 231 Р232) bagaragaje, ni uko bishobora gutuma usubiza abogama. Impamvu yթngenzi batanga ni uko iyo ibisubizo byatanzwe bidaha usubiza amahirwe menshi yo gutanga ibindi bisubizo yitekerereje ku giti ke. Ikindi ni uko bishobora ahubwo kumuha amahitamo atashoboraga kwitekerereza ku bwe. Ibibazo bifunguye Ibibazo bifunguye ni ubwoko bwթbibazo bidaha ubazwa ibisubizo ahitamo ahubwo bikamuha uburenganzira bwo gusubiza ibyo atekereza mu bwisanzure busesuye. Urugero rworoshye ni nkթkibazo giteye gitya: Ni ibihe bibazo byթngutu byugarije abanyarwanda utekereza ko Leta yյ Rwanda yakwibandaho muri ibi bihe turimo? Ikibazo nkթki gifunguye akenshi gikoreshwa iyo umushakashashatsi ashaka kumenya icyo rubanda rutekereza ku kibazo runaka kireba inyungu rusange. Ikiza kթbibazo bifunguye ni uko bidafungira usubiza mu ndorerwamo zթbibazo nաmahitamo byatanzwe nյmushakashatsi gusa. Iyo usubiza amaze kumva neza aho ikibazo kiganisha, ataga ibitekerezo bye mu bwisanzure busesuye. Biba byiza iyo abajijwe kandi asubije mu rurimi yumva neza kuko byongera ububonere bwթbisubizo atanga. Iyo icyo gisubizo kitumvikana ubaza ashobora gusiganuza neza hanyuma usubiza agasobanura neza cyangwa agatanga impamvu yatumye atanga igisubizo runaka. Ibizubizo bifunguye bituma ubaza avanaho urujijo urwo ari rwo rwose, kandi bigatuma haba ubusabane hagati yյbaza nյsubiza. Icyakora ibibazo nkթbi bigora isubiza nթsesengura. Kugira ngo umushakashasti yiyorohereze akazi agomba guhanga imbata yթnkurikizo kugira ngo buri gisubizo kigire itsinda ryihariye gishyirwamo.Mu bushakashatsi bujyanye nթmibanire yաbantu, imbata yթnkurikizo ikoreshwa iyo bashaka kubara no kusensengura amakuru yavuye mu iganirabaza ryakusanyije ibisubizo bitagiye umujyo umwe. Urugero ni nkթbisubizo ku bibazo bifunguye bikubiye mu iganirabaza cyangwa mu rutonde rwթbibazo, inyandiko zo mu binyamakuru, ibiganiro byo kuri televisiyo, nթbindi. Iyo habonetse ibisubizo ku bibazo bifunguye, umushakashatsi afata ibisubizo byաbantu akabikusanya mu matsinda anyuranye. Hanyuma iyo amaze gukora amatsinda, umushakashatsi aha nimero ayo matsinda. Kugira ngo byumvikane neza, reka twifashishe urugero rwatanzwe na Schuman na Presser (1996, p. 88). Aba bashakashatsi babajije ikibazo kerekeye ibiranga umurimo abantu bose bahitamo kurusha iyindi, hanyuma ibisubizo byatanzwe babishyira mu matsinda 11 ku buryo bukurikira: (1) Umushahara, (2) kumva umuntu hari intego agezeho, (3) kumva ufite akazi, (4) akazi gashimishije, (5) umutekano, (6) amahirwe yo kuzamurwa mu ntera, (7) amasaha make yաkazi, (8) imiterere yաkazi, (9) inyungu mu kazi, (10) ukunyurwa, (11) ibindi bisubizo bitandukanye. Nkյko bigaragara buri tsinda ryahawe umubare waryo kuva kuri (1) kugeza kuri (11). Mu gihe kթsesengura, iyi mibare ituma umushakashatsi yegeranya ibisubizo bijya gusa, ku buryo byakoroha kumenya umubare wաbabitanze cyangwa ishuro byagiye bigaruka. Ibibazo biteganyaIbibazo biteganya ni ibibazo biteye ku buryo bwihariye bireba gusa agatsinda kihariye gato kageruwe mu itsinda ryաbabazwa bose. Impamvu yթbi bibazo ni uko akenshi haba hari ibibazo biba bireba ababazwa bamwe abandi bitabareba. Urugero ni nkթkibazo giteye gutya: ҈itamo impamvu zatuma ujya kwiga muri kaminuzaӮ Aha birumvikana ko iki kibazo kireba gusa abanyeshuri bo mu mashuri yisumbuye kuko nko mu gihugu cyacu cyյ Rwanda, abantu bose bahawe amahirwe yo kwiga bahereye ku mashuri abanza kugeza muri kaminuza. Ariko usesenguye neza iki kibazo usanga abiga mu mashuri yisumbuye ari bo kireba kuko ni bo baba bafite gahunda yo guhita bajya muri kaminuza igihe barangije ikiciro barimo. Iyo habajijwe ikibazo nkթki ni ngombwa guteganya ibibazo bireba iri tsinda ryihariye. Bitewe nթntego cyangwa imiterere yյbushakashatsi, itsinda nkeshwamakuru rishobora kuba rigizwe nաbagore nաbagabo ariko hakaza kuba umwihariko wթbibazo bigenerwa abagore gusa. Icyo gihe mbere yo kugena ibyo bibazo ubaza agena ikibazo rusange gihigika bamwe mu babazwa kigasiga abandi. Icyo kibazo bakita ikibazo kiyungurura. Urugero, umushakashatsi ashaka kumenya amakuru ku muntu, yabaza ikibazo gikurikira: Ujya usoma ibinyamakuru kenshi? (sobanura). Aha kugira ngo haboneke itsinda rirebwa nթbibazo bikurikiraho harakenerwa ikibazo kiyungurura giteye gutya: 1. Yego (subiza ibibazo bikurikiraho); 2. Oya (simbuka ukomereze ku kibazo cya 3)Urutonde rwթbibazo rwoherezwaUrutonde rwթbibazo rwoherezwa ni bumwe mu buryo bwo gukusanya amakuru. Uru rutonde rwohererezwa abagize itsinda nkeshwamakuru buri wese agahabwa kopi ye asubiza ibibazo ari wenyine. Hari uburyo bwinshi bwo gutegura urutonde rwթbibazo rwoherezwa gusa ubwoko buzwi cyane kurusha ubundi ni urutonde rwթbibazo rucishwa mu iposita cyangwa kuri imeyili. Muri ubu buryo, urutonde rwթbibazo iyo rumaze gutunganywa rwohererezwa usubiza hakoreshejwe iposita cyangwa imeyili. Iyo ubazwa amaze kuzuza ibisubizo ahabugenewe, arongera akarusubiza akoresheje uburyo yari yararwohererejwemo. Icyakora, igihe cyose bishoboka, ni ngombwa kubanza gukora igerageza mbere yo gukoresha urutonde rwթbibazo rwoherezwa cyangwa urwifashishwa mu iganirabaza rigiye umujyo umwe. Akenshi umumaro wթryo gerageza si ukugira ngo ubaza agenzure niba ibibazo bibajije neza, ahubwo ni ukureba niba muri rusange uburyo bwo kubaza bwakoreshejwe nta ngorane buzateza mu gihe igikorwa cyo gukusanya amakuru kizaba kirimbanije. Iri geregeza rigira akamaro kurushaho iyo umushakashatsi yifashishije urutonde rwթbibazo rwoherezwa mu gukusanya amakuru. Impamvu ni uko igihe cyo gusubiza ibibazo ubaza aba atari kumwe nյbazwa kugira ngo amufashe mu gusobanura ikibazo icyo ari cyo cyose cyatera urujijo. No mu iganirabaza igerageza ni ngombwa kuko hari ibibazo byavuka nyuma yo kubaza abantu bake maze ubaza akabikemura mu maguru mashya. Ibibazo bivutse mu gihe kթgerageza, umushakashatsi ashobora kubikemura yongera gutondekanya amagambo, interuro cyangwa ibibazo neza, avanamo ibibazo bidafite akamaro, cyangwa yongeramo ibindi byatuma urutonde muri rusange rugira injyana yumvikana. KwitegerezaKwitegereza ni bumwe mu buryo bwթngenzi bukoreshwa mu bushakashatsi nyamuntu nթmibanire yաbantu. Bukoreshwa mu gukusanya amakuru ahereye ku byo umuntu abona mu myitwarire yթkintu cyangwa umuntu uyu nյyu. Urugero: nkաbakora ubushakashatsi mu bya politiki, bagira uburyo bwabo bwo kwitegereza abayobozi bari mu myanya iyi nթyi, abazobereye mu bumenyi bwa muntu, bareba imigenzo yo mu miryango ituye mu byaro cyangwa mu migi. Naho abita ku bijyanye nյbumenyi bwo mu mutwe, bitegereza ubusabane hagati yյdutsinda duto twաbantu. Ibyo byose bishobora gukorwa mu buryo bugendeye ku mbata yթnkurikizo cyangwa ku buryo bwisanzuye. Mu gukusanya amakuru, umushakashatsi ashobora gukoresha uburyo bumwe cyangwa burenze bumwe bitewe nյbwoko bwաmakuru akeneye. Iyo yamaze kubuhitamo agakusanya amakuru, umurimo ukurikiraho ni ukuyasensengura nkյko bigaragara mu gice cya kabiri cyյyu mutwe. IsesenguramakuruMbere yo gutangira isesenguramakuru, bitewe nթmiterere yյbushakashatsi, bwaba nyamimerere cyangwa nyamubaro, ni ngombwa kumenya ubwoko bwաmakuru yakusanyijwe. Umushakashatsi ashobora kuba akeneye kumenya ibisobanuro byimbitse ku makuru yabonye icyo gihe akoresha uburyo bwթsesenguramimerere. Naho iyo ashaka kumenya ku buryo bubarika ibyavuzwe cyangwa ababivuze, hakoreshwa isesesengura nyamubaro. Isesengura ryթkivugwaDuhereye ku byanditswe na Bryman (2008, p. 274), isesengura ryթkivugwa ni uburyo bukoreshwa gusesengura inyandiko cyangwa amashusho. Ubwo buryo buba bugamije gushyira mu mibare ikivugwa hagendewe ku matsinda yateguwe kandi mu buryo buri kuri gahunda. Ubu buryo bushobora kukoreshwa no mu bundi bushakashatsi busa nյbwo. Nko mu buryo bunyuranye bwթsakazamakuru, isesengura ryթkivugwa rishobora gukoreshwa iyo umushakashatsi ashaka kumenya ingano nթmiterere yյko ibitangazamakuru byibanda ku ngingo iyi nթyi. Urugero usomye itangazamakuru ryandika ugasanga zimwe mu nkuru zթngenzi ryandika ari kuri Sida cyangwa indwara yթbisazi byաmatungo ni ngombwa kwibaza ibibazo bikurikira: 1. Ni ryari izi nkuru zasohotse mu binyamakuru bwa mbere?2. Ni ikihe gitangazamakuru cyatanze ibindi kwandika kuri iyi ngingo? 3. Ni ikihe gitangazamakuru kitaye kuri iyi nkuru kurusha ibindi? 4. Ni mu kihe gihe ibitangazamakuru byagabanije umurego mu kwandika kuri iyi ngingo? 5. Hari ubwo abanyamakuru bigeze bahindura aho bahagaze kuri iyi ngingo? Nkյrugero kuba babogamira cyangwa bakitandukanya nյbumenyi buriho kuri iyo ngingo cyangwa bakabogamira cyangwa bakitandukanya nթkerekezo cya Leta. Kugira ngo umuntu abashe gusubiza ibibazo biteye gutya agomba gusesesengura ikivugwa. Nkյko Berelson (1971, p. 18) na Holsti (1969, p. 14) babivuga, gusesengura ikivugwa bigomba gukurikiza aya mahame: gukorwa ku buryo butabogamye kandi bugendera kuri gahunda. Iyo aya mahame yombi yubahirijwe abashakashatsi batandukanye ariko bakora ku nyandiko zimwe bagomba kugera ku musaruro umwe. Ikindi kandi Berelson (1971, Idem) avuga ko gusesengura ikivugwa bijyana nթsobanura nyamubaro. Ibi bikavuga ko gusesengura ikivugwa bishingiye ku buryo bwյbushakashatsi nyamubaro kubera ko buba bugamije kugaragaza ku buryo bubarika amakuru avangitiranye hakurikijwe amatsinda yagenwe, hakurikijwe kandi nաmabwiriza yյbushakashatsi. Uburyo bwo kubara bwongera insobanuro ku myumvire yյburyo bugiye kuri gahunda kandi butabogamye. Ibyo bituma umushakashatsi yemeza neza ko mu gihe runaka, ku buryo bufitiwe gihamya, ikinyamakuru iki nթki ugereranije nթbindi binyamakuru, kibanze ku nkuru runaka. Berelson (1952, p. 18) akomoza ku ԫivugwa kigaragaraծ Ibi bikavuga ko iri sesengura riba rigamije guhishura ikivugwa kiba gisa nթkigaragara ku ngingo iyi ni iyi. Ibyo bigatandukana nթmyumvire ya Holsti (1969, Idem), we wibanda ku cyo yita ԩkivugwa kihisheծ Ibi bikavuga inyito yihishe munsi yյturango twթkivugwa turi ahagaragara. Itoranywa ryթnyandiko mu gusesengura ikivugwaItoranywa ryթnyandiko zikoreshwa mu gusesengura ikivugwa rikorwa mu byiciro byinshi. Nյbwo muri rusange uburyo bukoreshwa hatoranywa inyandiko zitandukanye ari bumwe, aha turibanda ku buryo bwo gutoranya inyandiko zթbitangazamakuru bwibanzweho cyane na Bryman (2008, p. 278). Gutoranya ibitangazamakuruUbushakashatsi bwiga ibijyanye nթbitangazamakuru, akenshi busaba kugaragaza ibibazo byյbushakashatsi biteye gutya: icyo ҸӠihagarariye mu bitangazamakuru. ҸӠishobora kuba ihagarariye ishyirahamwe ryաbakozi, ibura ryթbiribwa, icyaha cyյbugome, nթbindi. Ahangaha ikibazo nyoborabushakashatsi kiba giteye ku buryo bukurikira: ni ikihe gitangazamakuru kibanda kuri imwe muri izi ngingo? Byaba ari ikinyamakuru cyandika cyangwa igishushanya, televisiyo cyangwa radiyo? Icyo gihe umushakashatsi akomeza kwibaza niba, nkյrugero ari igitangazamakuru cyandika, ni ubuhe bwoko bwթkinyamakuru: byaba se ari ikinyamakuru cyo ku rwego ruciriritse cyangwa icyo mu rwego rwo hejuru? Niba se ari ikinyamakuru cyo mu rwego rwo hejuru, cyaba se ari icyandikirwa imbere mu gihugu cyangwa hanze yթgihugu? None se inkuru zose ziri mu kinyamakuru zose zigomba gusesengurwa? Reka dufate urugero rwյbushakashatsi bwakozwe na Mukama (2018), aho yigaga isano iri hagati yթbyifuzo bya Guverinoma yյ Rwanda kuri politiki yթyakure mu burezi nթshyirwa mu bikorwa ryayo. Muri ubu bushakashatsi, Mukama yasesenguye ibyifuzo bya Guverinoma kuri politiki yթyakure mu nyandiko 13 zakozwe kuva mu mwaka wa 2001 ari na wo ntangiro yթkerekezo cyյ Rwanda 2020 kugeza muri 2016 ubwo yakoraga ubwo bushakashatsi. Mu gusesengura izo nyandiko, Mukama yasanzemo imvugo (discourses) umunani zigaragaza ibyifuzo bya Guverinoma kuri iyo politiki: kwegereza uburezi bose, kuzamura ireme ryյburezi, uburezi busubiza ibibazo byաbaturage, uburezi budahenze, gukwiza uburezi hose, kwigira mu burezi, gukoresha ikoranabuhanga mu kwiga nյburezi budaheza. Cyakora Mukama yasanze izo mvugo zigaragara mu nyandiko zimwe na zimwe gusa.Nyuma yo gucukumbura izo mvugo no kwiga impamvu zatumye Guverinoma yյ Rwanda ari zo yibandaho, Mukama yasesenguye uko politiki yթyakure yagiye ishyirwa mu bikorwa nթbigo bya Leta bishinzwe kwigisha hakoreshejwe iyakure mu gihe kթmyaka itanu, ni ukuvuga kuva muri 2012 kugeza muri 2016. Yifashishije inama zյndi mushakashatsi Fejes (2005) maze yiga isano ya politiki yթyakure nթshyirwa mu bikorwa ryayo. Feyes uwo agereranya iryo sesengura nko kwiga igisekuru cyյmuryango umeze nkթgiti cyagabye amashami. Avuga ko umushakashatsi asubira inyuma akiga buri shami nյko ryera imbuto. Aha ishami twarigereranya nթmvugo. Kwiga ibyanditswe rero kuri ubu buryo, byatumye Mukama amenya uko ibigo bishinzwe gushyira mu bikorwa politiki yթyakure byumvise buri mvugo nթngaruka zatewe no kuyishyira mu bikorwa cyangwa se kutayishyira mu bikorwa. Ikindi ubu bushakashatsi bwagaragaje, ni uko hari ubwo ibyifuzo bya Guverinoma kuri politiki yյburezi bigarukira mu byifuzo gusa, bigasa nkաho nta we bireba mu kubishyira mu bikorwa.Nkյko bigaragara muri ubu bushakashatsi bwa Mukama (2018), mu gutoranya inyandiko zյbu bwoko ni ngombwa no gutekereza ku matariki. Nta cyo byaba bimaze gushaka inyandiko zanditswe ku gikorwa iki nթki kandi cyari kitaraba. Urugero twatanga ni nko gushaka inkuru zanditswe ku itorwa rwa Perezida Paul Kagame wյ Rwanda ku buyobozi bwՕmuryango wՁfurika Yunze Ubumwe muri 2016 kandi icyo gihe yari ataratorerwa kuwuyobora. Mu nkuru yanditse mu Mvaho Nshya ku wa 28 Mutarama 2018, Mutungirehe yanditse ko Kagame yatangiye imirimo ye yo kuyobora Afurika Yunze Ubumwe kuva ku wa 28 Mutarama 2018. Iyo umushakashatsi amaze kwemeza itariki aheraho agomba no kwemeza iyo azagarukiraho bitewe nթmpamvu zitandukanye: imiterere yթkibazo nyoborabushakashatsi, intego zյbushakashatsi, igihe afite cyo gukora ubushakashatsi, ingano yյmubare wթnkuru akeneye, nթbindi. Utubango tubarwa mu gusesengura ikivugwaIkibazo nyoborabushakashatsi ni ryo pfundo umushakashatsi aheraho kugira ngo afate ikemezo ku tubango twթngenzi agomba kubara mu gusesengura ikivugwa. Muri iri sesenguramakuru hari utubango twյbwoko bwinshi dushobora gusensengurwa. 1 Abafite uruhare rugaragara mu nkuru Aha ni ngombwa kumenya uwanditse iyo nkuru, uwanditsweho mu nkuru, abatanze amakuru yashingiweho mu kwandika inkuru, nթbindi. 2 AmagamboNյbwo Bryman (2008, p. 280) avuga ko iki gikorwa gisa nkթgikorwa kidashamaje, bijya biba ngombwa ko umushakashatsi ashaka kumenya inshuro amagambo amwe nաmwe yagiye agaruka kenshi mu nyandiko. Kuba amagambo amwe nաmwe yakoreshejwe kurusha ayandi akenshi bigira icyo bisobanura kubera ko ashobora kugira uruhare mu gutuma igikorwa iki nթki cyamamara. Igice kihariye cyյbumenyi cyangwa insanganyamatsikoMuri iri sesenguramakuru umushakashatsi akenera kumenya igice cyյbumenyi igikorwa iki nթki giherereyemo. Nko mu rwego rwյbumenyi nyamuntu umushakashi ashobora gushyira ikibazo iki nթki mu rwego rwյbukungu, ubucuruzi nթcungamutungo, imitekerereze, ibya politiki cyangwa mu ruhurirane rwյbumenyi. Iyo ibibazo byashyizwe mu mwanya wabyo hakoreshejwe insanganyamatsiko, icyo gihe isesenguramakuru ntiriba rireba gusa ikivugwa kigaragara ahubwo ryibanda mu gucukumbura ikivugwa kihishe mu byanditse cyangwa mu byavuzwe. Nko mu rugero twavuze haruguru ku bushakashatsi bwo gusesengura isano iri hagati yթbyifuzo bya Guverinoma yյ Rwanda kuri politiki yթyakure mu burezi nթshyirwa mu bikorwa ryabyo (Mukama, 2018). Imbonerahamwe ikurikira iragaragaza ubucucike bwa buri mvugo mu nyandiko 13 Mukama yakozeho ubwo bushakashatsi.Ubu buryo bushobora kandi gukoreshwa mu gusesengura ireme ryաmakuru nyamimerere yakusanyijwe. Icyo gihe umushakashatsi akenera gusesengura amakuru yatanzwe mu gusubiza ibibazo bifunguye bikamufasha kumenya icyo abantu batekereza, ku buryo bwimbitse, ku kibazo runaka cyabajijwe. Kugira ngo aka kazi korohe, ni ngombwa guhanga imbata yթnkurikizo kugira ngo buri gisubizo gihuzwe nթngingo cyangwa insangamatsiko yihariye yateguwe. Isesengura ryաmakuru nyamubaroMbere yo gukusanya amakuru ayo ari yo yose yյbushakashatsi ni byiza gutekereza ku buryo ayo makuru azasesengurwa. Kuva mu ntangiriro umushakashatsi arimo gutegura urutonde rwթbibazo bizifashishwa mu gukusanya amakuru ni ngombwa no gutekereza kuri tekiniki azakoresha mu gihe cyo kuyasesengura. Ibi bijyana kandi no gutekereza hakiri kare kuri gahunda izakurikizwa mu kwitegereza ndetse nթmbata yթnkurikizo izifashishwa. Mu gusobanura akamaro kյbu buryo bwթmikorere, Bryman (2008, p. 314) atanga impamvu ebyiri zթngenzi:1. Tekinike zթsesengura zigomba guhura neza nթmfatashusho zյbushakashatsi. Ibyo byoroha iyo umushakashatsi yumva neza uburyo imfatashusho zitandukanye zյbushakashatsi zizatondekwa. 2. Bitewe nթngano nթmiterere yթtsinda nkeshwamakuru bishobora gutuma umushakashatsi ahitamo hakiri kare tekiniki zihariye mu gusesengura amakuru azabona. Tugerageje gusobanura kurushaho ubu buryo bwթmigirire, twatanga urugero rurambuye aho umushakashatsi yaba ashaka kumenya uruhare rwթkoranabuhanga mu kongera ubushobozi bwթngo. Ubu bushakashatsi bwaba buhereye ku nyandiko nyinshi zivuga ko uko ikoranabuhanga ryagiye ritera imbere, ubukungu bwաbantu, cyanecyane ubwթngo zabo, bwagiye bwiyongera kurushaho. Uku kwiyongera kյbukungu kukaba kwaragiye guhera ku bushobozi bwաbantu mu kubona uburyo butandukanye buborohereza gukora ibikorwa bitandukanye bibateza imbere. Aha twavuga nko kohererezanya amafaranga, kubona amakuru ku masoko yo kugurishaho umusaruro, kugurizanya amafaranga, gushakisha akazi nթbindi. Duhereye ku byanditswe kuri iyi ngingo yյbushakashatsi, biroroshye kugira amakuru anyuranye avuye mu bushakashatsi bwakozwe nաbandi. Twe icyo dukenera ni ukumenya niba mu mudugudu runaka abaturage bawo bumva kimwe akamaro kթkoranabuhanga mu kwiteza imbere mu ngo zabo. Kugira ngo tubashe gucukumbura aya makuru neza tugomba kwibaza ku mfatashusho duhereye ku itsinda nkeshwamakuru. Nkյko Frankfort-Nachmias na Nachmias (2008, PP. 49 Р52) babisobanura, ibibazo byյbushakashatsi biba bihetswe nթtsinda ryթnshoza. Ariko akenshi izo nshoza ziba ziri mu buryo budafatika. Kugira ngo zumvikane kurushaho biba ngombwa ko zihindurwamo utubango dufata imisusire ishobora guhinduka kandi ikabarwa ku buryo bufatika ari hano twise imfatashusho. Ibi bigasobanura ko imfatashusho ishobora kubarwa hakoresheshwe imibare ibiri cyangwa irenga bitewe nաgaciro kayo. Urugero twatanga ni nkթnshoza yթkiciro cyյbudehe mu Rwanda. Ikiciro cyյbudehe ni imfatashusho kuko gishobora guhabwa agaciro ku buryo butandukanye. Bishobora kuba ari ikiciro cyo hasi, hagati, giciriritse, ndetse nթcyo hejuru. Ni kimwe nթyo umuntu yareba inshoza yթkizere abantu bafitiye umushinga uyu nյyu, umushakashatsi yakigabamo ibice bibiri: ikizere kiri hasi cyangwa kiri hejuru. Frankfort-Nachmias na Nachmias (2008: idem) bateganya ubwoko butatu bwթngenzi bwթmfatashusho: imfatashusho yigenga, imfatashusho igengwa nթmfatashusho igenzura. Imfatashusho igengwa ni itanga igisobanuro kթkibazo umushakashatsi yabonye naho iyigenga ni imfatashusho ihagaririye ikibazo umushakashatis ashaka gusobanura. Ku buryo bugaragara hakoreshwa iyi nganyagaciro: Y= f(x). Y ihagarariye imfatashusho igengwa naho X ikaba imfatashusho yigenga. Bivuze ko ikibazo Y giterwa nթmpamvu X. Naho imfatashusho igenzura ni imfatashusho iba itatekerejweho mu ntangiriro yյbushakashatsi. Urugero ni uko umushakashatsi yatangira yibaza igituma abanyeshuri bo muri Kamizuza yյ Rwanda batsindwa agatekereza ko byaba ari uko badashyira umuhate mu kwiga ariko yamara gukora ubushakashatsi agasanga biterwa nյko badafite ibikoresho bihagije. Icyo gihe iyo mpamvu ibonetse nyuma ni imfatashusho igenzura ebyiri za mbere zari zatekerejweho ari zo gutsindwa (imfatashusho igengwa) no kutagira umuhate mu kwiga (imfatashusho yigenga). Mu gutoranya itsinda nkeshwamakuru, turakoresha uburyo bwa tombora dutoranye ingo 20 mu mudugudu ufite ingo 50. Tumaze kwemeza izo ngo, turafata umwanzuro ko tuzabaza umutware wa buri rugo bivuze ko amakuru azatangwa nաbantu 20. Mu gutegura ibibazo tuzabaza abagize izo ngo twifashishije imfatashusho zթngenzi zikurikira: igitsina cyյmutangamakuru, imyaka ye, kuba akoresha ikoranabuhanga, ubwoko bwթkoranabuhanga akoresha cyane, inshuro akoresha ikoranabuhanga, impamvu akoresha ikoranabuhanga, umubare wաmafaranga yinjiza mu rugo. Mukumenya uyu mubare turashingira ku mibare itangwa mu nyandiko ya Cho na Kim yitwa ҄eterminants of poverty in RwandaӠbasohoye muri 2017 aho bashyira umurongo wյbukene ku mafaranga 45000 Frw ku muntu mu mwaka. Ni ukuvuga ko urugo rurimo umuntu umwe cyangwa barenga binjiza amafaranga yյ Rwanda arenga 45000; urwo rugo ruba rwararenze umurongo wյbukene. Ayo makuru amaze kumenyakana twakora urutonde ryթbibazo ku buryo bukurikira: Kodi1Uri umugore cyangwa umugabo: (Hitamo 1 kuri gabo cyangwa 2 kuri gore) Umugabo _____________________ Umugore _____________________122Ufite imyaka ingahe? ______________3Ukoresha ikoranabuhanga? Ibi bivuga ko hari igihe utanga amakuru ashobora kuba hari ibibazo atashatse gusubiza. Icyo gihe ahatabonetse igisubizo turahashyira umubare 0. Iyo ibyo birangiye buri mfatashusho igendanye na buri kibazo cyabajijwe turayiha umubare uyiranga ubanzirizwa nթmpine yթjambo imfatashusho. Urugero twakwandika imfa0001, imfa0002, tugakomeza bitewe nյmubare wթbibazo. Aha umubare wa nyuma waba imfa0009.Duhereye kuri rwa rutonde rwթbibazo twari twoherereje buri mutware wյrugo, turajya dushyira akamenyetso kuri kodi ijyanye nթgisubizo yatanze.Kugira ngo tubashe guha igisobanuro ibisubizo buri mutware wյrugo yatanze, ni ngombwa kubanza kubihuriza mu mbata yթnkurikizo idufasha kubona ishusho rusange yabyo biri hamwe. Mu buryo bwo koroshya akazi twifashisha porogaramu zabugenewe za mudasobwa nka Excel cyangwa impuzamakuru (izizwi cyane ni nka MATLAB, SPSS, na Statistix). Duhereye ku rudonde rwթbisubizo byatanzwe nյmwe mu basubije, twakuzuza imbata yթnkurikizo ku buryo bukurikira: Imbonerahamwe 2: Uko buzuza imbata yթnkurikizoImfa0001Imfa0002Imfa0003Imfa0004Imfa0005Imfa0006Imfa0007Imfa0008Imfa00092302113112Aha turakomeza kuzuza buri mibare iranga buri gisuzubizo. Niturangiza kuyuzuza muri iyi mbata yթnkurikizo turatangira kureba imiterere ya buri gisubizo. Urebye uko ibi bisubizo biteye biratandukanye. Ku bibazo bimwe ni ukuzuza umubare wuzuye nko ku kibazo cya 2. Ahandi nko ku kibazo cya 1 cyangwa icya 3, usubiza yari yahawe guhitamo hatagati ya 1 cyangwa 2. Naho ikibazo cya 6 kirabaza umubare wթnshuro bikaba bivuze ko tugomba kumenya abakoresha ikoranabuhanga inshuro nyinshi cyangwa nkeya. Nkյko twabibonye duhereye ku nyandiko ya Frankfort-Nachmias na Nachmias (2008, pp. 49 Р52), dushobora gusobanura imfatashusho duhereye ku isano iri hagati yazo. Ariko iyo bigeze mu ikusanyamakuru no mu isesenguramakuru ni ngombwa kuzitandukanya duhereye ku mikoreshereze yazo. Duhereye ku bisobanuro birambuye byatanzwe na Bryman (2008, p. 321) tubona ubwoko bwթmfatashusho bwթngenzi bukirikira: Imfatashusho nyamubaro: urugero ni nkթntera iri hagati ya buri gihe, inshuro nyinshi, cyangwa nke cyane. Izi ntera ntizingana;  Imfatashusho igena intera: birashoboka ko twaba twatanze uburyo bwo gusubiza bugena intera zingana hagati yթbisubizo. Urugero ni nkթkibazo cya 9 aho twashyize intera ingana hagati yյmubare wաmafranga umukuru wյrugo yinjiza mu kwezi: 1.000 Frw Р5.000Frw Р10.000 Frw Р15.000Frw; Imfatashusho nyazina: aha urugero twatanga ni ikibazo cya 4 aho usubiza agomba guhitamo hagati yաmagambo akurikira: Ubuhinzi nյbworozi (1), akazi ka Leta (2) akazi kաbikorera (3), ndikorera (4); Imfatashusho nyabubiri: izi ni imfatashusho ziba zifite amakuru agabanije ukubiri gusa. Urugero ni nkթkibazo cya 1, icya 3 nթcya 5. a. 	Isesengura ryթmfatashusho imweMu gusesengura, umushakashatsi akoresha imbonerahamwe yerekana umubare wաbantu ndetse nթjanisha ryabo. Imbonerahamwe yerekana umubare wաbantu nթjanisha ryաbagore nաbagabo. Imbonerahamwe 3: IbisubizoIgitsinaUmubareIjanisha (%)Abagabo1260Abagore840Igiteranyo20100Imbonerahamwe 4: IbisubizoAbakoresha ikoranabuhangaUmubareIjanisha (%)Yego1680Oya420Igiteranyo20100Imbonerahamwe ya 3 iragaragaza ko mu bisubizo twasesenguye twasanze umubare wաbagabo ari 12 bivuze ko bahagarariye ijanisha rya 60 ku mubare wաbabajijwe bose. Naho umubare wաbagore ukaba 8, ufashe ijanisha rya 40 mu babajijwe bose. No mu mbonerahamwe ya 4 ibisubizo bya Yego biragaragaza ijanisha rya 80 bivuze umubare wաbakoresha ikoranabuhanga naho Oya ikaba 20% bivuze abatarikoresha. Uburyo bwթsensengura ryթmfatashusho imwe bwakoreshwa no ku zindi zose zagaragajwe mu bibazo byabajijwe. Uburyo bwo kwerekana ibivuye mu isensengura bushobora kuba ubu bwթmbonerahamwe cyangwa ubundi bukoresha amashusho nյbwoko butandukanye. b. 	Isesengura ryթmfatashusho ebyeriUbu buryo bukoreshwa iyo dushaka guhuza imfatashusho ebyiri kugira ngo turebe niba hari aho zihurira. Hakoreshwa uburyo butandukanye bitewe nյbwoko bwթmfatashusho. Urugero twatanga ni nkթgihe twakenera kumenya niba imyaka cyangwa igitsina byաbasubije bifite aho bihuriye nյburyo abatware bթngo bakoresha ikoranabuhanga. Imbonerahamwe 5Gukoresha ikoranabuhangaIgitsinaAbagaboAbagoreUmubareIjanisha (%)UmubareIjanisha (%)Yego 840840Oya42000Igiteranyo1260840Mu gusesengura byimbitse amakuru ari muri iyi mbonerahamwe ya 5, biragaragara ko nյbwo umubare wաbagabo uruta uwաbagore, umubare wաbagore bakoresha ikoranabuhanga ungana nյwաbagabo barikoresha. Ibyo bikavuga ko abagore ari bo bakataje mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga. c. 	Isesengurengura ryթmfatashusho nyinshiDuhereye ku mbonerahamwe ya 5, aho twakoze isesengura ryթmfatashusho ebyiri zigaragaza isano iri hagati yթgitsina no gukoresha ikoranabunga, dushobora no kureba aho izi ebyiri zishobora guhurira nթzindi mfatashusho zigaragazwa nաmakuru yatanzwe. Aha twahera ku mfatashusho ijyanye nթnshuro abagore cyangwa abagabo bakoresha ikoranabuhanga cyangwa se nթmpamvu zituma barikoresha. Muri rusange icyo tugomba kwitondera ni ukureba niba koko hari isano nyayo iri hagati yթzo mfatashusho zose kuko hari igihe nta sano ifatika iba ihari. Umwanzuro Mu kwandika uyu mutwe wթgitabo twibanze cyane ku bice bibiri byթngenzi byթyoboramikorere mu bushakashatsi ari byo: ikusanyamakuru nթsesenguramakuru. Nkյko twabigaragaje, ibi bice byombi bibanzirizwa nթbindi byթngenzi ari byo gutegura ubushakashatsi no kugena itsinda nkeshwamakuru. Iyo itsinda rimaze kuboneka nյmubare wաbazatanga amakuru wemejwe, umushakashatsi afata amwanya wo gutegura ibikoresho nkusanyamakuru azifashisha. Ibyo bikoresho bigendera ku bwoko bwաmakuru azakenerwa yaba ari agendeye ku ireme cyangwa ku mibare. Nkյko byasobanuwe kandi bikanatangirwa ingero, iyo amakuru amaze kuboneka umushakashatsi akurikizaho guhanga imbata yթnkurikizo izamufasha gusesengura amakuru. Nkյko byagaragaye, biba byiza iyo ibi biteguwe mbere yo kugena ibibazo bizabazwa ndetse hakaba nթgerageza ryյrutonde rwթbibazo. Iki gikorwa gifasha kumenya niba nta bibazo bitumvikana neza byaba bihari bigakosorwa hakiri kare. Nյbwo uyu mutwe ushobora kuba utavuye imuzingo inzira zose zikoreshwa mu gukusanya no gusesengura amakuru yյbushakashashatsi, turizera ko uburyo bwasobanuwe buhagije kugira ngo umushakashatsi wumva ururimi rwՉkinyarwanda acengere uburyo bwթngenzi yakoresha mu bushakashatsi bwe ku buryo bwa gihanga. IndangasokoBerelson, B. Kenshi na kenshi abashakashatsi bաbatangizi bibaza ibibazo nyamubaro ariko mu kubisesengura bagakoresha ijanisha gusa. Kuba rero twahisemo uyu mutwe wihariye ku gusesengura amakuru nyamubaro ukoresheje ibarurishamibare ntabwo tugamije kwigisha isomo ryթbarurishamibare, ahubwo twahisemo ingero nkeya zikunze gukoreshwa kugira ngo dutange urumuri rwյko umushakashatsi yakusanya amakuru nyamubaro, uko yayasesengura akoresheje intoki cyangwa porogaramu yթkoranabuhanga yabugenewe izwi nka Microsoft Excel. Ntabwo twashatse gukoresha ikoranabuhanga ryabugenewe kandi ryihutisha gusesengura amakuru nyamubaro mu bumenyi bwթmibanire yաbantu nka SPSS (Statistical Package for the Social Sciences) kubera inzitizi zթkoranabuhanga ridahagije mu bihugu bikiri mu nzira yաmajyambere harimo nյ Rwanda. Twahisemo rero uburyo bushobora gukoreshwa na buri mushakashatsi ubishaka atagombye kwifashisha ikoranabuhanga rihambaye. Ibi bisobanuye ko hari itandukaniro rinini hagati yաbahungu nաbakobwa mu buryo bahitamo kwiga amasomo yՉkinyarwanda, Icyongereza nթmibare.Isesengura ryթsano iri hagati yթmfatashusho ebyeriIsano ni uburyo bukoreshwa mu ibarurishamibare hagati yթmfatashusho ebyiri hagamijwe kureba uburemere bwթryo sano ndetse nթkerekezo cyaryo. Ku byerekeye uburemere bwթsano, agaciro karyo gapimwa hagati ya б na +1. Iyo agaciro kթsano kangana na  1, byerekana ko imfatashusho ebyiri zihuye ku buryo bwuzuye. Uko agaciro kթsano kagenda gasatira umubare 0, isano hagati yթmfatashusho ebyiri igenda iba nto cyangwa se icika intege. Ikerekezo kթsano kigaragaza uburyo imfatashusho ebyiri zibanye: zishobora kubana mu buryo bwo kuzuzanya (positive correlation) cyangwa mu buryo bwo guhungana (negative correlation). Ikerekezo kթsano hagati yթmfatashusho ebyiri zuzuzanya kigaragazwa nթkimenyetso cyo guteranya (+). Naho ikerekezo kթsano hagati yթmfatashusho zihungana kigaragazwa nթkimenyetso cyo gukuramo (-). Amashusho akurikira arerekana amasano ashoboka hagati yթzi mfatashusho ebyiri. Igishushanyo-mbonerahamwe: Agaciro nթkerekezo kթsano hagati yթmfatashusho ebyiriAho byavuye: Kiatdd (2012) Ubusanzwe mu ibarurishamibare hari ubwoko bune bwաmasano: isano rya Pearson, isano rya Kendall, Isano rya Spearman, nթsano bita Ԑoint-Biserialծ Muri iyi nyandiko, turibanda ku isano rya Spearman nթrya Pearson. Isesengura ryթsano riri hagati yթmfatashusho ebyiri ukoresheje isano ryյmwanya rya Spearman (soma ғipiyamaniөUbu buryo bwo gushaka isano ryթbarurishamibare riri hagati yթmyanya (nkյko wavuga uti ҵyu yabaye iwa mbere, undi aba uwa kabiri, undi uwa gatatu, gutyogutyo) nթmfatashusho ebyiri, bwahimbwe na Charles Spearman, bakunze kubwita isano ryյmwanya rya Spearman cyangwa se Spearman Rho (soma Ғoө. Iri sano bakunze kuryerekana bakoresheje inyuguti yթkigereki ya ғ (rho) cyangwa bakaryerekena bakoresheje ҲsӮ Isano hagati yթmfatashusho ebyiri rishobora kuva kuri +1 kugera kuri б gusa. Niba iri sano ringana na + 1 cyangwa Р1 ni ukuvuga ko izo mfatashusho zikurikira inzira idahinduka rwose. Ikimenyetso cya teranya (+) cyagnwa kuramo (Щ gishobora kujya imbere yթngano ya rs kerekana ikerekezo kթsano riri hagati ya X (imfatashusho yigenga) na Y (imfatashusho ngengwa). Niba Y yiyongera mu gihe X na yo yiyongera, icyo gihe ikerekezo kթsano rs kiba na cyo kizamuka (positive). Ariko niba Y igenda igabanuka mu gihe X yo yiyongera, icyo gihe, ikerekezo kթsano rs kiba kimanuka (negative). Niba isano rya Spearman rs ari zero ni ukuvuga ko nta mpinduka yabaye: ntabwo bigaragara ko Y yiyongera cyangwa ko igabanuka mu gihe X yiyongera.Urugero 1:Ese uri mu kihe kiciro cyաmanota mu isomo ryo gusoma Ikinyarwanda?Ndatsina cyaneNdatsinda bisanzwe NdageragezaNdatsindwaUrugero 2:Ese ibyo usoma muri iki gitabo urabyumva?Ndabyumva cyaneNdabyumva mu rugeroMbyumva gahoroSimbyumvaSimbyumva na mbaIzi ngero zirerekana ko ibisubizo byաbatangamakuru ushobora kubikurikiranya mu byiciro. Abanyeshuri babonye amanota ari mu kiciro cya A kugera kuri D kandi turibuka ko A = 1; B = 2; C = 3 na D = 4. Ni iyo mibare yanditse mu rubariro rwa mbere nյrwa kabiri. Mu rubariro rwa gatatu nյrwa kane, twashyizemo umwanya umunyeshuri afite bitewe nթkiciro amanota ye arimo muri buri somo. Duhereye ku Kinyarwanda, Umunyeshuri uri mu kiciro cya 1 twamuhaye umwanya wa 1. Abanyeshuri bari mu kiciro cya 2 ni 3. Ubwo umwanya wabo ni 2, 3, na 4. Kubera ko bari ku mwanya umwe, turateranya imyanya yabo maze tugabanye umubare wabo ari wo 3. Ni ukuvuga (2 + 3 + 4) / 3 = 3. Bari ku mwanya wa 3. Abari ku kiciro cya 3 na bo ni 3. Ubwo umwanya wabo ni 5, 6, 7. Kubera ko bari ku mwanya umwe, turateranya imyanya yabo maze tugabanye umubare wabo ari wo 3. Ni ukuvuga (5 + 6 + 7) / 3 = 6. Umunyeshuri uri mu kiciro 4 ni umwe, ni ukuvuga ko ari ku mwanya ukurikiyeho ari wo wa 8.Ku mfatashusho ya kabiri igaragaza amanota yթmibare naho turabigenza nkյko twabibaze mu Kinyarwanda. Umunyeshuri uri mu kiciro cya 1 ni umwe, ubwo ari ku mwanya wa 1. Abanyeshuri bari mu kiciro cya 2 ni 3. Ubwo imyanya yabo ni 2, 3, na 4. Ni ukuvuga ko umwanya wabo bose hamwe turawubona dufashe (2 + 3 + 4) / 3 = 3. Abanyeshuri bari mu kiciro cya 3 ni babiri. Ubwo umwanya wabo turawubona dufashe (5 + 6) / 2 = 5.5. Abanyeshuri bari mu kiciro cya 4 ni 2. Umwanya wabo turawubona dufashe (7 + 8) / 2 = 7.5.Muri iriya nzira ihinnye yo kubara, inyuguti ҤӠihagarariye ikinyuranyo hagati yթmyanya umunyeshuri yabonye mu masomo atandukanye. Umwanzuro:Biragaragara rero ko hari isano rizamuka (rs = 0.87) hagati yթbyiciro byաmanota yՉkinyarwanda nաyթmibare, t (6) = 4.32, p < .01. Ibi bivuze ko kugira amanota yo mu kiciro cyo hejuru mu Kinyarwanda bifitanye isano no kigira amanota yo mu kiciro cyo hejuru mu mibare.Isesengura ryթsano riri hagati yթmfatashusho ebyiri ukoresheje isano rya Pearson rIsano rya Pearson r ni ryo rikunda gukoreshwa cyane mu ibarurishamibare kugira ngo hagaragazwe igipimo kթsano hagati yթmfatashusho ebyiri. Tugomba kwibuka ko kuba hari isano hagati yթmfatashusho A nթmfatashusho B bitavuze ko A ituma habaho B cyangwa ko B iterwa na A (causation). Oya rwose, si cyo bivuga. Ahubwo bivuze ko bifitanye isano gusa. Iri sano rikoreshwa iyo imfatashusho ebyiri zifite agaciro mubare kթbipimo byթntera (interval scale) cyangwa byթbigereranyo (ratio scale, i.e. continuous). Reka dufate ingero.  Turifuza kumenya niba hari isano hagati yաmanota umunyeshuri yagize mu isomo ryթmibare (imfatashusho Ҹө nաmanota yagize mu myitwarire (imfatashusho ҹө. Turifuza kumenya niba hari isano hagati yթzo mfatashusho zombi, uburemere bwթryo sano ndetse nթkerekezo cyaryo. Dushaka kumenya niba hari isano hagati yթmyaka yաbantu nkeshwamakuru nյmubare wաmafaranga binjiza. Reka dufate urugero rwa mbere. Dufite abanyeshuri 10. Buri wese yahawe amanota mu isomo ryթmibare, ahabwa nաmanota ajyanye nթmyitwarire ku ishuri. Turibaza niba hari isano riri hagati yաmanota abanyeshuri bagize mu mibare nաyo bagize mu myitwarire. Mu yandi magambo, turibaza niba abanyeshuri bagize amanota menshi mu mibare ari na bo bagira menshi mu myitwarire cyangwa se niba ntaho bihuriye. Yerekana uburemere nթkerekezo byթsano hagati yթmfatashusho ebyiri. Urugero twafashe muri uyu mutwe rwagaragaje ko r ifite agaciro kangana na 0.537. Uyu ni umubare wemeza. Bivuze ko hari isano yemeza iri mu rugero hagati yաmanota abanyeshuri babona mu mibare nաyo babona mu myitwarire. Muri make, iyo amanota yo mu mibare yiyongereye, amanota yo mu myitwarire nayo ariyongera ku kigero kimwe. Mu yandi magambo, abanyeshuri bafite amanota menshi mu mibare nibo bagira amanota menshi mu myitwarire.Ntitwagombye kwibagirwa ko muri uru rugero twatanze, itsinda nkeshwamakuru ryari rigizwe nաbantu 10 gusa. Birushaho kuba byiza iyo isano rya Pearson ishatswe hakoreshejwe itsinda nkeshwamakuru rigizwe nաbantu barenze icumi. Isesengura ryթmpinduka iri hagati yաmatsinda nkeshwamakuru yigengaIsesengura rya Mann-Whitney (soma Mani Witine) РImfatashusho zյruhererekane (ordinal variables)Ibisubizo byթbibazo twabajije ku bipimo byթnkurukirane (ordinal scale) dushobora kubisesengura tugereranya amatsinda yաbahungu nաbakobwa. Icyo gihe, turifashisha isesengura rya Mann-Whitney (soma Mani Witine) ari ryo bita mu rurimi rwՉcyongereza ҍann-Whitney U TestӮIkibazo cyյbushakashatsi turaba dushaka gusubiza ni iki: ҅se hari itandukaniro hagati yաbahungu nաbakobwa mu byiciro byաmanota bagize mu isomo ryՉkinyarwanda?ӠTwibukiranye ko icyo kibazo kibajije kuri ubu buryo:Ni ikihe kiciro cyաmanota wagize mu kizamini cya Leta mu Kinyarwanda?	Ikiciro A (90Р100%)Ikiciro B (80 Р89%)Ikiciro C (70 Р79%)Ikiciro D (60 Р69%)Dore rero inzira ihinnye ikoreshwa mu isesengura ryթsuzuma rya U rya MannWhitney:U1 = n1n2 + n1(n21 + 1) РR1U2 = n1n2 + n2(n22 + 1) РR2u1 = Igipimo cya U cya Mann-Whitney mu itsinda rya 1 u2 = Igipimo cya U cya Mann-Whitney mu itsinda rya 2 n1 = Umubare wաbagize itsinda nkeshwamakuru rya 1 n2 = Umubare wաbagize itsinda nkeshwamakuru rya 2 R1= Igiteranyo kթmyanya yթbyiciro byաmanota yթtsinda rya 1R2 = Igiteranyo kթmyanya yթbyiciro byաmanota yթtsinda rya 2AbakobwaAbahunguUmwanya wթkiciro cyաmanota yաbakobwaUmwanya wթkiciro cyաmanota yաbahungu 421663311.511.54116221623211.5613211.53211.56431611.526R1 = 90.5R2 = 62.5Uko babara umwanya wթkiciro cyաmanota yյmunyeshuri: ni uguhera ku mubare muto ukabara inshuro zose uwo mubare wisubiramo mu matsinda yombi. Isano ryյmwanya ushingiye ku bimenyetso (ҫӠcyangwa ҭҩ rya Wilcoxon (soma җilikogusoniө ryita ku manota cyangwa ibipimo buri muntu umwe umwe yagize mu bihe bitandukanye ndetse no ku itandukana ryթbimenyetso byթkinyuranyo cyաyo manota cyangwa ibyo bipimo. Birumvikana ko nթngano yթkinyuranyo yitabwaho. Isano ryյmwanya ushingiye ku bimenyetso rya Wilcoxon risobanurwa neza na Sullivan (2017) kandi yifashishishije ingero zifatika.Reka twifashishe urugero kugira ngo turisobanure neza. Abanyeshuri 8 bakoze ikizamini kimwe inshuro ebyiri, mbere yթsomo na nyuma yթsomo. Ibi bishatse kuvuga ko ikizamini kimwe cyakoreshejwe abanyeshuri bamwe inshuri ebyiri. Umubare muto uragira umwanya wa mbere, ugakomeza uko imibare igenda isumbana kugera ku wa nyuma. Iyo ibinyuranyo binganya agaciro utitaye ku bimenyetso byabyo, urabiteranya ukabara impuzandengo akaba ari yo iba umwanya wayo (mean rank). Iyo hari ibinyuranyo bibiri bingana na zero, impuzandengo ya mbere uyiha ikimenyetso cya ҐӠindi ukayiha icya ҫӮ Iyo amazeru ari atatu cyangwa se igiharwe, imwe urayisiba.Ikinyuranyo cyաmanota ya mbere na nyuma yթsomoGukurikiranya ibinyuranyo byաmanota uko birutana utitaye ku bimenyetsoUmwanya wթkinyuranyo cyաmanotaб01.5001.5вб4бб4вб40в7бв7вв7Igikurikiyeho rero ni uguha ikimenyetso (ҫӠcyangwa ҭө imyanya yթkinyuranyo cyաmanota urebeye ku kimenyetso kiri ku kinyuranyo cyաmanota ya mbere na nyuma yթsomo. Ikinyuranyo cyաmanota ya mbere na nyuma yթsomoGukurikiranya ibinyuranyo byաmanota uko birutana utitaye ku bimenyetsoUmwanya wթkinyuranyo cyաmanotaIkinyuranyo cyաmanota gifite ikimenyetso bijyanyeб01.51.5001.5б.5вб4дбб4двб4д0в7збв7звв7зKuri uru rugero twakoresheje, mu gushaka isano ryյmwanya rishingiye ku bimenyetso rya Wilcoxon, turifashisha igipimo cyo hagati mu binyuranyo byաmanota ya mbere na nyuma yթsomo.  H0: Inkeneragihamya ntacyahindutse: Igipimo cyo hagati mu binyuranyo byաmanota ya mbere na nyuma yթsomo ni 0 ugereranyije na H1: Inkeneragihamya yյbushakashatsi: Igipimo cyo hagati mu binyuranyo byաmanota ya mbere na nyuma yթsomo gifite ikimenyetso ҫӬ  = .05.Isuzuma ryթbarurishamibare ryթsano ryյmwanya rishingiye ku bimenyetso rya Wilcoxon ryubakiye kuri җӠigaragazwa nթngano nto kurusha indi hagati ya җ+Ӡ(igiteranyo kթmyanya yթbipimo cyangwa yաmanota bifite ikimenyetso cya ҫө na җ-Ӡ(igiteranyo kթmyanya yթbipimo cyangwa yաmanota bifite ikimenyetso cya ҭө. Niba җ+Ӡingana na җ-Ӡni ukuvuga ko inkeneragihamya Ho ari ukuri. Byaba bivuze ko ntacyahindutse. Nko mu rugero twakoresheje hejuru W+ = +1.5 naho W- = +34.5 (Ntabwo twita ku bimenyetso). Buri gihe igiteranyo kթmyanya kingana na n(n+1)/2 (tutitaye ku bimenyetso). Mu rugero twakoresheje ni ukuvuga ko igiteranyo kթmyanya turakibona dutya: 8(9)/2= 36. Iki giteranyo rero kigomba kuba kingana na 1.5 + 34.5 = 36. Ubwo rero isuzuma ryթbarurishamibare ni W = 1.5. Twibukiranye ko җӠigaragazwa nթngano nto cyangwa se umubare muto kurusha indi hagati ya җ+Ӡna җ-ӮIgisigaye rero ni ugushaka gihamya igaragaza niba W ishigikira ҩnkeneragihamya ntacyahindutseӠ(Ho) cyangwa ҩnkeneragihamya yյbushakashatsiӠ(H1) tugereranyije na W ngenderweho. Umubare wաbagize itsinda ngenderwaho na wo turawureberaho (n = 8). Turakoresha isuzuma ryյmujyo umwe (One-tailed test) ku rwego rwյbwemerwe rwa  = .05. Mu rugero twakoresheje, W ngenderwaho ni 5 ari byo bivuze ko ҩnkeneragihamya ntacyahindutse (Ho) turayirekaӠniba W  5. Ni ukuvuga ko Ho turayireka kuko 1.5  5. Ibi bisobanuye ko abanyeshuri bateye imbere mu myumvire ku buryo bugaragara ku kigero cya  = .05 mu isuzuma ryasubiwemo.UmwanzuroHari uburyo bwinshi bwo gusesengura amakuru nyamubaro. Muri uyu mutwe twatoranyije bumwe muri bwo kandi twerekana uko umushakashatsi ashobora kubukoresha atifashishije ikoranabuhanga rihanitse. Mu macapwa yթki gitabo azakurikiraho, dushobora kuzagenda twongeramo ubundi buryo bwisumbuyeho bwo gusesengura amakuru nyamubaro hakoreshejwe ikoranabuhanga. Mu bihe bizaza kandi tuzarushaho guha umwanya uburyo bwo gutara, gukosora no gushyira ku murongo amakuru nyamubaro kugira ngo umushakashatsi ashobore kuyasesengura. Ni ngombwa ko umushakashatsi ashobora gusoma amakuru nyamubaro, kureba atuzuye, kureba aho agiye abusana, no kuyatandukanya nաyթmpfabusa. Umushakashatsi kandi arasabwa gutunganya amakuru, kuyandika no kuyagaragaza ku buryo busobanutse kandi bwumvikana. Ibyo byose bituma umushakashatsi ashobora kuyasesengura, kuyabarura, kuyasobanura mu magambo, kuyagereranya nաndi yavuye ahandi no kuyashyira mu byiciro. Ni ngombwa kandi ko umushakashatsi ashobora kwerekana amakuru nyamubaro ku buryo bworohereza uyasoma guhita ayabona kandi ayumva. Ashobora gukoresha imbonerahamwe, ibishushanyo nթbindi. Mu magambo make, mu buryo twibanzeho bushobora gukoreshwa mu gusesengura amakuru nyamubaro, umushakashatsi akwiye kuzirikana izi ngingo zթngenzi:Isuzuma rya ?2 Muri iki gitabo twakoresheje isuzuma rya ?2 mu isesengura ryթmfatashusho ebyiri mu matsinda nkeshwamakuru abiri cyangwa menshi yigenga. Inkeneragihamya ntacyahindutse: Ho: ivuga ko ntacyahindutse ku mfatashusho runaka hagati yաmatsinda nkeshwamakuru. Isuzuma ryթbarurishamibare: Ubushakashatsi bwagaragaje ko kugira ngo umushakashatsi amenye ko hari itandukaniro hagati yթmfatashusho ebyiri, akoresha ?2 ahereye ku bwisubire bwabaruwe (observed frequencies) nյbwisubire butegerejwe (expected frequencies). Hakoreshwa iyi nzira ihinnye: (OЅE )2  Itegeko rigenga umwanzuro riterwa nթngano yթgipimo cyյbwigenge (degree of freedom) babara kuri ubu buryo: df = (k Р1)(r Р1); k = Inkingi (column) na r = Urubariro (row). Umwanzuro ni uko tureka kwemeza Ho igihe ?20  twabonye iruta ?2 ngenderwaho yo mu mbonerahamwe ku gipimo cyյbwigenge cyashatswe.Gukoresha isano rs rya Spearman nթsayo r rya PearsonUbu buryo bukoreshwa mu gushaka isano yթbarurishamibare iri hagati yթmfatashusho ebyiri. Isano rs rya Spearman rishingiye ku bipimo bidasumbanya agaciro. Isano r rya Pearson rikoreshwa iyo imfatashusho ebyiri zitandukanye zifite agaciro mubare kթbipimo byթntera (interval scale) cyangwa byթbigereranyo (ratio scale, i.e. continuous). Naho isano rs rya Spearman rikoreshwa gusa iyo izi ngingo zuzuye: Ibipimo byաmakuru bigomba kuba bifata amakuru yյrukurikirane (ordinal scale) cyangwa ibipimo byթntera (interval) cyangwa se byթbigereranyo (ratio). Amakuru yatanzwe akusanywa inshuro ebyiri zitandukanye ku itsinda nkeshwamakuru rimwe. Ayatawe bwa mbere agereranywa nաyakusanyijwe ku nshuro ya kabiri. Isano igomba kuba igenda umujyo umwe (Ni ukuvuga ko imfatashusho zombi uko ari ebyiri zishobora kwiyongera icyarimwe, cyangwa se imwe ikagenda yiyongera mu gihe indi igenda igabanuka).Isuzuma rya U rya Mann-Whitney  Iri suzuma rikoreshwa mu isesengura ryթmpinduka iri hagati yաmatsinda nkeshwamakuru yigenga. Inkeneragihamya ntacyahindutse: Ho: Amatsinda yigwaho arangana. Isuzuma ryթbarurishamibare: iryo suzuma rya Mann-Whitney ni U ntoya muri izi zombi:U1 = n1n2 + n1(n21 + 1) РR1 na U2 = n1n2 + n2(n22 + 1) РR2 Aho R1 ari igiteranyo kթmyanya yթbyiciro byաmanota yթtsinda rya 1 na R2 ikaba igiteranyo kթmyanya yթbyiciro byաmanota yթtsinda rya 2. Itegeko rigenga umwanzuro: Kureka Ho niba U twabonye  U ngenderwaho yo mu mbonerahamwe.Isuzuma ryյmwanya ushingiye ku bimenyetso rya Wilcoxon Iri suzuma rikoreshwa mu isesengura ryթmpinduka iri imbere mu itsinda (Amatsinda nkeshwamakuru ngengwa) Inkeneragihamya ntacyahindutse: H0: Igipimo cyo hagati (median) mu binyuranyo byաmanota ya mbere na nyuma yթsomo kingana na 0. Isuzuma ryթbarurishamibare: isuzuma ryթbarurishamibare ryթsano ryյmwanya ushingiye ku bimenyetso rya Wilcoxon rishingiye kuri җӠigaragazwa nթngano nto kurusha indi hagati ya җ+Ӡ(igiteranyo kթmyanya yթbipimo cyangwa yաmanota bifite ikimenyetso cya ҫө na җ-Ҡ(igiteranyo kթmyanya yթbipimo cyangwa yաmanota bifite ikimenyetso cya ҭө. Itegeko rigenga umwanzuro: Kureka Ho niba W twabaze  W ngenderwaho yo mu mbonerahamwe.IndangasokoField, A.
