Statistics for health policy and administration using Microsoft Excel. San Francisco: Jossey-Bass.UMUTWE 9 UKO BANDIKA IBYAGARAGAJWE NՕBUSHAKASHATSI, ISOBANURA BWITE NՉMYANZUROEvode Mukama, Joseph Rusanganwa, Marie Chantal Uwimana na Oliva BazireteIriburiroIyo umushakashatsi amaze gutara amakuru ni ngombwa ko yandika mu buryo busobanutse kandi bwumvikana ibyagaragajwe nյbwo bushakashatsi (findings/ results) ndetse akabisesengura. Umushakashatsi agerageza gusubiza ibi bibazo: ҍbese ko nakoze ubushakashatsi, nasanze bimeze bite?Ӡcyangwa se Ҏavumbuye iki?ӠKwibaza bene ibi bibazo mu kwandika ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi bifasha umushakashatsi gusubiza bya bibazo byյbushakashatsi yibazaga kuva mu ntangiro. Kuri buri kibazo cyյbushakashatsi agerageza kugaragaza ibimenyetso bifatika kandi bihagije cyangwa amakuru nyayo agaragaza uko gihagaze. Ibyo bimenyetso nաyo makuru aba yabivanye mu batangamakuru cyangwa mu nyandiko yifashishije. Ese umushakashatsi yandika ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi ate? Uyu mutwe uragerageza gusubiza iki kibazo.Uretse kwandika ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi, umushakashatsi akora isobanura bwite (discussion). Nkյko twabigarutseho mu mitwe ibanza, akamaro kյbushakashatsi ni ivumburabumenyi. Hari ibintu bitatu byթngenzi umushakashatsi agomba kugaragaza byerekana ko hari akarusho ubushakashatsi bwe bwongereye mu bumenyi busanzwe buzwi, cyangwa se mu migendekere yթbintu runaka: umushakashatsi agomba kugaragaza mu magambo make icyo ubushakashatsi bwagaragaje; icya kabiri, agaragaza uruhare rwյbushakashatsi bwe mu kongera, gusobanura kurushaho cyangwa se mu kuvuguruza ingingo runaka mu bumenyi busanzwe buzwi; icya gatatu, agaragaza uruhare rwյbushakashatsi bwe mu gusubiza ibibazo sosiyete yibaza, ari ibijyanye no gukora politiki zivuguruye, ari ugukora imirimo mu buryo runaka nթbindi. Muri uyu mutwe, turasesengura uko isobanura bwite rikorwa. Hari ubwo usanga isobanura bwite rifatanye nյmwanzuro wյbushakashatsi. Ariko hari nյbwo umwanzuro wa raporo yյbushakashatsi uba wanditse ukwawo. Muri uyu mutwe kandi, turagaragaza uko ushobora kwandika umwanzuro muri raporo yյbushakashatsi.Uko bandika ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi Gukoresha umwandiko (text)Akenshi na kenshi umushakashatsi atara amakuru menshi ariko si ko agomba kuyandukura yose uko yakabaye muri raporo yյbushakashatsi. Hari ubwo abatangamakuru basubiramo kenshi ibintu bimwe. Amakuru asa kandi avuga ku nsanganyamatsiko imwe agomba kwegeranywa, agasesengurirwa hamwe kabone nյbwo aba yavuzwe mu bihe bitandukanye. Tugiye kwifashisha ingero zifatika kugira ngo birusheho kumvikana neza. Mu gihe iki gitabo cyandikwaga, Mukama (2018b) yakoraga ubushakashatsi ku buryo urubyiruko nաbapfakazi bashobora kwihangira imirimo bafatanyije kandi babifashijwemo nյbumenyi mu ikoranabuhanga nթtumanaho. Mu ikusanyamakuru, yakoresheje ikiganiro mu itsinda ryաbayobozi batanu bյmushinga witwa ҩRebero Smart CommunityӮ Dore agace gato kթbyagaragajwe nյbwo bushakashatsi:Kwiga uhereye ku bibazo uhura na byoMu ntangiro zյmushinga iRebero Smart Community hagaragayemo ingorane zitandukanye ariko izo ngorane zabaye imbarutso zաmasomo arambye. Ingorane ya mbere: abagize ubuyobozi bwյmushinga bemeza ko abagenerwabikorwa hafi ya bose bari bizeye ko bazahita babona akazi bakimara kwiyandikisha. Emwe ndetse bamwe muri bo bari bazi ko kwiyandikisha mu bagenerwabikorwa bյmushinga bivuga kubona akazi. Monika asobanura icyo kibazo muri aya magambo: ҍu guhitamo abagenerwabikorwa, twabonye abakandida benshi batujuje ibisabwa [ɝ. Twabonye abubatse ingo bazaga bagatinyuka kubeshya, bagira bati Դuri abapfakazi, nimutwandikeծӠAbajijwe impamvu abo bantu baje kubeshya kandi byari bizwi neza ko umushinga ugenewe urubyiruko nաbapfakazi, yarasubije ati ҂atekerezaga ko harimo amafaranga. Bari bazi ko hari uburyo umugenerwabikorwa azayabonaho byanze bikunzeӮ Itsinda ryաbayobozi bյmushinga ryasobanuye ko byabaye ngombwa ko abarigize bakora iperereza ku baje kwiyandikisha kugira ngo bamenye niba abiyandikishije bari babikwiye koko. Iyi ngorane ubuyobozi bwahuye na yo mu kwandika abagenerwabikorwa ishobora kugaragaza ko ikibazo cyյbushomeri atari ikibazo kihariwe nյrubyiruko nաbapfakazi gusa, ahubwo ko ari ikibazo rusange cyաbaturage bo mu karere ka Gicumbi.Umuntu yitegereje neza uko ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi nyamimerere byanditse muri iki gika, ashobora kubonamo ingingo eshatu zikwiye kwitabwaho mu myandikire: iki gika gitangira kivuga mu magambo make ibikubiye mu bigiye kuvugwa: ҍu ntangiro zյmushinga iRebero Smart Community hagaragayemo ingorane zitandukanye ariko izo ngorane zabaye imbarutso zաmasomo arambye.ӠNi ngombwa ko umusomyi amenyeshwa ibyo agiye gusoma nթcyo biramugezaho. Umwanditsi aragaragaza ko hari ingorane zabaye mu ntangiro zյmushinga ariko akanavuga ko izo ngorane zatanze amahirwe yաmasomo agenderwaho. Si byiza guhita utangiza igika cyangwa amagambo yavuzwe nաbatangamakuru utabanje gusobanura impamvu yayo. Cyakora hari aho umwanditsi ashobora kubikora iyo umwandiko wաmagambo yյmutangamakuru yihagije mu gusobanura igika kigiye gukurikira. Nko mu nyandiko ye yasohotse mu gitangazamakuru cyյbushakashatsi kitwa Ҋournal of Religious and Theological InformationӬ hari aho Mukama (2018c) atangiza igika muri ubwo buryo igihe yari agiye gusobanura aho Kiriziya Gatolika ihagaze ku birebana no gukoresha ikoranabuhanga nթtumanaho. Ibyo biragaragara ku nsanganyamatsiko yise ҍwigira ubwoba bwթkoranabuhanga rigezwehoӠ(Pope Saint John Paul II, 2005).Umwandikitsi Mukama aterura ikibazo cya mbere yerekana aho avanye amakuru nթbiyakubiyemo. Aragira ati ҡbagize ubuyobozi bwյmushinga bemeza ko abagenerwabikorwa hafi ya bose bari bizeye ko bazahita babona akazi bakimara kwiyandikisha.ӠAravuga amakuru yahawe mu buryo bwe ni ukuvuga mu buryo buziguye. Ibi bifasha umushakashatsi kuvuga mu buryo buvunaguye kandi icyarimwe amagambo yavuzwe nաbatangamakuru benshi. Byongeye, ibi bituma ashobora kuvuga mu buryo buboneye igitekerezo cyաbatangamakuru ariko akirinda rwose kubahimbira ibyo batavuze. Mu kugaragaza ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi nyamimerere, ni ngombwa no gukoresha amagambo uko yavuzwe nաbatangamakuru. Urugero tuvanye muri icyo gika cyo hejuru: ҂atekerezaga ko harimo amafaranga. Bari bazi ko hari uburyo umugenerwabikorwa azayabonaho byanze bikunze.Ӈusubiramo uko abatangamakuru babyivugiye ni ingenzi rwose kuko byongera ububonere nյbwizerwe bwաmakuru kandi bikaba nյbuhamya bwթbyavuzwe koko. Iki gika kirangizwa nթmyanzuro ibiri yթngenzi. Uwa mbere uragaragaza ko itsinda ryաbayobozi bյmushinga bakora iperereza ku baje kwiyandikisha kugira ngo bandike umugenerwabikorwa wujuje ibyangombwa bisabwa koko: kuba uri mu rubyiruko cyangwa se mu bapfakazi. Umwanzuro wa kabiri uratangwa nյmushakashatsi. Ahereye ku kibazo cyavutse gitewe nյko nաbashakanye bakiri kumwe baza kwiyandikisha bakabeshya ko bapfakaye kandi atari byo, byagaragariye umushakashatsi ko na bo bakeneye akazi kabazanira amafranga. Bityo umushakashatsi yanzura, agira ati ҉yi ngorane ubuyobozi bwahuye na yo mu kwandika abagenerwabikorwa ishobora kugaragaza ko ikibazo cyյbushomeri atari ikibazo kihariwe nյrubyiruko nաbapfakazi gusa, ahubwo ko ari ikibazo rusange cyաbaturage bo mu karere ka Gicumbi.Ӊbi ni byo benshi bakunze kwita kumenya ҧusoma hagati yթmirongoӮ Ni nko kubona ikimenyetso ku muhanda ukaba wakwibaza uti ҭbese iki kimenyetso kiramenyesha iki?ӠUmushakashatsi rero agomba kumenye gusoma ibimenyetso no gufutura aho byerekeza. Agerageza gushaka igisobanuro kihishe mu makuru yakusanyije. Biba byiza iyo umushakashatsi agiye mu makoraniro mpuzabashakashatsi agatangaza ubushakashatsi bwe, maze bagenzi be bakabujora, kabamuha ibitekerezo bityo akarushaho kubunoza. Ibitangazamakuru byյbushakashatsi bishyira ahagaragara ubushakashatsi ari uko byabanje kubujora. Ugira umusomera kandi akamukosorera raporo yյbushakashatsi aba afite amahirwe menshi yo kwikosora no kurushaho kunoza ubushakashatsi bwe.Gukoresha ibipimo byթbarurishamibareUmwandiko ushobora no kwifashishwa ugaragaza ibyavuye mu bushakashatsi bukoresheje ibarurishamibare. Reka twifashije imibare yavuye mu bushakashatsi bwakozwe nՉkigo kՉgihugu kՉbarurishamibare mu Rwanda (National Institute of Statistics of Rwanda, 2018).Imibare igaragazwa nՉkigo kՉgihugu kՉbarurishamibare (National Institute of Statistics of Rwanda, 2018) yerekana ko ijanisha ryաbashomeri mu Rwanda ryakomeje kuzamuka ku buryo ryageze ku gipimo cya 20.3% mu 2017. Muri uyu mwaka nyine, ubushomeri bwagaragaye cyane mu bagore (24.4%) kurusha mu bagabo (17.1%). Ikigo kՉgihugu kՉbarurishamibare cyasanze ubushomeri bwiganje mu migi ku gipimo cya 20.4% kurusha mu cyaro aho buhagaze kuri 19.8%. Iki kigo kigaragaza kandi ko ubushomeri mu rubyiruko rufite hagati yթmyaka 16 kugera kuri 30 bwari buhagaze ku gipimo cya 23.6% (abahungu ni 20% naho abakobwa bakaba 27.4%). Bigaragara ko iki gipimo kikubye hafi inshuro ebyiri zose ikigereranyo cyյbushomeri mu rubyiruko ku isi (13.1%) nթcyo mu bihugu biri munsi yյbutayu bwa Sahara (11.1%) nkյko bitangazwa nՉkigo Mpuzamahanga cyՕmurimo (International Labour Organisation, 2017).Nkյko bigaragara muri iki gika, Mukama (2018b) arifashisha igereranya ryթbipimo byavuye mu bundi bushakashatsi kugira ngo arusheho kwerekana ubukana bwթkibazo cyյbushobomeri mu Rwanda. Arakoresha umwandiko mu guha igisobanuro ibyo bipimo. Uyu mushakashatsi yigaga ku kibazo cyյbushomeri mu rubyiruko rwo mu Rwanda. Kugira ngo agisobanure neza, atangira avuga uko ubushomeri bwifashe muri rusange mu Rwanda, akabona kurasa ku ntego. Ni ukuvuga ko ava ku bisobanuro byթkibazo rusange agana ku kibazo kihariye: ubushomeri mu rubyiruko. Ikindi cyongera kumvikanisha uburemere bwթkibazo muri icyo gika ni igereranya ryթgipimo byյbushomeri mu Rwanda nթbipimo byabwo ku rwego mpuzamahanga. Umusomyi ashobora kumva ko iki kibazo kitakiri ikibazo gisanzwe ahubwo ko ari nkթmpuruza isaba ko hari igikwiye gukorwa mu maguru mashya kugira ngo gikemuke.Gukoresha imbonerahamwe (table)Nkյko ijambo ribisobanura, imbonerahamwe ifasha umushakashatsi kwerekana ku buryo bwegeranye amakuru ashobora kuba anyanyagiye hirya no hino. Ibyo bishobora kumufasha kwerekana ayo makaru yose mu magambo make, cyangwa se mu mibare, kwerekana isano iri gahagi yayo, kuyasesengura no gufasha umusomyi kuyabonera hamwe mu gihe gito. Imbonerahamwe ubwayo igomba kwivugira noneho, nkյko twabikomojeho haruguru, umushakashatsi agasesengura icyo ayo makuru amenyesha atagombye kuyasubiramo yose mu mwandiko. Dore urugero twavanye mu gitangazamakuru Panorama (2018, Kanama 9) ku mbonerahamwe igaragaza uko uturere two mu Rwanda twesheje imihigo ya 2017 Р2018. Imbonerahamwe 1: Uko uturere two mu Rwanda twesheje imihigo ya 2017 Р2018UmwanyaAkarareAmanota ku ijana1Rwamagana84.52Gasabo82.53Rulindo82.54Gakenke80.35Kicukiro77.56Gicumbi76.37Kayonza74.98Gatsibo73.59Rubavu72.810Rutsiro72.4UmwanyaAkarareAmanota ku ijana11Bugesera72.112Ngororero71.913Kirehe71.514Nyagatare70.915Musanze70.216Muhanga68.417Nyamasheke67.118Nyabihu66.819Huye6620Nyarugenge65.121Karongi64.822Ngoma64.723Rusizi64.524Nyaruguru64.125Gisagara63.126Kamonyi59.327Burera57.228Nyamagabe54.129Ruhango53.430Nyanza53Aho byavuye: Panorama (2018, Kanama 9)Igitangazamakuru Panorama (2018, Kanama 9) gikora isesengura muri aya magambo magufi:Akarere ka Rwamagana kongeye kuza ku isonga nաmanota 84.5 mu gihe akarere ka Muhanga kabimburira utundi mu Ntara yՁmajyepfo ari aka 16 ku rutonde, utundi turere 6 twթyi Ntara turi mu myanya 10 ya nyuma harimo na Nyanza yaherukiye utundi.  Iri sesengura ryakozwe na Panorama rirahagije. Riravuga ibyթngenzi umusomyi akeneye kumenya : akarere kabaye aka mbere, akabaye aka nyuma nյmwihariko wagaragaye mu Ntara yՁmajyepfo. Umusomyi ubwe arabona ko iyi ntara ishobora kuba yaragize ingorane mu kwesa imihigo ya 2017 Р2018 ugereranyije amanota yյturere tuyigize nաyյturere twթzindi ntara. Umushakashatsi na we rero asabwa kuvuga amakuru yթngenzi gusa agaragara mu mbonerahamwe, akagaragaza ibifite agaciro kurusha ibindi cyangwa se ibigomba kwitabwaho. Imbonerahamwe igomba kuba yoroshye kuyisoma, amakuru asobanuye neza ku buryo umusomyi ashobora kwifuturira andi makuru rusange ayirimo. Birashoboka ko imbonerahamwe iba igizwe nաmagambo gusa nta mibare irimo. Hano tugiye kwifashisha urugero twakuye mu bushakashatsi bwakozwe na Gahamanyi (2010) mu kwerekana ukuntu abatwara tagisi, abubatsi nաbafite inzu zicuruza ibiryo bakora ubucuruzi bwabo kugira ngo bunguke. Gahamanyi yifashisha imbata ngenderwaho (model) yյmushakashatsi Leontեv (1981). Imbonerahamwe 2 : G usesengura ibigize umurimo mu kazi ka buri munsi hakoreshejwe imbata ngenderwaho ya Leontեv (1981)Abashoferi ba tagisiAbubatsiAbafite inzu zicururizwamo ibiryoUmurimoGukora akazi kabyara inyunguIcyamuhagurukijeKubona inyungu ituma umuntu atera imbere mu mibereho yeIgikorwaGuciririkanya igiciro nյmukiriya, kugura lisansi Kugereranya no gushyiraho igiciro gishobora guhangana ku isoko ryյmurimo, kuyobora imirimo yյbwubatsi Kugereranya ibiciro byթbiribwa bihiye ugereranyije nթbibisi biri ku isoko, kugurisha ibiribwa bihiyeIntegoInyungu ishimishijeInyungu ishimishijeInyungu ishimishijeUko bikorwaKugereranya intera, kugereranya igihe, kureba uko igiciro cya lisansi kifasheGukora gahunda, gusura abagenerwabikorwa barebwa nթgikorwaGukora gahunda, kuganira nաbakiriya, gusura amasoko atandukanyeIbisabwaUko umuhanda umeze, uko ikirere kimeze, umubare wաbakiriya, ikiciro cyաbakiriya nթgiheIgihe kubaka bifata, umubare wաbandi bubatsi bashobora gukora akazi nkաkawe, uko ibiciro byյbwubatsi bihagaze, uko umushahara wաbakozi uhagazeUmubare wաbakiriya, ibiciro byo mu zindi nzu zicuruza ibiryo hafi aho, iminsi yաkazi nթminsi ya wikendiAho byavuye: Gahamanyi (2010, p. 67)Iyi mbonerahamwe irerekana uburyo abashoferi ba tagisi, abubatsi bաmazu nաbafite inzu zicururizwamo ibiryo bakoresha imibare ku buryo buziguye mbese nkաbatabitekerezagaho. Ni nko gukoresha ubunararibonye kugira ngo bagere ku ntego yo kubyaza umusaruro akazi bakora. Iyi mbonerahamwe iradufasha kugereranya ibikorwa byաbanyamwuga bari mu byiciro bitatu bitandukanye ugereranyije nյmurimo bakora, icyatumye bawukora, ibyo bakora nyirizina, intego, uko bikorwa nթbisabwa. Gukoresha igishushanyo-mbonerahamwe (figure)Kugaragaza ibyavuye mu bushakashatsi ntibikorwa hakoreshejwe umwandiko nթmbonerahamwe gusa, umushakashatsi ashobora no gukoresha igishushanyombonerahamwe. Icyo gishushanyo-mbonerahamwe kigomba kubanzirizwa nյmwandiko usobanura icyo bigiye kugaragaza, hanyuma kandi bigaherekezwa nյmwandiko wթnshamake yթsesengura ryաmakuru agikubiyemo.Reka dufate urugero ku bushakashatsi bwakozwe nՕwimana na Kerr (2017) ku guhangayika gukabije abaforomo nաbaforomokazi bagira muri bimwe mu bitaro byo mu Rwanda. Abo bashakashatsi basanze uko guhangayika kugira ingaruka mu kazi kabo. Izo ngaruka bazigaraje mu gishushanyo-mbonerahamwe gikurikira: 	0%	10%	20%	30%	40%	50%	60%	70%Igishushanonyo mbonerahamwe 1: I ngaruka ziterwa no guhangayika gukabije kwաbaforomo nաbaforomokazi mu kaziAho byavuye: Uwimana na Kerr (2017, pp. 47)Umutwe wթgishushanyo-mbonerahamwe (figure) wandikwa munsi yacyo. Mu kugisesengura rero si ngombwa gusubiramo amakuru yose kigaragaza kubera ko umusomyi ashobora kuyisomera. Ahubwo umushakashatsi agomba gusesengura ayo makuru kugira ngo agaragaze isomo umusomyi yakuramo. Nko muri icyo Gishushanyo mbonerahamwe 1 (Figure 1), biragaragara ko ingaruka nini iterwa no guhangayika gukabije kwաbaforomo nաbaforomokazi ari ukudakora akazi kabo mu buryo bwa kinyamwuga (61%). Ikiciro cya kabiri cyթngaruka zo guhangayika mu kazi kwաbaforomo nաbaforomokazi babigize umwuga ni ukugira ikifuzo cyo kureka akazi, kugira umunaniro ukabije no kubihirwa nաkazi bakora. Ikindi iki gishushanyo-mbonerahamwe kigaragaza ni uko abaforomo nաbaforomokazi bumva bahitamo kureka akazi (8%) cyangwa bakagasiba (7%) kubera ibibazo bahura na byo mu kazi ari bo bake. Ibi rero bishaka kuvuga iki? Isesengura Uwimana na Kerr (2017) bakora aha ni irihe? Ibi bishobora kusobanura ko aho kureka akazi cyangwa se kugasiba kubera guhangayika gukabije, abaforomo nաbaforomokazi babigize umwuga benshi ari abahitamo kukagumamo kabone nթyo bagakora nabi (bitari kinyamwuga). Gushobora gukora isesengura nkթri ni cyo umushakashatsi agombwa kugerageza kugeraho. Bimusaba rero gutekereza, kwibaza no kwisubiza. Ni byo twise kumenya ҧusoma hagati yթmirongoӮ Agomba guha igisobanuro amakuru yatangaje muri raporo yյbushakashatsi bwe. Ingingo zo kwitabwahoHari ingingo zikwiye kwitabwaho mu kwandika ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi. Zimwe muri zo ni izi zikurikira: Ni ngomba kurasa ku ntego kandi ku buryo bwumvikana. Umushakashatsi ashobora gukusanya amakuru menshi. Kuyarundarundanya muri raporo yյbushakashatsi si cyo kigamijwe. Ikigamijwe ni ugutoranya ayթngenzi kandi agararagaza ibimenyetso bihagije ku nsanganyamatsiko runaka. Kuyavuga mu buryo bworoheje ku buryo umusomyi ashobora kuyumva byongerera agaciro ubushakashatsi. Amakuru yյbushakashatsi agomba kuba asubiza ibibazo byյbushakashatsi. Umushakashatsi agomba rwose kwirinda guhimba amakuru, cyangwa kuyaha ibisobanuro bidafitiwe ibimenyetso. Igice cyo kwerekana uko ubushakashatsi bwagenze kijya mu iyoboramikorere (methodology), ntabwo kivangwa nթbyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi. Byongeye, isesengura bwite (discussion) na ryo rigira igice kihariye rigomba gukorerwamo. Si byiza kurivanga nթbyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi, kereka mu bushakashatsi bumwe na bumwe, cyanecyane nko mu iyigabumenyamuntu (anthropology) cyangwa mu bushakashatsi mbandamoko (ethnography). Ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi byandikwa mu mpitagihe (past tense). Umushakashatsi akoresha umwandiko, imbonerahamwe cyangwa igishushushanyo-mbonerahamwe akurikije uburyo abona bugaragaza neza amakuru ashaka kwerekana. Si ngombwa gusubiramo amakuru amwe ukoresheje uburyo bwinshi icyarimwe.  Nkյko bigaragara mu ngero twatanze, izina ryթmbonerahamwe ryandikwa hejuru yթmbonerahamwe naho izina ryթgishushanyo-mbonerahamwe rikandikwa munsi yacyo.Uko bakora isobanura bwite Akamaro kթbanze kյbushakashatsi, nkյko twabigarutseho kenshi, ni ivumburabumenyi. Kugira ngo umushakashatsi aterure gukora ubushakashatsi bwe ni uko hari ibibazo byյbushakashatsi aba ashaka gusubiza. Ibyo bibazo na none biba byaravuye mu isesengura ryթbyanditswe mbere. Iri sesengura ryյbushakashatsi bwanditswe mbere rifasha umushakashatsi kugira ubumenyi ku bushakashatsi buba bwarakozwe mbere no guha ikerekezo ubushakashatsi bwe akurikije impamvu zitandukanye zirimo izi zikurikira: 1) kuziba icyuho mu bumenyi busanzwe buzwi; 2) kongera ibisobanuro ku bumenyi abandi bagaragaje kugira ngo burusheho gusobanuka byisumbuye, 2) kugira ngo bwumvikane kurushaho, 4) kugira ngo bukosorwe cyangwa se 5) bwaguke. Isobanura bwite rero rigamije kugaragaza mu magambo make umusanzu ubushakashatsi bwakozwe buzanye hashingiwe ku bimenyetso bifatika byatanzwe mu byagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi. Umusanzu wյbushakashatsi uri ugutatu: 1) icyo ubushakashatsi bwagezeho gishingiye ku gutara no gusesengura amakuru (empirical contribution); 2) umusanzu wյbushakashatsi mu ihange ryյbumenyi (theoretical contribution); 3) umusanzu wյbushakashatsi mu bikorwa (practical contribution). Rusanganwa (2013) agaragaza neza umusanzu wյbushakashatsi muri ibyo byiciro uko ari bitatu mu buryo butaziguye. Reka turebe uko umusanzu wյbushakashatsi ugaragazwa mu isobanura bwite.Umusanzu wթcyo ubushakashatsi bwagezeho gishingiye ku gutara no gusesengura amakuru (empirical contribution)Ese ibisubizo ku bibazo byյbushakashatsi ni ibihe? Mu yandi magambo, umushakashatsi yabonye iki? Ubushakashatsi bwe buragaragaza iki mu magambo make kuri buri kibazo cyյbushakashatsi? Izingiro ryo kugaragaza uyu musanzu ni ukwibutsa umusomyi icyo ubushakashatsi bwabozwe bwari bugamije. Ni ukwibutsa bya bibazo byյbushakashatsi yibazaga agitangira ubushakashatsi. Nka Rusanganwa (2013, p. 42) aterura isobanura bwite yibutsa mu magambo make ibibazo byյbushakashatsi bwe. Aragira ati:Intego nyamukuru yթyi nyigo yari ugucukumbura icyo ikoreshwa ryաmajwi nաmashusho bishobora gufasha mu myigire no mu gufata mu mutwe amuga akoreshwa mu masomo yյbugenge hakoreshejwe mudasobwa ugereranyije no kubyiga hakoreshejwe uburyo bwa kera bwo gukoresha ingwa nթkibaho. Kugira ngo ibyo tubigereho, twasesenguye uko abanyeshuri bigaga mu mahugurwa bahawe, tugereranya amanota babonye mu kwiga muri ubwo buryo bwombi.Ubu bushakashatsi bwa Rusanganwa (2013) bwagaragaje ibintu bibiri byթngenzi: Mu kwiga hakoreshejwe gutega amatwi amuga yյbugenge, gusubiramo uko avugwa no kwerekana icyo amenyesha, usanga abanyeshuri bose barabishoboye kandi batera imbere; Mu isuzuma ryakozwe ku bushobozi bwo gufata mu mutwe amuga yյbugenge, ubushakashatsi bugaragaza ko abanyeshuri bo mu itsinda ryigaga ryifashishije urwunge rwաmajwi nաmashusho kuri mudasobwa babonye amanota menshi (ku gipimo cya Cohen d = 0.95) kurusha abize bakoresha ingwa nթkibaho.Reka twifashishe nյrundi rugero rwerekana umusanzu wթcyo ubushakashatsi bwagezeho gishingiye ku gukusanya no gusesengura amakuru kugira ngo birusheho kumvikana. Mu bushakashatsi bwe, Mukama (2009, pp. 546 Р547) atangira yibutsa icyo ubushakashatsi bwari bugamije hamwe nթbibazo byյbushakashatsi:Nkյko byavuzwe mbere, ubu bushakashatsi bwari bugamije gucukumbura uko abanyeshuri bitoza umwuga wյbwarimu bakoresha ikoranabuhanga mu buzima bwabo bwa buri munsi bwo kwiga ugereranyije nյbumenyi baba barigishijwe. Kugira ngo ibyo mbigereho, nibajije ibi bibazo byյbushakashatsi: Abanyeshuri bitoza umwuga wյbwarimu bakoresha bate ikoranabuhanga mu gukemura ibibazo byabo bya buri munsi? Ni iki gifasha cyangwa kibera imbogamizi abanyeshuri bitoza umwuga wյbwarimu mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga mu myigire yabo? Abanyeshuri bitoza umwuga wյbwarimu bafashanya bate mu gukemura ibibazo bijyanye nթkoranabuhanga mu myigire yabo ya buri munsi?Ibisubizo kuri ibyo bibazo, nabihiniye mu izi ngingo zikurikira: [...]30 Ibyagaragajwe nյbu bushakashatsi birerekana ko bamwe mu bitoza umwuga wյbwarimu usanga bashishikarira gukoresha ikoranabuhanga mu myigire yabo ya buri munsi kurusha bagenzi babo. Byongeye, ikoreshwa ryթkoranabuhanga rishobora kuba rifitanye isano nթngorane ikigo bigamo gifite (ingero, ubuke bwa za mudasobwa; kubura bya hato na hato kwa murandasi cyangwa umuriro wաmashyanyarazi; ubuke bwաbize gukoresha ikoranabuhanga; ubwinshi bwաmakuru ari kuri murandasi) cyangwa se ku mpamvu zituruka ku muntu ku giti ke (ingero, gutinya gukoresha ikoranabuhanga; kutagira amakuru ahagije ku bijyanye nթkoranabuhanga nաkamaro karyo; ubunebwe cyangwa kutagira umwete wo gukoresha ikoranabuhanga rigezweho). Abanyamurava mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga usanga badatinya gushakira umuti ingorane twavuze haruguru bakoresheje gufata ikemezo, ubwitange nյbushobozi bwabo mu gufasha cyangwa kwigisha bagenzi babo mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga mu buzima bwabo bwa buri munsi.Ubwo buryo bwo kuvuga mu magambo make ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi cyangwa se, mu yandi magambo, icyo ubushakashatsi bwagezeho ni ingenzi. Iyi nshamake yibanze cyanecyane ku myanzuro yanditse mu byagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi. Ni kuri iyo myanzuro rero umushakashatsi aheraho yerekana aho ubushakashatsi bwe buhagaze ugereranyije nյbwo abandi bamubanjirije. Ni byo tugiye gusobanura muri iyi ngingo ikurikiyeho.Umusanzu wյbushakashatsi mu ihange ryյbumenyi  (theoretical contribution)Kuba umushakashatsi yarakusanyije amakuru yarangiza akayasesengura ntibihagije. Agomba na none kugaragaza umusanzu we mu bumenyi busanzwe buzwi. Nkյko twabisobanuye mu mutwe urebana no gusesengura ibyanditswe mbere, ubushakashatsi bwakorwa bukazana ibisobanuro byisumbuye ibisanzwe, ibikosora imyumvire yari isanzwe cyangwa se ibizana imyumvire mishya itari isanzwe izwi, ibyo byose ni umusanzu mu kongera ubumenyi cyangwa imyumvire ku gitekerezo shingiro runaka cyյbushakashatsi. Niba hari amakuru mashya ubushakashatsi buzanye atuma urwego rwթkizere ku myumvire yari isanzwe izwi rwiyongera cyangwa se rugabanuka na byo ni uburyo bwo kongera ubumenyi.Duhereye ku ngero twifashishije haruguru, Rusanganwa (2013) atanga umusanzu mu kwerekana ko ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi bwe byuzuzanya nթbyաbandi bashakashatsi barimo Chun, Mayer, Plass na Leutner (1998). Igishya Mukama (2009) yagaragaje mu bushakashatsi bwe ni uko guhugura abanyeshuri cyangwa abarimu no kubaha ikoranabuhanga rikenewe bidahagije ngo babibyaze umusaruro mu myigire no mu kazi kabo ka buri munsi. Mukama yerekana ko abanyeshuri nաbarimu batitabira gukoresha ikoranabuhanga ku rwego rumwe. Hari igice cya mbere kigizwe nաbanebwe mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga (passive ICT users): aba bahabwa amahugurwa kimwe nաbandi ariko yarangira bagahora baganya ko bafite akazi kenshi, mbese ko nta mwanya babona wo gukoresha ikoranabuhanga. Iyo abanebwe mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga bahuye nթngorane iyo ari yo yose, bahita barekera aho bagategereza ko abandi baza kuyibakemurira. Igice cya kabiri kigizwe na ba ntamwete mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga (reluctant ICT users): aba bo bagaragazwa nյko hari ibyo bagerageza gukora bifashishije ikoranabuhanga kandi bakabikora neza. Nyamara usanga batigirira ikizere ahubwo bagahora basaba amahugurwa. Akenshi na kenshi usanga badaha ikoranabuhanga umwanya wթbanze mu byabafasha kwiga. Ikiciro cya gatatu ni ikigizwe nթtsinda ryաbanyamurava mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga (active ICT users): aba bo bazi kwishakira ibisubizo no kwikemurira ibibazo bahura na byo. Usanga ari bo bafasha bagenzi babo. Rimwe na rimwe bakoresha kwigomwa ibindi no gukora iyo bwabaga ngo bagere ku ntego yabo bakoresheje ikoranabuhanga. Mu isesengura bwite rye, Mukama (2009) yerekana ko ubushakashatsi bwe bufite akamaro mu gusobanura impamvu Bush na Middlewood (1997) bafite ukuri iyo bemeza ko ibigo byաmashuri bigera ku ntego yabyo atari ukubera ikoranabuhanga ryաgatangaza, ahubwo ari ubushobozi bwաbakozi bթbyo bigo mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga. Mukama (2009) kandi yuririra ku bushakashatsi bwa Rogoff (1994) wemeza ko abanyeshuri bashobora kwiga bafashanya maze na we agasobanura ukuntu abanyamurava mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga bashobora kuba abafashamyumvire nթmbarutso mu gufasha bagenzi babo mu kwiga bakoresheje ikoranabuhanga.Nkյko iki gika cyo hejuru kibigaragaza, umushakashatsi asobanura ibyթngenzi byagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi bwe abugereranya nյbwաbandi bamubanjirije. Ashobora kwerekana aho bahurira, aho batandukanira, aho buzuzanya cyangwa aho babusanya. Ashobora kandi kuvuga igishya abandi batigeze bavugaho. Umushakashatsi akora isesengura bwite yifashishije ishuri ryթbitekerezo runaka. Usanga nkթbisobanuro Mukama (2009) atanga byubakiye ku ishuri ryթbitekerezo bishingiye ku mibanire yաbantu nյmuco wabo (socioculture) byahimbwe na Vygotsky (1978).Umusanzu wյbushakashatsi mu bikorwa (practical contribution)Umusanzu wa gatatu umushakashatsi ashobora kugaragaza ni uruhare rwյbushakashatsi bwe mu gusubiza ibibazo sosiyete yibaza, ari ibijyanye no gukora politiki zivuguruye cyangwa ingamba zihariye, ari ugukora imirimo cyangwa ibikorwa runaka nթbindi. Aha kandi umushakashatsi ashobora kwerekana ubundi bushakashatsi bushobora gukorwa nաbandi bashakashatsi bahereye kubwe. Ni ukuvuga ko ubushakashatsi butuma havuka ibindi bibazo byյbushakashatsi ku buryo nyiri ukubukora cyangwa se undi mushakashatsi ashobora kuzabyigaho mu gihe kiri imbere. Akenshi ibi abikora agamije kwerekana ko ubushakashatsi yakoze bufite aho bugarukira. Izi mbago zյbushakashatsi (research limitations) bwe zishobora kugaragarira mu iyoboranziza, ku hantu ubushakashatsi bwabereye, ku nsanganyamatsiko yizweho mu bushakashatsi nաhandi. Urugero: niba Mukama (2009) abona ko abanyeshuri bաbanyamurava mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga bafite ubushobozi bwo gufasha bagenzi babo kwiga baryifashishije, ashobora gutanga igitekerezo avuga ko abandi bashakashatsi bakwiye gucukumbura uburyo abanyeshuri cyangwa abarimu bաbanyamurava bashobora kuba abafashamyumvire nթmbarutso mu gutsimbakaza ikoreshwa ryթkoranabuhanga mu mashuri. Byongeye, abarimu nաbashyiraho politiki zյburezi bashobora gushyiraho ingamba cyangwa politiki zatuma iki gitekerezo kijya mu bikorwa mu burezi. Dore urugero rwյko umushakashatsi ashobora kubyandika mu isesengura bwite:Icyo nshaka kuvuga ni uko ubufatanye hagati yաmatsinda yյrungano afite ubunararibonye butandukanye bishobora gutuma haba impinduka zubaka kandi zubakiye ku bufatanye mu gihe ikoranabuhanga rikoreshejwe mu guhanga ibishya no mu kwikemurira ibibazo. Urugero: ibyagaragajwe nյbu bushakashatsi bishobora kwifashishwa nաbarimu, abashakashatsi nաbashyiraho politiki mu gutsimbakaza ikoreshywa ryթkoranabuhanga mu kwiga cyangwa mu kwigisha abaturage gurikoresha (Mukama, 2009, pp. 547 Р549).Nko mu nyandiko ya Rusanganwa (2013), ayo moko atatu yյmusanzu wյbushakashatsi agaragarira amaso kuko imitwe mito igize isesengura bwite irivugira: umusanzu wթcyo ubushakashatsi bwagezeho gishingiye ku gutara no gusesengura amakuru; umusanzu wյbushakashatsi mu ihange ryյbumenyi, nյmusanzu wյbushakashatsi mu bikorwa bifatika. Rusanganwa yongeraho nյmutwe muto uvuga ku mbago zյbushakashatsi bwe nթkerekezo cyյbushakashatsi cyangwa ibikorwa bishoboka mu gihe kizaza. Nյbwo abashakashatsi benshi badakunda kwandika iyo mitwe mito muri raporo zյbushakashatsi bwabo, nyamara iyo uzisomye witonze usanga ibivugwa mu isobanura bwite iyo misanzu uko ari itatu nkյko twayivuze haruguru igaragaramo. Cyakora kwandika imitwe mito igaragaza imisanzu yյbushakashatsi mu isesengura bwite nkյko Rusanganwa (2013) abivuga, bishobora gufasha cyanecyane abashakashatsi bagitangira guha agaciro gakwiye buri musanzu. Byongeye, bishobora kubafasha gukora no kwandika isesengura bwite barasa ku ntego.Uko bakora umwanzuro (conclusion)Mu bushakashatsi, ijambo ҵmwanzuroӠntabwo rivuga gusa ҵmusozoӮ Umwanzuro hano rikwiye kumvikana mu gisubizo waha umuntu aramutse akubajije ati ҉bi bintu birashaka kuvuga iki?ӠҎiba kanaka avuga ati Ԯ..լ na runaka akavuga ati Ԯ..լ ubwo rero ge ndumva bashaka kuvuga bati Ԯ..Փ. Gusubiza bene ibi bibazo ni nko gukora amahurizo akurikira: Niba A = B kandi B = C, ni ukuvuga ko (umwanzuro) A = C  	Niba A = B kandi B  C, ni ukuvuga ko (umwanzuro) A  C Niba A  B kandi B = C, ni ukuvuga ko (umwanzuro) A  CIzi ngero zisobanuye ko iyo ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi bisa nթbyo ubundi bushakashatsi bwakozwe mbere bwagaragaje, umushakashatsi agomba kubivuga. Niba kandi hari aho ibyo ubushakashatsi bwe bibusana cyangwa bivuguruza ibyաbandi bashakashatsi bagaragaje, na byo agomba kubyerekana. Birashoboka kandi ko hari aho ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi bigira aho bihuza nթbyաbandi bakoze ubushakashatsi mbere nyamara bikabusanya nթbya bamwe na bamwe. Ibyo na byo ni ingezi kubigaragaza. Ubushakashatsi bushobora kuvumbura ikintu kitari gisanzwe kizwi, mbese nta wundi mushakashatsi wakigaragaje mbere. Yifashishije ibimenyetso bifatika, ibyo umushakashatsi agomba kubishyira ahagaragara kandi akerekana aho atandukanira nաbandi bashakashatsi bamubanjirije.Gukora umwanzuro rero si ukwandika mu magambo make gusa ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi, ahubwo ni ugusigura icyo ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi bishaka kuvuga. Umwanzuro si ikintu umushakashatsi ahimba ngo agikubite aho. Uhubwo umushakashatsi agomba gushingira umwanzuro we ku bimenyetso bifatika bivuye mu byagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi.Mu bushakashatsi habamo imyanzuro myinshi ni na yo mpamvu usanga abashakashatsi benshi bandika ҩmyanzuroӠ(conclusions) mu bwinshi aho kwandika umwanzuro umwe. Kuri buri kibazo cyյbushakashatsi, umushakashatsi agifataho umwanzuro cyangwa imyanzuro myinshi akurikije amakuru yabonye nթsesengura yakoze. Ziriya nshamake rero umushakashatsi yandika ku musanzu wթcyo ubushakashatsi bwagezeho gishingiye ku gutara no gusesengura amakuru ni iyo myanzuro ikomoka ku bibazo byյbushakashatsi aba yavuze mu magambo make. Kubera ko imyanzuro ari yo ifasha umushakashatsi gukora isobanura bwite, ushobora gusanga umushakashatsi yashoje raporo yյbushakashatsi bwe cyanecyane mu bitangazamakuru byյbushakashatsi yanditse gusa ҕmwanzuro/ ImyanzuroӠ(urugero: (Bahati, Tedre, Fors, & Mukama, 2016) cyangwa akandika gusa ҉sobanura bwiteӠ(urugero: Ruterana, 2012a) cyangwa se na none akabifatanya byombi: ҉sobanura bwite nՕmwanzuro/ImyanzuroӠ(urugero: Rusanganwa, 2013). Rimwe na rimwe hari nյbwo usanga abashakashatsi babanje kwandika imyanzuro ukwayo bagakurikizaho isesengura bwite (urugero: Mukama, 2010); abandi na bo bakabanza isensengura bwite bagakurikizaho umwanzuro (ingero: Ruterana, 2011; Mutwarasibo, 2013; Mukama, 2018a). Uburyo bworoshye bwo kwiga kwandika isobanura bwite ni ukubanza gusoma izindi nyandiko cyangwa raporo zյbushakashatsi bifitanye isano nյbushakashatsi bwawe kabone nթyo mwaba mutaranditse ku nsanganyamatsiko zimwe. Ibyo rero bigufasha kureba uko abandi bashakashatsi bթnararibonye bandika igitekerezo, uko bakijyaho impaka, uko berekana ibimenyetso byavuye mu byagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi, uko bafata umwanzuro ku nsanganyamatsiko runaka nթbindi. Ibi bishobora kukwigisha kudata umwanya ahubwo bikuzamura ku rwego rwաbashakashatsi bթnararibonye cyanecyane iyo wimenyereje kwifashisha inyandiko zabo.Nkյko ubushakashatsi buba bwatangiye bwerekana ko hari icyuho buje kuziba, cyangwa se ko buje gusobanura ikibazo runaka ku buryo bwimbitse, bugomba kurangira bugaragaza uko icyo cyuho cyazibwe cyangwa uko ikibazo runaka cyasobanuwe ku buryo bwisumbuye ubwari busanzwe buzwi. UmusozoKumenya kwandika ibyagaragajwe nյbushakashatsi ni ingenzi. Ubushakashatsi bushobora gukorwa neza, ariko iyo bwanditse nabi buba imfabusa. Ubushakashatsi bwiza ni ubugaragaza ibimenyetso kandi bushingiye ku makuru nyayo yavuye mu batangamakuru. Umushakashatsi na we agomba kumenya guhitamo ayթngenzi, akayasesengura, akayandika mu magambo yumvikana. Amakuru yandikwa agomba kuba afitanye isano nթbibazo byյbushakashatsi. Mu gukora isobanura bwite, umushakashatsi asubiza ibyo bibazo, ku buryo buciye mu mucyo kandi yifashishije ibimenyetso byavuye mu byagaragajwe nյbwo bushakashatsi. Aho ni ho ahera yerekana umusanzu wթcyo ubushakashatsi bwagezeho gishingiye ku gutara no gusesengura amakuru (empirical contribution), umusanzu wյbushakashatsi mu ihange ugereranyije nյbumenyi busanzwe buzwi ku nsanganyamatsiko yizweho (theoretical contribution), nյmusanzu wյbushakashatsi mu bikorwa bifatika (practical contribution). Ibyo byose bikorwa bishingiye ku myanzuro yյbushakashatsi. IndangasokoBahati, B., Tedre, M., Fors, U., & Mukama, E. (2016).
